### [1] [SPOQ: Specialist Orchestrated Queuing for Multi-Agent Software Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03115v1)
*Royce Carbowitz,Dheeraj Kumar*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SPOQ通过波形调度、双重验证和人类作为智能体集成，显著提升了多智能体软件工程自动化任务的质量、效率和可监督性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法存在协调开销、质量控制差距和有限的人类监督，需要一种更高效、更可靠的多智能体系统架构。

Method: SPOQ结合了基于波形的拓扑调度、双重验证门和人类作为智能体集成，并采用三层智能体层次结构优化成本质量。

Result: 实验显示，波形调度接近关键路径下界（加速达14.3倍），规划覆盖率提升至99.75，缺陷减少至0.20/任务，测试通过率提升至99.75%，人工审查进一步将残余缺陷降至0.03/任务。

Conclusion: SPOQ的编排方法能有效提升多智能体系统的性能，且收益独立于特定模型。

中文摘要：多智能体人工智能系统在自动化软件工程任务方面显示出前景，但现有方法存在协调开销、质量控制差距和有限的人类监督。我们引入SPOQ（专家编排队列），一种结合三项创新的方法：（1）基于波形的拓扑调度，从任务依赖图计算并行执行波次；（2）双重验证门，在执行前（规划验证）和执行后（代码验证）应用质量指标，以减少返工周期；（3）人类作为智能体（HaaA）集成，其中人类专家参与分解并在执行期间可以被咨询。SPOQ使用三层智能体层次结构（Opus工作者、Sonnet评审者、Haiku调查者）来优化成本-质量权衡。我们通过四个实验评估SPOQ。实验1：波形调度接近关键路径下界（比率1.03-1.11，加速高达14.3倍）；在2槽本地后端上，它提供稳定的1.4倍加速。实验2：SPOQ将规划覆盖率从93.0提高到99.75，消除了循环规划，并将并行度从31.0提升到75.25。实验3：双重验证将每个任务的缺陷从0.34减少到0.20，并将测试通过率从91.25%提升到99.75%。实验4：人工审查将每个任务的残余缺陷从0.47减少到0.03。结果在本地托管的开源权重模型（Qwen3.6-35B-A3B）上复现，验证了收益归因于编排而非特定模型。一项横跨17个仓库、8589次提交、1822个任务和13866个测试（通过率99.87%）的纵向研究提供了生态有效性验证。

Original abstract: Multi-agent AI systems show promise for automating software engineering tasks, yet existing approaches suffer from coordination overhead, quality control gaps, and limited human oversight. We introduce SPOQ (Specialist Orchestrated Queuing), a methodology combining three innovations: (1) wave-based topological dispatch that computes parallel execution waves from task dependency graphs; (2) dual validation gates applying quality metrics before execution (planning validation) and after (code validation) to reduce rework cycles; and (3) Human-as-an-Agent (HaaA) integration, where a human specialist participates in decomposition and can be consulted during execution. SPOQ uses a three-tier agent hierarchy (Opus workers, Sonnet reviewers, Haiku investigators) to optimize cost-quality tradeoffs. We evaluate SPOQ through four experiments. Experiment 1: wave dispatch approaches the critical-path lower bound (ratio 1.03--1.11, speedup up to 14.3x); on a 2-slot local backend it delivers a stable 1.4x speedup. Experiment 2: SPOQ improves planning coverage from 93.0 to 99.75, eliminates cyclic plans, and lifts parallelism from 31.0 to 75.25. Experiment 3: dual validation reduces defects from 0.34 to 0.20 per task and lifts test pass rate from 91.25% to 99.75%. Experiment 4: human review reduces residual defects from 0.47 to 0.03 per task. Results are replicated on a locally hosted open-weights model (Qwen3.6-35B-A3B), verifying gains are attributable to orchestration rather than any specific model. A longitudinal study across 17 repositories, 8,589 commits, 1,822 tasks, and 13,866 tests (99.87% pass rate) provides ecological validation.

</details>


### [2] [Analyzing the Evolution of Structural Communities within Microservice Architecture](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04047v1)
*Alexander Bakhtin,Matteo Esposito,Valentina Lenarduzzi,Davide Taibi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 使用时间社区检测方法分析微服务架构退化，在train-ticket基准的六个版本中发现稳定的两个社区对应业务流程，并识别出跨社区和双向连接的服务，成员强度度量支持细粒度评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检测微服务架构退化，特别是通过社区发现分析与服务网络结构相关的反模式（如错误切割和结服务），以识别职责划分或通信问题。

Method: 对train-ticket基准的六个连续版本进行时间社区检测，分析社区组成、成员活动以及成员强度度量。

Result: 观察到稳定的两个社区对应两个业务流程；发现服务属于多个社区以及同一社区内既有传入又有传出连接；成员强度度量提供了细粒度社区评估。

Conclusion: 时间社区检测能有效揭示微服务架构中的结构稳定性和潜在退化问题，成员强度度量有助于深入分析服务归属关系。

中文摘要：近年来，微服务架构中反模式的检测逐渐受到关注，特别是用于识别微服务架构退化实例。在此类任务中，微服务架构通常被建模为微服务依赖网络。最近的研究探索了如何通过考虑项目连续版本的结构来评估此类架构网络的演化。与服务网络结构相关的特定反模式包括错误切割和结服务。社区检测是一种识别网络中相互高度依赖的服务组的方法。如果这些组无法映射到系统中的业务流程，或者同一服务属于多个社区，则可能表明由于职责划分不当或通信未优化而导致的架构退化。时间社区检测方法已被提出用于分析随时间演化的社区结构。我们在train-ticket基准测试的六个版本的微服务架构中执行了时间社区检测，并分析了所发现社区的组成及其随时间的变化。我们观察到一个稳定的架构，服务清晰分为两个社区，我们将其识别为系统执行的两个业务流程。我们发现属于多个社区的服务，以及同一社区内既有传入连接又有传出连接的服务。所利用算法提供的成员强度度量能够对微服务社区进行细粒度评估。

Original abstract: In recent years, the detection of anti-patterns in microservice architecture has gained traction, particularly to identify instances of Microservice Architectural Degradation. In such tasks, the microservice architecture is often modeled as a network of microservice dependencies. Recent works have explored how to assess the evolution of such architectural networks by considering the architecture of consecutive releases of the project. Particular anti-patterns related to the structure of the service network include Wrong cuts and Knot services.
  Community detection is a way to identify groups of services in a network that strongly depend on each other. If such groups cannot be mapped to business processes in the system, or if the same service belongs to multiple communities, this could indicate architectural degradation due to an inappropriate division of responsibilities or unoptimized communication. Temporal community detection methods have been proposed to analyze community structure that evolves in time.
  We performed temporal community detection within the microservice architecture of six releases of the train-ticket benchmark and analyzed the composition of the discovered communities and their activities over time. We observed a stable architecture with a clear separation of services into two communities, which we could identify with two business processes performed by the system. We found services belonging to several communities, as well as services within the same community with both incoming and outgoing connections. The membership strength metric provided by the leveraged algorithm enables fine-grained assessment of the microservice communities.

</details>


### [3] [AlgoTouch: An Execution-Centered Approach to Incremental Construction of Imperative Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03349v1)
*Michel Adam,Patrice Frison,Sabine Letellier Zarshenas,Moncef Daoud*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AlgoTouch是一个基于执行、通过直接操作程序数据增量构建命令式程序的系统，能够从执行行为中确定性合成控制结构并自动生成多种命令式语言的代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统命令式编程需要开发者预测指令对数据状态的影响，增加了认知负荷和出错概率，尤其在早期和增量开发中。

Method: 通过执行具体的数据转换并记录到中间表示，利用显式概念机器暴露数据存储、计算和控制流，从执行行为中合成条件语句和循环宏，支持部分程序执行和增量完善。

Result: 在代表性算法基准上验证了正确性、表达能力、鲁棒性和语言独立性，自动生成Python、C、C++、Java的正确可读代码。

Conclusion: 该工作引入了一种新的以执行为中心的交互式程序构建模型，贡献了一类执行中心开发系统。

中文摘要：命令式语言的程序构建仍然主要基于编写文本代码，这些代码指定了对程序数据进行操作的指令序列。这种方法要求开发者预测指令对不断变化的数据状态的影响，这在早期和增量开发过程中增加了认知负荷和出错的可能性。本文提出了AlgoTouch，一个基于执行的系统，通过直接操作程序数据来增量构建命令式程序。它不是组装语法结构，而是通过执行具体的数据转换来构建程序，这些转换被记录并整合到内部中间表示中。AlgoTouch依赖于一个显式的概念机器，它暴露了数据存储、计算和控制流，使得观察到的执行与程序结构之间能够持续对齐。该系统的一个核心贡献在于从执行行为中确定性合成控制结构。条件语句从观察到的比较中派生，而迭代行为则封装在支持非线性增量构建的循环宏中。这种设计使得部分和不完整的程序可以被执行、完善和完成，同时保持语义一致性。AlgoTouch自动生成多种主流命令式语言（包括Python、C、C++和Java）的正确且可读的程序。该系统通过在一组代表性算法基准上进行工程级验证来评估，展示了正确性、表达能力、鲁棒性和语言独立性。通过将执行、构建和代码生成集成在一个统一的架构中，这项工作引入了一种用于交互式程序构建的替代模型，并贡献了一类新的以执行为中心的开发系统。

Original abstract: Program construction in imperative languages remains largely based on writing textual code that specifies sequences of instructions operating on program data. This approach requires developers to anticipate the effects of instructions on evolving data states, which increases cognitive load and the likelihood of errors during early and incremental development. This paper presents AlgoTouch, an execution-based system for incremental construction of imperative programs through direct manipulation of program data. Rather than assembling syntactic structures, programs are constructed by executing concrete data transformations that are recorded and incorporated into an internal intermediate representation. AlgoTouch relies on an explicit notional machine that exposes data storage, computation, and control flow, enabling continuous alignment between observed execution and program structure. A central contribution of the system lies in its deterministic synthesis of control structures from execution behavior. Conditional statements are derived from observed comparisons, while iterative behaviors are encapsulated in loop macros that support non-linear and incremental construction. This design enables partial and incomplete programs to be executed, refined, and completed while preserving semantic consistency. AlgoTouch automatically generates correct and readable programs in several mainstream imperative languages, including Python, C, C++, and Java. The system is evaluated through engineering-level validation on a representative set of algorithmic benchmarks, demonstrating correctness, expressiveness, robustness, and language independence. By integrating execution, construction, and code generation within a unified architecture, this work introduces an alternative model for interactive program construction and contributes a new class of execution-centered development systems.

</details>


### [4] [Neural Change Prediction: Relating Software Changes to Their Effects and Vice Versa](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03378v1)
*Laura Plein,Souhila Zidane,Jordan Samhi,Andreas Zeller*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出神经变更预测技术，通过学习代码变更与行为变更的关联，实现行为驱动的代码定位和变更影响预测，无需执行代码或先验知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件工程中理解变更与效果的关系很重要，但预测代码语义（不执行）是挑战；现有AI在软件工程中进展显著但仍难以胜任。

Method: 自动对程序应用大量变异，观察输出变化，从（变更，行为变化）对中训练模型，用于特征定位和影响预测；案例研究使用CSS和Python程序验证。

Result: 通过CSS和Python案例展示技术通用性；模型能准确预测变更位置和影响。

Conclusion: 神经变更预测是自动化的、无需先验知识的技术，适用于任何可执行且输出可观察的软件工件，在软件演化和修复中有广泛应用潜力。

中文摘要：软件开发在很大程度上围绕着理解软件变更及其影响之间的关系。如果我们能够学习并预测这些关系，那么这样的预测将有益于软件工程的多个领域。尽管人工智能的最新进展在软件工程任务中显示出巨大潜力，但在不执行代码的情况下预测代码的语义仍然是一个巨大的挑战。在本文中，我们提出了神经变更预测（Neural Change Prediction），这是一种新颖且基础的技术，用于学习和预测软件变更与其对程序行为的动态影响之间的关联。具体来说，对于给定的程序和测试输入，我们自动对代码应用大量变异，并观察这些变更如何改变程序的输出。从这些（代码变更，行为变更）对中，我们创建模型：（1）对于期望的行为变更，预测应该在哪里以及如何修改代码（特征定位、软件演化和软件修复）；（2）对于给定的代码变更，预测该代码变更如何影响输出（影响预测）。我们通过一个详细的CSS配置文件案例研究和一个Python程序评估来展示神经变更预测的通用性和广泛适用性。虽然神经变更预测需要大量变异（因此需要多次执行被测程序），但它是完全自动化的，不需要任何关于代码或其语义的先验知识，这使得它适用于任何可执行且输出可观察的软件工件。

Original abstract: Much of software development revolves around understanding the relationship between software changes and their effects. If we could learn and predict those relationships, such predictions could benefit several areas of software engineering. While recent advances in artificial intelligence have shown great promise in software engineering tasks, predicting the semantics of code without executing it remains a big challenge. In this paper, we present Neural Change Prediction, a novel and fundamental technique to learn and predict associations between software changes and their dynamic effects on program behavior. Specifically, for a given program and test inputs, we automatically apply numerous mutations to the code and observe how these changes alter the program's output. From these (changes to software, changes in behavior)-pairs, we create models that: (1) for a desired change in behavior, predict where and how the code should be changed (feature localization, software evolution, and software repair); and (2) for a given code change, predict how this code change affects the output (effect prediction). We have conducted a detailed case study on CSS configuration files and an evaluation on Python programs to demonstrate the generality and wide applicability of Neural Change Prediction. While Neural Change Prediction requires numerous mutations (and thus numerous executions of the program under test), Neural Change Prediction is fully automatic and does not require any prior knowledge of the code or its semantics, making it applicable to any software artifact that can be executed and whose output can be observed.

</details>


### [5] [Human-AI Collaboration and the Transformation of Software Engineering Work](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03394v1)
*Mamdouh Alenezi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 随着生成式人工智能和自主智能体人工智能融入软件开发，工程师的核心价值从编写代码转向意图规范、批判性判断和负责监督，本文提出了一个面向未来工程师的能力框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式人工智能和自主智能体人工智能正在重新配置软件工程，从以人类编写代码为中心转向指导、验证和治理自主系统，这需要重新思考工程师所需的能力。

Method: 采用结构化解释性综合方法，基于精心策划的多源证据基础，包括对自主编码智能体在开源仓库中贡献的大规模实证观察。

Result: 提出了一个原创的、理论驱动的能力框架，包含五个相互作用的类别（技术、认知、社会技术、治理和组织），并通过能力矩阵和转型框架进行操作化，推导出九个可实证检验的命题。

Conclusion: 随着代码变得丰富，软件工程师的持久价值体现在意图规范、批判性判断和负责任的监督上，而非代码生产数量。

中文摘要：生成式人工智能（GenAI）和自主智能体人工智能（Agentic AI）融入软件开发，正在将软件工程从一项以人类编写代码为中心的活动，重新配置为一门以指导、验证和治理自主及半自主系统为中心的学科。本文基于精心策划的多源证据基础，包括近期同行评审和档案研究——例如对自主编码智能体在开源仓库中贡献数十万个拉取请求的大规模实证观察——综合分析了工程工作的焦点如何从个人编码生产力转向人机协作、智能体编排、验证与确认、治理以及社会技术系统思维。我们采用结构化解释性综合方法，刻画了三种共存的范式：传统软件工程、生成式人工智能赋能软件工程和自主智能体人工智能赋能软件工程。我们映射了哪些传统活动正在被自动化、哪些正在被增强、哪些正在新出现，并追踪了未来十年可能的角色演变轨迹。本文的主要贡献是一个原创的、理论驱动的能力框架，它将未来工程师所需的能力组织成五个相互作用的类别——技术、认知、社会技术、治理和组织——通过一个能力矩阵和一个将范式转变与能力需求联系起来的转型框架进行操作化。我们推导出九个可实证检验的命题，并阐述了对理论、行业劳动力转型、大学课程设置和组织领导力的启示。我们认为，随着代码变得丰富，软件工程师的持久价值越来越多地体现在意图规范、批判性判断和负责任的监督上，而不是所产生代码的数量上。

Original abstract: The integration of Generative AI (GenAI) and Agentic AI into software development is reconfiguring software engineering from an activity centered on human authorship of code into a discipline centered on directing, verifying, and governing autonomous and semi-autonomous systems. Drawing on a curated, multi-source evidence base of recent peer-reviewed and archival studies -- including large-scale empirical observations of autonomous coding agents contributing hundreds of thousands of pull requests to open-source repositories -- this paper synthesizes how the locus of engineering work is shifting from individual coding productivity toward human--AI collaboration, agent orchestration, verification and validation, governance, and socio-technical systems thinking. We adopt a structured interpretive synthesis to characterize three coexisting paradigms: Traditional, Generative AI-Enabled, and Agentic AI-Enabled software engineering. We map which traditional activities are being automated, which are being augmented, and which are newly emerging, and we trace plausible role trajectories over the next decade. The paper's principal contribution is an original, theory-driven competency framework that organizes the capabilities required of future engineers into five interacting categories -- % technical, cognitive, socio-technical, governance, and organizational -- % operationalized through a competency matrix and a transformation framework linking paradigm shifts to capability demands. We derive nine empirically testable propositions and articulate implications for theory, industry workforce transformation, university curricula, and organizational leadership. We argue that, as code becomes abundant, the durable value of the software engineer increasingly resides in intent specification, critical judgment, and accountable oversight rather than in the sheer volume of code produced.

</details>


### [6] [Multi-Modal Assessment of Road Roughness Using Smartphone Applications, Acceleration, and Passenger Ratings](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03427v1)
*Novel Certada,Amirhesam Aghanouri,Joseba Gorospe,Cristina Olaverri-Monreal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种低成本、多模态的基于智能手机和乘客感知的路面粗糙度评估方法，通过1700公里实地测试发现两个手机App虽有强相关性但存在系统偏差，IRI与PSR负相关、与加速度正相关，验证了感知与物理关联，但消费级传感集成面临挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统路面粗糙度评估依赖高成本专业设备，本文旨在探索利用智能手机与乘客感知作为低成本替代方案。

Method: 收集三个互补数据源（两个智能手机IRI、GNSS-IMU加速度、乘客PSR）在1700公里道路上实测，使用相关性分析、ICC和Bland-Altman评估一致性。

Result: 两个手机App强相关但存在系统偏差；IRI与PSR显著负相关；IRI与垂直加速度正相关。

Conclusion: 消费级传感与感知评估集成可作低成本方案，但存在互换性挑战，需进一步改进一致性。

中文摘要：本文研究了一种用于低成本路面粗糙度评估的多模态和以人为中心的框架。评估基于三个互补的数据源：基于智能手机的国际粗糙度指数（IRI）估计值（来自两个独立的智能手机应用程序）、车载GNSS-IMU接收器（全球导航卫星系统接收器与惯性测量单元）测量值，以及乘客的现时服务能力评级（PSR）。数据是在奥地利、匈牙利和罗马尼亚的实际交通条件下，在1700多公里的路程上收集的。使用相关性分析、组内相关系数（ICC）和Bland-Altman方法评估了应用程序间的一致性。虽然两个智能手机应用程序显示出强相关性，但系统偏差限制了它们的可互换性。IRI与PSR之间显著的负相关证实了对粗糙度的感知敏感性，而IRI与垂直加速度之间的正相关验证了路面不平整与车辆动力学之间的物理联系。结果证明了将消费级传感与基于感知的评估集成用于路面粗糙度监测作为高成本专用调查设备替代方案的挑战。

Original abstract: This paper investigates a multi-modal and human-centric framework for low-cost road roughness assessment. The evaluation was based on three complementary data sources: smartphone-based International Roughness Index (IRI) estimates from two independent smartphone-based applications; in-vehicle GNSS-IMU Receiver (Global Navigation Satellite System Receiver with Inertial Measurement Unit) measurements, and passenger Present Serviceability Ratings (PSR). Data were collected over 1700 km across Austria, Hungary, and Romania under real traffic conditions. Inter-application agreement was evaluated using correlation analysis, Intraclass Correlation Coefficient (ICC), and Bland-Altman methods. While the two smartphone applications show strong correlation, systematic bias limits their interchangeability. A significant inverse relationship between IRI and PSR confirms perceptual sensitivity to roughness, and positive correlations between IRI and vertical acceleration validate the physical linkage between pavement irregularities and vehicle dynamics. The results demonstrate the challenges of integrating consumer-grade sensing and perception-based evaluation for road roughness monitoring as an alternative to high-cost specialized survey equipment.

</details>


### [7] [Token Budgets: An Empirical Catalog of 63 LLM-Agent Budget-Overrun Incidents, with an Affine-Typed Rust Mitigation as a Case Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04056v1)
*Sajjad Khan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过63个生产事件目录和基于仿射类型系统的token-budgets库，解决了LLM代理预算超支问题，证明编译时防止多代理委托错误的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理预算超支是已知的生产故障，但现有系统缺乏类型系统层面的保护，导致昂贵的运行时错误。

Method: 构建了包含63个生产事件的故障分类法，并开发了基于Rust仿射所有权的token-budgets库，将预算操作错误转化为编译错误。

Result: 在多个运行时和API测试中，token-budgets实现了零上限违规和零误拒绝，多代理委托竞争在编译时被阻止，静态过度预留4-6倍（自适应2.11倍）。

Conclusion: 仿射类型系统能有效防止预算超支，但二进制级别上限健全性仍为开放问题。

中文摘要：LLM代理预算超支是一个有记录的生产故障类别：单次重试循环可能在操作员注意到之前花费数千美元，而可以防止这种情况的进程内完整性属性（无别名、无双重花费、无使用后委托的成本承载价值）即使有，也是通过临时包装器而非类型系统来强制执行的。我们的核心贡献是实证性的：一个包含来自21个编排框架（2023-2026年）的63个已确认生产事件的目录，每个事件都有引用的GitHub问题，并且如果报告了美元损失，则包含损失金额，组织成一个八类故障分类法（评估者间Cohen's kappa = 0.837，N = 113），外加47个补充结构条目。作为针对此分类法评估的一种缓解措施，我们构建了token-budgets，一个1180行的Rust crate（无unsafe），它实现了仿射所有权，使得克隆、双重花费或在委托后使用预算成为编译错误，而不是操作员必须记住避免的运行时危险。美元上限是在估计器假设下的运行时算术；仿射层使该算术不可绕过。在单代理工作负载上，一个4行的Python计数器与这个crate匹配，0/30超调，因此区别价值在于多代理委托中操作员错误下的不可绕过性：在11个事件中记录的委托扇出竞争在编译时被借用检查器拒绝，而相同的模式在asyncio下超调30/30，三个有纪律的替代方案超调0/30。跨五个运行时、三个提供商和一个温度分层的实时API测试（N = 160），该方法报告了零上限违规和零误拒绝，与并发工作操作性能相当。静态过度预留为4-6倍（自适应为2.11倍）。运行中二进制文件上的二进制级别上限健全性留作开放问题。

Original abstract: LLM-agent budget overruns are a documented production failure class: a single retry loop can spend thousands of dollars before an operator notices, and the in-process integrity properties that would prevent it (no aliasing, no double-spend, no use-after-delegation of a cost-bearing value) are enforced, if at all, by ad-hoc wrappers rather than by the type system. Our central contribution is empirical: a catalog of 63 confirmed production incidents from 21 orchestration frameworks (2023-2026), each backed by a quoted GitHub issue and, where reported, a dollar loss, organized into an eight-cluster failure taxonomy (inter-rater Cohen's kappa = 0.837, N = 113), plus 47 supplementary structural entries. As one mitigation evaluated against this taxonomy, we build token-budgets, an 1,180-line Rust crate (no unsafe) that operationalizes affine ownership so that cloning, double-spending, or using a budget after delegating it are compile errors rather than runtime hazards an operator must remember to avoid. The dollar cap is runtime arithmetic under an estimator assumption; the affine layer makes that arithmetic non-bypassable. On single-agent workloads a 4-line Python counter matches the crate at 0/30 overshoot, so the distinguishing value is non-bypassability under operator error in multi-agent delegation: the delegation-fanout race documented in 11 incidents is rejected by the borrow checker at compile time, while the same pattern under asyncio overshoots 30/30 and three disciplined alternatives overshoot 0/30. Across five runtimes, three providers, and a temperature-stratified live-API test (N = 160), the approach reports zero cap violations and zero false refusals, at operational parity with concurrent work. Static over-reservation is 4-6x (2.11x adaptive). Binary-level cap-soundness on the running binary is left open.

</details>


### [8] [The Invisible Lottery: How Subtle Cues Steer Algorithm Choice in LLM Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04057v1)
*Akanksha Narula,Mofasshara Binte Rafique,Laurent Bindschaedler*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型生成代码时，偶然提示线索会显著改变算法选择，导致性能、安全性和可维护性上的不可控变化，直接命名算法可有效缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究提示中的偶然线索如何无意中影响LLM的算法选择，即使输出正确性相同，从而揭示潜在的不可控风险。

Method: 在11个任务、19种线索类型和15种模型配置上进行46,535次受控实验，测量算法族分布的变化。

Result: 发现线索引起算法族分布高达100个百分点的系统性偏移，且与线索语义一致；直接命名算法是最有效的缓解措施。

Conclusion: 偶然上下文导致LLM输出在性能、安全性和可维护性上产生不可预测的差异，即“隐形彩票”，需通过明确指定算法来规避风险。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）现在生成大量生产代码，通常用于具有多种有效算法解决方案的任务。偶然的提示线索，即任务规范之外的上下文单词或元数据，可以引导模型选择哪个算法，即使所有输出都通过相同的测试。提示敏感性作为提高输出质量的工具已被广泛研究。在这里，输出策略是指在固定正确性下的算法选择。我们将算法引导定义为由线索引起的算法族分布变化，并在11个任务、19种线索类型（18个通道加上一个记忆化语义与表面消融，在改变排版和标点的同时保留含义）和15种模型配置上进行了46,535次受控实验。我们发现算法族分布发生了大的系统性偏移（高达100个百分点），很大程度上与线索语义一致，包括在限速等应用任务中。直接命名算法是我们测试的最可靠的缓解措施。因此，意外上下文造成了性能、安全性和可维护性的“隐形彩票”。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) now generate substantial production code, often for tasks with multiple valid algorithmic solutions. Incidental prompt cues, meaning contextual words or metadata outside the task specification, can steer which algorithm the model selects, even when all outputs pass the same tests. Prompt sensitivity is well studied as a tool to improve output quality. Here, output policy means algorithm choice under fixed correctness. We define algorithm steering as cue-induced shifts in algorithm-family distributions and run 46,535 controlled experiments across 11 tasks, 19 cue types (18 channels plus a memoization semantic-vs-surface ablation that preserves meaning while changing typography and punctuation), and 15 model configurations. We find large, systematic shifts in algorithm-family distributions (up to 100 pp), largely consistent with cue semantics, including in applied tasks such as rate limiting. Direct algorithm naming is the most reliable mitigation we tested. Accidental context therefore creates an "invisible lottery" over performance, security, and maintainability.

</details>


### [9] [Making Embodied AI Reliable: A Community Agenda from Testing to Formal Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03593v1)
*Xi Zheng,Dulanga Weerakoon,Yintong Huo,Teresa Yeo,Guy Van Den Broeck,Vijay Ganesh,Daniel Neider,Biplav Srivastava,Ivan Ruchkin,Archan Misra,Corina Pasareanu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出通过集成测试、验证和运行时自适应的生命周期保证工作流来实现具身AI的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身AI在开放世界中的可靠性是一个生命周期保证问题，现有方法（测试、验证、运行时自适应）独立处理不足以应对不确定性、人机交互和涌现行为。

Method: 提出三个互补方向：基于场景的测试、组合验证、运行时保证，并通过共享神经符号表示和持续反馈进行集成。

Result: 给出了集成保证工作流的概念框架，但没有具体实验结果。

Conclusion: 集成测试、验证和运行时自适应的工作流可以为复杂真实环境中的可信具身AI系统提供基础。

中文摘要：具身人工智能系统越来越多地部署在开放世界环境中，但确保其可靠性仍然是一个基本挑战。借鉴AAAI'26桥接计划“通过测试和形式验证使具身AI可靠”的讨论，本文认为，具身AI的可靠性本质上是一个生命周期保证问题，源于不确定性、人机交互以及紧密耦合系统组件之间的涌现行为。我们确定了实现可靠具身AI的三个互补方向：（1）由经过验证的规范和有意义覆盖指标支持的可靠基于场景的测试，（2）通过系统行为和环境的符号化结构化表示实现的组合验证，以及（3）能够在部署期间适应不确定性和分布变化的运行时保证机制。我们主张不将这些方法独立对待，而是通过共享的神经符号表示和系统生命周期中的持续反馈，将测试、验证和运行时自适应连接起来的集成保证工作流。这种集成为构建能够在复杂真实世界中安全可靠运行的值得信赖的具身AI系统提供了基础。

Original abstract: Embodied AI systems are increasingly deployed in open-world environments, yet ensuring their reliability remains a fundamental challenge. Drawing on discussions from the AAAI'26 Bridge Program on "Making Embodied AI Reliable with Testing and Formal Verification", this article argues that reliability in embodied AI is inherently a lifecycle assurance problem arising from uncertainty, human interaction, and emergent behaviors across tightly coupled system components. We identify three complementary directions toward reliable embodied AI: (1) trustworthy scenario-based testing supported by validated specifications and meaningful coverage metrics, (2) compositional verification enabled by structured symbolic representations of system behavior and environmental context, and (3) runtime assurance mechanisms capable of adapting to uncertainty and distribution shifts during deployment. Rather than treating these approaches independently, we advocate integrated assurance workflows that connect testing, verification, and runtime adaptation through shared neuro-symbolic representations and continuous feedback across the system lifecycle. Such integration provides a foundation for building trustworthy embodied AI systems that can operate safely and reliably in complex real-world environments.

### [10] [DDOR: Delta Debugging for Explainable Overrefusal Testing and Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03601v1)
*Qinyan Zhou,Peixin Zhang,Jun Sun,Haonan Zhang,Dongxia Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: DDOR是一个自动化框架，通过delta调试定位导致过度拒绝的短语片段并生成测试套件，同时利用这些片段进行提示修复，在保持安全性的同时减少过度拒绝。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全对齐和护栏可能导致LLM对良性查询过度拒绝，影响可用性，而现有方法缺乏自动化和可解释性。

Method: 提出DDOR框架，使用delta调试定位最小触发拒绝片段（mRTF），基于mRTF生成多样化提示并通过多预言验证过滤，构建测试套件，并利用mRTF进行针对性提示修复。

Result: DDOR能自动生成约1000个模型特定的测试案例，并显著减少过度拒绝，同时保持对有害输入的防御和原始意图。

Conclusion: DDOR提供了评估和缓解过度拒绝的端到端解决方案，在提高LLM可用性的同时不牺牲安全性。

中文摘要：虽然安全对齐和护栏有助于大型语言模型（LLM）避免有害输出，但它们也可能导致过度拒绝，即对看似有风险但实际上良性的查询进行不必要的拒绝。我们提出了DDOR（用于过度拒绝的Delta调试），这是一个完全自动化且可解释的框架，用于在黑盒设置下进行过度拒绝测试和修复，其中只能访问模型输入和输出，内部安全机制保持不透明。DDOR应用delta调试来定位最小的触发拒绝片段（mRTF），这些片段提供了短语级别的、可解释的证据，说明拒绝发生的原因。基于这些mRTF，DDOR生成多样化的、上下文丰富的提示，并执行多预言验证以过滤内在不安全或模棱两可的情况，从而产生可扩展且模型特定的过度拒绝测试套件（每个模型约1000个案例）。除了评估之外，我们进一步利用定位的mRTF进行有针对性的提示修复，显著减少过度拒绝，同时保留原始意图并在真正有害的输入上保持安全性。总体而言，DDOR提供了一个实用的端到端解决方案来评估和缓解过度拒绝，在不牺牲安全性的前提下提高LLM的可用性。

Original abstract: While safety alignment and guardrails help large language models (LLMs) avoid harmful outputs, they can also induce overrefusal, i.e., unwarranted rejection of benign queries that merely appear risky. We present DDOR (Delta Debugging for OverRefusal), a fully automated and explainable framework for overrefusal testing and repair in a black-box setting, where only model inputs and outputs are accessible and internal safety mechanisms remain opaque. DDOR applies delta debugging to localize minimal refusal-triggering fragments (mRTFs) that provide phrase-level, explainable evidence for why a refusal occurs. Conditioned on these mRTFs, DDOR generates diverse, context-rich prompts and performs multi-oracle validation to filter intrinsically unsafe or ambiguous cases, producing scalable and model-specific overrefusal test suites (approximately 1K cases per model). Beyond evaluation, we further leverage localized mRTFs to perform targeted prompt repair, substantially reducing overrefusal while preserving the original intent and maintaining safety on genuinely harmful inputs. Overall, DDOR offers a practical end-to-end solution to both evaluate and mitigate overrefusal, improving LLM usability without sacrificing safety.

</details>


### [11] [Agentic Generation and Evolution of Knowledge Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03662v2)
*Man Zhang,Tao Yue,Nazareno M. Aguirre,Diego Garbervetsky,Sebastian Uchitel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TrustModel愿景，通过建模、一致性、演化三个自主子系统实现活知识模型的自主生成与演化，以支持持续演化软件系统的可靠工程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂软件系统与动态环境交互，知识模型可能过时或不一致，需要持续演化的知识模型来支持系统的可靠工程。

Method: TrustModel包含三个子系统：建模子系统构建和更新知识模型；一致性子系统评估模型与系统及环境的一致性；演化子系统生成指导，使模型与变化同步。

Result: 演示了TrustModel在基于模型的测试中的实例化，并讨论了其对需求监控、架构漂移跟踪、变更影响评估等MDE活动的支持潜力。

Conclusion: TrustModel将活知识模型定位为持续演化软件系统可靠工程的基础。

中文摘要：复杂软件系统，如自动驾驶汽车、机器人等，日益与动态的物理、网络和社会环境交互。推理它们的行为、在持续变化中维护它们、以及安全地演化它们，需要关于系统、其假设和运行环境的可信知识。知识模型为这种推理提供了实用基础，但它们在系统演化过程中可能变得不完整、不一致或过时。本文提出TrustModel，一种用于自主生成和演化活知识模型的愿景。TrustModel包含三个自主子系统：建模（用于构建和更新知识模型）、一致性（用于评估它们与系统及其环境的一致性）、以及演化（用于生成指导以保持知识模型与新兴变化同步）。我们演示了如何将TrustModel实例化用于基于模型的测试，并讨论了它支持其他MDE活动（如需求和假设监控、架构漂移跟踪、变更影响评估）的潜力。总体而言，TrustModel将活知识模型定位为持续演化软件系统可靠工程的基础。

Original abstract: Complex software systems such as autonomous vehicles, robotics increasingly interact with dynamic physical, cyber, and social environments. Reasoning about their behavior, maintaining them under continuous change, and evolving them safely require trustworthy knowledge about the system, its assumptions, and its operating context. Knowledge models (KMs) provide a practical basis for such reasoning, but they may themselves become incomplete, inconsistent, or outdated as systems evolve. This paper presents TrustModel, a vision for the agentic generation and evolution of living KMs. TrustModel comprises three agentic subsystems: Modeling, for constructing and updating KMs; Conformance, for assessing their alignment with the system and its environment; and Evolution, for generating guidance to keep KMs synchronized with emerging changes. We demonstrate how TrustModel can be instantiated for model-based testing and discuss its potential for supporting other MDE activities, such as requirements and assumption monitoring, architectural drift tracking, and change impact assessment. Overall, TrustModel positions living KMs as a foundation for dependable engineering of continuously evolving software systems.

### [12] [An AutomationML Domain Library for the Formalized Process Description](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03691v2)
*Hamied Nabizada,Rainer Drath,Felix Gehlhoff,Alexander Fay*

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于AutomationML的FPD领域库，解决了FPD缺乏标准化机器可读数据格式的问题，并通过双向映射工具验证了其适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FPD缺乏标准化、工具无关的数据格式，无法进行机器可读的模型交换。

Result: 通过双向映射工具成功在基于Web的FPD建模器和AML之间实现转换，证明了库的可用性。

Conclusion: 该AML领域库为FPD提供了标准化的机器可读数据交换格式，支持工具无关的模型互操作性。

中文摘要：根据VDI/VDE 3682的形式化过程描述（FPD）提供了一种跨工程领域描述过程的标准化图形符号，但缺乏用于机器可读模型交换的标准化、工具无关的数据格式。本文提出了一种自动化标记语言（AML）领域库，该库基于计算机辅助工程交换（CAEX）3.0元模型，将FPD语言元素的完整集合（包括其属性、连接语义和图形表示信息）形式化为类库。该库包含五个相互关联的部分：定义语义角色的RoleClassLib、用于连接类型的InterfaceClassLib、用于信息模型和图表交换的两个AttributeTypeLib，以及提供实例化模板的SystemUnitClassLib。讨论了关于继承、图表结构、层次分解和图形信息表示的关键设计决策以及所考虑的替代方案。一个双向映射工具通过将基于Web的FPD建模器与AML之间的转换，展示了该库的适用性。

Original abstract: The Formalized Process Description (FPD) according to VDI/VDE 3682 provides a standardized graphical notation for describing processes across engineering domains but lacks a standardized, tool-independent data format for machine-readable model exchange. This paper presents an AutomationML (AML) domain library that formalizes the complete set of FPD language elements, their attributes, connection semantics, and graphical representation information as class libraries based on the Computer Aided Engineering Exchange (CAEX) 3.0 metamodel. The library comprises five interrelated parts: a RoleClassLib defining the semantic roles, an InterfaceClassLib for connection types, two AttributeTypeLibs for the information model and diagram interchange, and a SystemUnitClassLib providing instantiation templates. Key design decisions regarding inheritance, diagram structure, hierarchical decomposition, and the representation of graphical information are discussed along with the alternatives that were considered. A bidirectional mapping tool demonstrates the library's applicability by converting between a web-based FPD modeler and AML.

</details>


### [13] [FLARE: Fine-Grained Diagnostic Feedback for LLM Code Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03852v1)
*Yinsheng Yao,Hongxiang Zhang,Weixi Tong,Tianyi Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Flare框架，利用轻量级诊断模型进行行级可疑性预测，结合候选搜索提升代码错误定位与修复效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反馈信号（如测试失败、自我批评）粒度粗或层次高，无法精确指导错误位置，需要更细粒度的定位方法。

Method: Flare通过轻量级诊断模型预测每行代码的可疑性分数，搜索前k个可疑区域，并根据执行结果选择最佳候选进行代码修复。

Result: 在LiveCodeBench和BigCodeBench上，即使不进行候选搜索（k=1），Flare也以1.72%-7.42%绝对改进超越最强基线；搜索10候选平均提升8.50%；诊断模型单独评估优于现有故障定位方法。

Conclusion: 轻量级诊断模型能提供可靠的细粒度错误定位信号，从而有效指导代码优化。

中文摘要：大型语言模型经常生成带有错误的代码。现有方法依赖测试失败和自我批评等反馈信号来迭代改进生成的代码。这些信号要么过于粗糙，要么过于高层，不足以告知模型错误的位置。在这项工作中，我们提出了Flare，一个迭代框架，配备了一个轻量级的诊断模型，用于预测行级别的可疑性信号，以进行错误定位和代码优化。鉴于诊断预测固有的不确定性，Flare搜索前k个可疑区域，并根据执行结果选择最佳候选。在LiveCodeBench和BigCodeBench上使用五个基础LLM的实验表明，即使没有候选搜索（k=1），Flare也以1.72%到7.42%的绝对改进超过了最强基线。此外，与无候选搜索相比，搜索10个候选平均提高了8.50%。在单独评估时，我们的轻量级诊断模型与最近的故障定位方法相比取得了最佳性能，证明了它能够为代码优化提供可靠的细粒度指导。

Original abstract: Large language models often generate code with bugs. Existing methods rely on feedback signals such as test failures and self-critiques to iteratively refine the generated code. Such signals are either too coarse-grained or too high-level, which is not sufficient to inform the model where to fix the bug. In this work, we present Flare, an iterative framework with a lightweight diagnostic model that predicts line-level suspiciousness signals for bug localization and code refinement. Given the inherent uncertainty of diagnostic predictions, Flare searches over the top-k suspicious regions and selects the best candidate according to execution outcomes. Experiments on LiveCodeBench and BigCodeBench with five base LLMs show that, even without candidate search (k=1), Flare outperforms the strongest baseline with an absolute improvement from 1.72% to 7.42%. Furthermore, searching over 10 candidates yields an average improvement of 8.50% compared with no candidate search. When evaluated in isolation, our lightweight diagnostic model achieves the best performance compared with recent fault localization methods, demonstrating that it can provide reliable fine-grained guidance for code refinement.

</details>


### [14] [Automated Repair of Requirements for Cyber-Physical Systems in Simulink Requirements Tables](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03870v1)
*Aren A. Babikian,Alessio Di Sandro,Federico Formica,Claudio Menghi,Marsha Chechik*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个利用系统执行数据修复CPS需求以恢复需求与系统一致性的框架，实验证明有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂软件系统（如CPS）的需求和实现独立演化，导致需求与系统不一致，而传统方法只修复系统，忽略了需求可能错误的问题。

Method: 提出一个框架，基于系统执行数据，使用MATLAB Simulink需求表语言评估声明性需求的正确性，并通过七种变体在六个真实案例（12个需求）上进行评估。

Result: 框架能产生正确且有用的修复需求，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 该框架能有效修复不一致的CPS需求，恢复需求与系统的合规性。

中文摘要：复杂软件系统（例如，网络物理系统（CPS））的开发涉及系统实现及其需求的持续演进。这两个工件通常独立进行，从而产生不一致的风险。例如，系统可能因实现层面的关注点而更新，产生的新版本可能不再满足其原始需求。传统的合规恢复技术（例如，自动程序修复）通过修改系统来解决此问题，同时假设需求是正确的。然而，在实践中，错误、过时或不充分的需求是一个公认的挑战，这激发了需求修复这一补充任务。在本文中，我们提出了一种利用系统执行数据来修复不一致的CPS需求的框架，从而恢复需求与系统之间的合规性。我们的方法评估使用MATLAB Simulink需求表语言表达的基于时间、实值信号的声明性需求的正确性。我们在涵盖12个需求的六个真实案例研究上评估了我们框架的七种变体。结果证实了所提出的框架在生成正确且有用的修复需求方面的有效性。

Original abstract: The development of complex software systems, e.g., cyber-physical systems (CPSs), involves continuous evolution of both system implementations and their requirements. These two artifacts often proceed independently, creating a risk of misalignment. For example, a system may be updated due to implementation-level concerns, yielding a new version that no longer satisfies its original requirements. Traditional compliance recovery techniques, e.g., automated program repair, address this problem by modifying the system while assuming that requirements are correct. However, faulty, outdated or inadequate requirements are a well-documented challenge in practice, motivating the complementary task of requirement repair. In this paper, we propose a framework that leverages system execution data to repair misaligned CPS requirements, thereby restoring requirement-to-system compliance. Our approach evaluates the correctness of declarative requirements over time-based, real-valued signals expressed using the MATLAB Simulink Requirements Tables language. We evaluate seven variants of our framework on six real-world case studies covering 12 requirements. Results confirm the effectiveness of the proposed framework in producing correct and useful repaired requirements.

</details>


### [15] [The Impact of Configuring Agentic AI Coding Tools on Build-vs-Buy Decisions: A Study Protocol](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03907v1)
*Jai Lal Lulla,Matthias Galster,Jie M. Zhang,Sebastian Baltes,Christoph Treude*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个预先注册的实验方案，研究配置机制如何影响自主式AI编码工具（Claude Code和OpenAI Codex）中的“构建与购买”决策，通过受控编程任务测量库选择及披露行为，并发布基准数据集和分析流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主式AI编码工具在编写代码时频繁做出构建与购买决策，直接影响软件安全、合规性、性能和可维护性，但尚无受控实验研究这些决策的支配因素。配置机制是实践者影响这些决策的主要手段，但缺乏对最有效配置机制的研究。

Method: 提出预先注册的实验方案，使用分阶段项目基准中的受控编程任务，任务围绕可识别的构建与购买点构建。操纵配置（无配置、上下文文件、技能、MCP库发现工具、权限控制），测量工具选择的库、披露情况及其准确性。九个预先注册的假设指导实验。

Result: 该研究将生成一个基准数据集和分析流程，作为可复用工件发布，但尚未给出具体实验结果。

Conclusion: 该方案旨在系统评估配置机制对自主式AI编码工具中构建与购买行为的影响，未来通过实验验证假设，并为从业者提供指导。

中文摘要：自主式AI编码工具以越来越高的自主性编写代码，并在此过程中决定是导入库还是从头实现功能。这些决定（即从头构建功能还是购买外部库，以下称为“构建与购买”）会直接影响软件安全性、许可证合规性、性能和长期可维护性。然而，尚无受控实验研究考察在自主式AI编码工具中什么因素支配着构建与购买决策。配置机制（即开发者根据项目或工作流定制自主式AI编码工具行为的手段）是实践者影响这些决策的主要方式之一。但尚不清楚哪些配置机制最有效地影响构建与购买决策。我们提出一个预先注册的实验方案，研究配置机制如何改变两种流行的自主式AI编码工具（Claude Code和OpenAI Codex）中的构建与购买行为。我们将执行来自分阶段项目基准的受控编程任务，每个任务围绕可识别的构建与购买点构建，并操纵提供给每种工具的配置（范围从无配置，到包含软偏好和明确禁止的上下文文件，到技能（可自主发现的指令）、支持MCP的库发现工具和权限控制），测量工具选择了哪些库、是否披露了新引入的库以及这些披露是否完整和准确。九个预先注册的假设构成了该方案的结构。所得到的基准数据集和分析流程将作为可复用的工件发布，用于评估自主式AI编码工具中的构建与购买行为。

Original abstract: Agentic AI coding tools write code with increasing autonomy and in doing so decide when to import a library and when to implement functionality from scratch. These decisions, whether to build functionality from scratch or buy into an external library, hereafter build-versus-buy, carry direct consequences for software security, licensing compliance, performance, and long-term maintainability. Yet no controlled experimental study has examined what governs build-versus-buy decisions in agentic AI coding tools. Configuration mechanisms, i.e., the means by which developers tailor agentic AI coding tool behavior to a project or workflow, are one of the primary means by which practitioners can influence these decisions. However, it is unclear which configuration mechanisms influence build-versus-buy decisions most effectively. We present a pre-registered protocol to study how configuration mechanisms alter build-versus-buy behavior in two popular agentic AI coding tools: Claude Code and OpenAI Codex. We will execute controlled programming tasks drawn from a benchmark of staged projects, each constructed around identifiable build-versus-buy points, and will manipulate the configuration supplied to each tool, ranging from no configuration, through context files with soft preferences and explicit prohibitions, to Skills (instructions that can be autonomously discovered), MCP-enabled library discovery tools, and permission controls, measuring which libraries the tool selects, whether it discloses newly introduced libraries, and whether those disclosures are complete and accurate. Nine pre-registered hypotheses structure the protocol. The resulting benchmark dataset and analysis pipeline will be released as a reusable artifact for evaluating build-versus-buy behavior in agentic AI coding tools.

</details>


### [16] [Proof-Carrying Agent Actions: Model-Agnostic Runtime Governance for Heterogeneous Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04104v1)
*Zexun Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Proof-Carrying Agent Actions (PCAA)，一种运行时无关的智能体治理模型，通过动作证书和五个检查点实现可移植的授权与证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体运行时控制点不同，导致相同高风险动作在不同系统中形式各异，难以统一回答授权、批准和证据等治理问题。

Method: 设计PCAA模型，以动作证书为中心，包含五个检查点（可接受性、动作开始、假设捕获、批准、结果关闭），并扩展外部性意识和可执行性类别；通过异构控制平面参考实现和96条轨迹的基准测试进行评估。

Result: PCAA在保留路由质量的同时，在消融实验中暴露了不同失败模式，验证了可移植性和治理一致性。

Conclusion: PCAA提供了运行时无关的治理形式化，能在运行时变更下保持可移植性，避免供应商锁定，并贡献了基于实现的实际经验。

中文摘要：智能体系统通过具有非常不同控制点的运行时执行：本地编码工具、框架SDK、托管智能体平台、API网关和仅观察集成。因此，一个高风险操作（如外部发布数据）可能在一个运行时表现为shell命令，在另一个运行时表现为工具调用，在第三个运行时表现为托管会话转换。这使得难以一致地回答一个基本的治理问题：什么操作被授权，在谁的授权下，具有什么批准语义，以及执行后有什么证据？本文提出了证明承载智能体动作（PCAA），一种以动作证书而非供应商原生会话记录为中心的运行时无关治理模型。PCAA围绕五个检查点组织控制：动作前可接受性、动作开始、假设捕获、批准和结果关闭。它将这些检查点绑定到可移植的动作信封、运行时和批准收据以及可重放证明。该模型通过两种实际方式扩展：证书具有外部性意识，承载边界事实如目标可见性和账户来源；批准由显式的可执行性类别描述，而非单一的已审查或未审查位。我们通过一个在异构智能体控制平面中的参考实现和一个披露有界评估协议来研究该模型。在一个受保护的基准测试上，从24个可执行种子扩展到跨越四个运行时家族的96条轨迹，PCAA在保留路由质量的同时，在消融下暴露了不同的失败模式。本文贡献了围绕证书承载动作的运行时治理的系统形式化，以及一个基于实现的说明，说明该形式化如何能够在运行时变更下保持可移植性，而不会崩溃到供应商特定的控制表面。

Original abstract: Agent systems execute through runtimes with very different control points: local coding tools, framework SDKs, managed agent platforms, API gateways, and observer-only integrations. A high-risk action such as publishing data externally may therefore appear as a shell command in one runtime, a tool call in another, and a hosted session transition in a third. This makes it difficult to answer a basic governance question consistently: what action was authorized, under whose authority, with what approval semantics, and with what evidence after execution?
  This paper presents Proof-Carrying Agent Actions (PCAA), a runtime-neutral governance model centered on an action certificate rather than on a vendor-native session record. PCAA organizes control around five checkpoints: pre-action admissibility, action open, assumption capture, approval, and outcome closure. It binds these checkpoints to a portable action envelope, runtime and approval receipts, and replay-ready proof. The model is extended in two practical ways: the certificate is externality-aware, carrying boundary facts such as destination visibility and account provenance, and approval is described by explicit enforceability classes rather than by a single reviewed or unreviewed bit.
  We study the model through a reference implementation in a heterogeneous agent control plane and a disclosure-bounded evaluation protocol. On a protected benchmark expanded from 24 executable seeds to 96 traces across four runtime families, PCAA preserves route quality while exposing distinct failure modes under ablation. The paper contributes a systems formulation of runtime governance around certificate-bearing actions and an implementation-grounded account of how that formulation can remain portable under runtime churn without collapsing into vendor-specific control surfaces.

</details>


### [17] [Where Do Large Language Models Fail on Competitive Programming? A Taxonomy of Failures by Algorithm Type and Difficulty Rating](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05228v1)
*Ayush Kumar Jha,Shalini Jha*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对GPT-4o和Claude在Codeforces问题上的系统研究发现，强制思维链会损害GPT-4o的通过率并加剧其贪心逻辑缺陷，同时增加Claude的编译错误，表明标准提示工程无法弥补算法推理差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要报告聚合通过率，掩盖了LLM在特定算法领域的脆弱性，需要系统研究失败模式。

Method: 使用315个Codeforces问题（7类算法、3个难度等级）进行平衡分类，评估GPT-4o和Claude Sonnet 4.6，控制温度0.2，进行消融研究比较零样本和零样本思维链。

Result: 强制CoT使GPT-4o通过率从46.0%降至36.8%，贪心逻辑弱点加剧；Claude通过率63.5%但编译错误增加244%；错误答案占绝大多数。

Conclusion: 标准提示工程不能弥合竞争性编程中的算法推理差距。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在竞争性编程基准测试中展现出日益增强的能力，然而技术报告主要发布聚合通过率，掩盖了特定领域的弱点。我们使用一个平衡的分类法，包含315个Codeforces问题，涵盖七种算法类别和三个难度等级，对LLM的失败模式进行了系统的实证研究。我们在严格的执行条件下评估了GPT-4o和Claude Sonnet 4.6，控制了温度（T=0.2）。为了隔离推理框架对算法正确性的影响，我们进行了一项消融研究，比较直接零样本生成与零样本思维链（CoT）。我们的发现揭示了与标准NLP基准的严重背离：强制使用CoT会严重惩罚GPT-4o，使其通过率从46.0%下降到36.8%，并加剧了其在贪心逻辑方面的关键弱点。相反，虽然Claude在CoT下保持了更高的逻辑基线（63.5%），但扩展的文本生成严重降低了其Markdown指令遵循能力，导致其编译错误增加了两倍以上（从9次增加到31次，增幅244%）。此外，失败模式分析表明，对于两个模型，错误答案（WA）是主要判决——占GPT-4o未通过解决方案的90%以上，以及Claude的大约70%。这些发现实证表明，标准的提示工程技巧无法弥合竞争性编程环境中的算法推理差距。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate increasing proficiency on competitive programming benchmarks, yet technical reports predominantly publish aggregate pass rates, obscuring domain-specific vulnerabilities. We present a systematic empirical study of LLM failure patterns using a balanced taxonomy of 315 Codeforces problems across seven algorithm categories and three difficulty tiers. We evaluate GPT-4o and Claude Sonnet 4.6 under strict execution-based conditions, controlling for temperature (T = 0.2). To isolate the impact of reasoning frameworks on algorithmic correctness, we conduct an ablation study comparing direct zero-shot generation against zero-shot Chain-of-Thought (CoT). Our findings reveal a severe divergence from standard NLP benchmarks: forcing CoT aggressively penalizes GPT-4o, dropping its pass rate from 46.0% to 36.8% and exacerbating a critical weakness in Greedy logic. Conversely, while Claude maintains a higher logical baseline (63.5% under CoT), the expanded text generation severely degrades its markdown instruction adherence, causing its Compile Errors to more than triple (from 9 to 31, a 244% increase). Furthermore, failure-mode analysis indicates that Wrong Answer (WA) is the dominant verdict for both models--accounting for over 90% of GPT-4o's and roughly 70% of Claude's unaccepted solutions. These findings empirically demonstrate that standard prompt engineering techniques fail to bridge the algorithmic reasoning gap in competitive programming environments.

</details>

### [18] [Inducing Reasoning Primitives from Agent Traces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02994v1)
*Zhihan Lei,Jiarui Yan,Joshua Momo,William W. Cohen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 从ReAct agent轨迹归纳推理原语，直接提升agent性能，方法可迁移

TL;DR: 提出推理原语归纳方法，从ReAct轨迹中挖掘并聚类高频推理动作形成伪工具库，使归纳出的库性能超越原始智能体，在多个推理任务上显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ReAct-style LLM agents often rediscover the same reasoning routines across problems but leave them trapped in transient scratchpads, leading to inefficiency. We aim to extract and reuse these routines.

Method: We propose Reasoning Primitive Induction, a single-pass method that mines successful ReAct traces, clusters recurrent reasoning moves, and converts the most frequent moves into a compact library of typed pseudo-tools with natural-language docstrings, then composes them in a standard ReAct loop at test time.

Result: Induced libraries outperform the agent that generated their traces: +44pp on RuleArena NBA, +30pp on MuSR team allocation, +22pp on NatPlan meeting planning. Across five subtasks, a fixed configuration improves over zero-shot CoT, matches/exceeds expert decompositions, and outperforms AWM at lower cost.

Conclusion: The proposed method effectively distills reusable reasoning primitives from ReAct agents, leading to substantial performance gains and efficiency improvements, suggesting that capturing and reusing reasoning patterns is beneficial.

中文摘要：ReAct风格的LLM智能体通常在不同问题中重新发现相同的推理例程，却将这些例程困在瞬态草稿板中。我们引入了推理原语归纳，这是一种单次方法，挖掘成功的ReAct轨迹，聚类重复的推理动作，并将最频繁的动作转换为紧凑的类型化伪工具库。每个伪工具由一条自然语言文档字符串指定，供LLM在调用时解释，而标准ReAct循环在测试时组合这些原语。核心结果是，归纳出的库优于生成其轨迹的智能体本身：在RuleArena NBA上提升44个百分点（30→74），在MuSR团队分配上提升30个百分点（38→68），在NatPlan会议规划上提升22个百分点（7→29）。在跨越叙事演绎、规则应用和约束满足规划的五个可比较子任务中，单个固定配置在零样本思维链上的每个子任务均有提升，匹配或超越专家编写的分解，并以更低的平均推理成本优于AWM。

Original abstract: ReAct-style LLM agents often rediscover the same reasoning routines across problems, yet leave those routines trapped in transient scratchpads. We introduce Reasoning Primitive Induction, a single-pass method that mines successful ReAct traces, clusters recurrent reasoning moves, and converts the most frequent moves into a compact library of typed pseudo-tools. Each pseudo-tool is specified by a natural-language docstring interpreted by an LLM at invocation time, and a standard ReAct loop composes these primitives at test time. The central result is that induced libraries outperform the very agent that generated their traces: by +44pp on RuleArena NBA (30 -> 74), +30pp on MuSR team allocation (38 -> 68), and +22pp on NatPlan meeting planning (7 -> 29). Across five comparable subtasks spanning narrative deduction, rule application, and constraint-satisfaction planning, a single fixed configuration improves over zero-shot Chain-of-Thought on every subtask, matches or surpasses expert-authored decompositions, and outperforms AWM at lower average inference cost.

</details>


### [19] [AUDITFLOW: Executable Symbolic Environments for Structured Financial Reporting Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03031v1)
*Yan Wang,Xuguang Ai,Jaisal Patel,Xueqing Peng,Fengran Mo,Yupeng Cao,Haohang Li,Mingyu Cao,Lingfei Qian,Víctor Gutiérrez-Basulto*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent审计框架，含符号环境与工具使用，架构可迁移

TL;DR: AuditFlow是一个基于图的多智能体框架，通过符号环境分离自适应搜索与确定性验证，在财务审计任务中达到82.09%准确率，显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构化财务审计验证对语言模型困难，因为正确性依赖于结构化证据而非纯文本，模型需链接事实、遍历关系并重新计算预期值。

Method: 提出AuditFlow框架，构建包含US-GAAP分类图和XBRL申报图的符号环境，通过类型化工具提供事实检索、分类遍历、数值检查和规则评估；采用两个初级审计员（监管和证据视角）和一个高级审计员进行多智能体协作，最终通过证据聚合生成审计结果。

Result: 在FinMR样本上，AuditFlow在GPT-5.5下联合审计准确率为82.09%，比最强基线高14.93个百分点；移除确定性检查后准确率降至17.91%。

Conclusion: 符号环境执行了语言模型无法可靠替代的验证步骤，确定性检查对准确率至关重要。

中文摘要：结构化财务审计验证对于语言模型代理来说是困难的，因为正确性取决于结构化证据而不仅仅是文本。模型必须将报告的事实与分类法概念联系起来，遍历计算或维度关系，并在应用审计规则之前重新计算预期值。我们提出了AuditFlow，一个基于图的多智能体框架，它将自适应搜索与确定性验证分开。AuditFlow从一个静态的US-GAAP分类图和一个动态的XBRL申报图构建一个符号环境，并通过类型化工具暴露它，用于事实检索、分类法遍历、数值检查和规则评估。两个初级审计员从监管和证据角度检查每个案例，而一个高级审计员解决分歧并可以要求进一步调查。最终报告通过证据聚合融合，产生审计裁决、预期值、证据链和可信度评分。在一个源自FinAuditing的FinMR样本上，AuditFlow在GPT-5.5下达到了82.09%的联合审计准确率，比最强基线高出14.93个百分点。移除确定性检查后，准确率降至17.91%，表明符号环境执行了模型无法可靠替代的验证步骤。

Original abstract: Structured financial audit verification is difficult for language-model agents because correctness depends on structured evidence rather than text alone. A model must link reported facts to taxonomy concepts, traverse calculation or dimensional relations, and recompute expected values before applying an audit rule. We propose AuditFlow, a graph-grounded multi-agent framework that separates adaptive search from deterministic verification. AuditFlow builds a symbolic environment from a static US-GAAP taxonomy graph and a dynamic XBRL filing graph, and exposes it through typed tools for fact retrieval, taxonomy traversal, numerical checking, and rule evaluation. Two junior auditors inspect each case from regulatory and evidentiary views, while a senior auditor resolves disagreements and can request further investigation. The final reports are fused through evidential aggregation to produce an audit verdict, expected value, evidence trail, and trustworthiness score. On a FinAuditing-derived FinMR sample, AuditFlow reaches 82.09% joint audit accuracy under GPT-5.5, outperforming the strongest baseline by 14.93 points. Removing deterministic checks drops accuracy to 17.91%, showing that the symbolic environment performs the verification step that the model cannot reliably replace.

### [20] [Toward Pre-Deployment Assurance for Enterprise AI Agents: Ontology-Grounded Simulation and Trust Certification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04037v2)
*Thanh Luong Tuan,Abhijit Sanyal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于本体的验证框架，通过操作包络、场景生成和信任证书，在四个受监管行业测试中相比基线提升监管覆盖率（48.3% vs 33.1%），为企业AI预部署提供可审计保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业AI智能体的部署前验证存在空白，现有运行时监控和控制手段保证有限，亟需一种系统化的预部署验证方法。

Method: 构建基于本体的验证框架，包含Agent操作包络、本体到场景的生成流水线、机器可验证信任证书；在美越四行业五单元进行受控实验，生成1800个场景，对比基线评估。

Result: 基于本体的生成在监管覆盖率上显著优于基于角色的基线（48.3% vs 33.1%，p_c=0.0006），领域特异性最高（4.77/5.0，p=2e-6）；跨三个LLM系列验证结果一致。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了可重复、基于监管的预部署保证路径，可审计地补充运行时治理，适用于企业AI智能体部署前验证。

中文摘要：企业人工智能（AI）智能体的部署前验证仍然是大型语言模型（LLM）能力基准测试与生产部署之间的关键缺口。一旦智能体在生产环境中运行，部署后监控、人在回路控制以及提示级护栏提供的保证有限。我们提出了一种基于本体的验证框架——据我们所知，这是第一个结合三个组件的框架：一个智能体操作包络，形式化了跨权限、领域约束、安全属性、治理规则和自主级别的认证空间；一个本体到场景的生成流水线，自动推导出监管、操作和对抗性测试场景；以及一个带有分级部署裁决的机器可验证信任证书。在四个受监管行业（金融科技、银行、保险、医疗保健）进行了一项受控试点，实例化为美国和越南的五个行业-监管制度单元（越南2025年AI法强制要求金融服务进行此类验证），生成了1,800个场景，针对125个主要来源监管要求和25个注入故障进行了评估。基于本体的生成在监管覆盖率上显著优于主流基于角色的基线（48.3%对33.1%；校正后p_c = .0006），并达到了最高的领域特异性（4.77/5.0；p = 2e-6）；透明地说，与普通提示和检索增强提示相比，其优势未通过Bonferroni校正。跨三个LLM系列（Claude Sonnet 4、Qwen 2.5 72B、Gemma 4 26B；总共5,400个场景）的交叉验证复现了角色与本体模式。该框架为企业AI智能体提供了一条可重复、以监管为基础的部署前保证路径，用可审计的部署门禁补充运行时治理。

Original abstract: Pre-deployment verification of enterprise artificial intelligence (AI) agents remains a critical gap between large language model (LLM) capability benchmarking and production deployment. Post-deployment monitoring, human-in-the-loop controls, and prompt-level guardrails offer limited assurance once an agent is operating in production. We present an ontology-grounded verification framework -- to our knowledge the first to combine three components: an Agent Operational Envelope formalizing the certification space across permissions, domain constraints, safety properties, governance rules, and autonomy levels; an ontology-to-scenario generation pipeline that derives regulatory, operational, and adversarial test scenarios automatically; and a machine-verifiable Trust Certificate with graduated deployment verdicts. A controlled pilot across four regulated industries (Fintech, Banking, Insurance, Healthcare), instantiated as five industry-by-regulatory-regime cells across the United States and Vietnam (where Vietnam's 2025 AI Law makes such verification legally mandated for financial services), generated 1,800 scenarios evaluated against 125 primary-source regulatory requirements and 25 injected faults. Ontology-grounded generation significantly outperformed the dominant persona-based baseline on regulatory coverage (48.3% versus 33.1%; corrected p_c = .0006) and attained the highest domain specificity (4.77/5.0; p = 2e-6); transparently, its advantage over plain and retrieval-augmented prompting did not survive Bonferroni correction. Cross-validation across three LLM families (Claude Sonnet 4, Qwen 2.5 72B, Gemma 4 26B; 5,400 total scenarios) replicated the persona-versus-ontology pattern. The framework offers a reproducible, regulation-grounded route to pre-deployment assurance for enterprise AI agents, complementing runtime governance with an auditable deployment gate.

### [21] [ToolGate: Token-Efficient Pre-Call Control for Tool-Augmented Vision-Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03054v1)
*Anjie Liu,Yan Song,Zhixun Chen,Ziqin Gong,Zhongwei Yu,Jun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出 ToolGate 对工具增强 VLM agent 进行预调用控制，减少 token 成本，方法可迁移至 coding agent 的工具调用控制。

TL;DR: 提出ToolGate控制器，通过轨迹特征决定是否执行工具调用，在降低计算成本的同时保持或提升准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具调用成本高且部分不必要，基线代理对有益和有害调用缺乏选择性。

Method: 设计轻量级外部控制器ToolGate，基于ReAct轨迹文本和结构特征预测执行/跳过决策。

Result: 在Qwen3-VL上将token成本降至64-69%，准确率不变；在Qwen3-VL-30B上匹配训练后准确率提升1.65点。

Conclusion: 工具增强VLM代理需显式控制工具调用时机，以平衡性能与成本。

中文摘要：工具增强的视觉语言代理可以通过OCR、检测、分割等工具获取外部感知证据，但执行每一个提议的工具调用成本高昂且有时不必要。我们研究预调用控制问题：在ReAct风格的VLM代理提出感知工具调用后，应该执行该调用，还是在其输出进入上下文之前跳过？在五个基准测试中，我们发现基线代理表现出较差的局部选择性：有益调用和有害调用以相似的比例发生（11.8% vs. 9.9%），而大多数调用不会改变即时强制答案预测。我们引入了ToolGate，一个轻量级的外部控制器，它根据轨迹文本和简单的结构特征来预测执行/跳过决策。在两个Qwen3-VL骨干网络上，ToolGate将标记成本降低到无限制ReAct基线的64-69%，同时保持了跨领域设置的平均准确率。在Qwen3-VL-30B上进行匹配领域轨迹训练后，它进一步将平均准确率提高了1.65个百分点。这些结果表明，工具增强的VLM代理不仅受益于更好的感知工具，还受益于对工具输出何时值得支付代价的显式控制。

Original abstract: Tool-augmented vision-language agents can acquire external perceptual evidence through OCR, detection, segmentation, and other tools, but executing every proposed tool call is costly and sometimes unnecessary. We study the pre-call control problem: after a ReAct-style VLM agent proposes a perceptual tool call, should the call be executed, or skipped before its output enters the context? Across five benchmarks, we find that the baseline agent exhibits poor local selectivity: helpful and harmful calls occur at similar rates (11.8% vs. 9.9%), while most calls do not change the immediate forced-answer prediction. We introduce ToolGate, a lightweight external controller that predicts execute/skip decisions from trajectory text and simple structural features. Across two Qwen3-VL backbones, ToolGate reduces token cost to 64-69% of the unrestricted ReAct baseline while preserving average accuracy in cross-domain settings. With matched-domain trajectory training on Qwen3-VL-30B, it further improves average accuracy by 1.65 points. These results show that tool-augmented VLM agents benefit not only from better perceptual tools, but also from explicit control over when tool outputs are worth paying for.

### [22] [SkillDAG: Self-Evolving Typed Skill Graphs for LLM Skill Selection at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03056v2)
*Tong Bai,Zhenglin Wan,Pengfei Zhou,Xingrui Yu,Yang You,Ivor W. Tsang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: SkillDAG 为 LLM agent 提供结构化技能图检索与在线演化，属于通用 agent 技能管理方法，可迁移至 coding agent 的技能选择。

TL;DR: SkillDAG通过将技能关系建模为有类型有向图，为LLM智能体提供推理时可调用的结构化检索接口，显著提升技能选择性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖于全枚举或嵌入相似性，无法捕捉技能间的依赖、冲突、特化或重复等结构性关系，导致选择子集时效果不佳。

Method: 提出SkillDAG，构建技能关系的有类型有向图，并通过推理时可调用的接口进行查询和演化；采用向量匹配、类型化边邻居和冲突信号搜索，以及提议-提交协议使智能体能注册新边。

Result: 在ALFWorld和SkillsBench上，SkillDAG分别达到67.1%成功率和27.3%奖励，超越最强基线12.8和8.6个点；在更大规模下保持鲁棒性，召回率从65.5提升至78.2。

Conclusion: SkillDAG有效利用技能关系结构，提升了LLM智能体在大型技能库中选择子集的能力，且性能优势可迁移到其他模型。

中文摘要：随着LLM智能体采用大规模技能库，选择正确的子集成为一个结构性问题，而非相似性匹配问题：技能之间相互依赖、冲突、特化或重复，这种结构在完全枚举和嵌入相似性中都是不可见的。我们提出了SkillDAG，它将技能间关系建模为有类型的有向图，并将其作为推理时可被智能体调用的结构化检索接口暴露给LLM智能体，该接口在执行过程中被查询和演化，而非嵌入到固定的检索流程中：每次搜索返回向量匹配、类型化边邻居和冲突信号，并且一个“提议-提交”协议允许智能体注册执行支持的边，从而使图在跨回合中积累结构。在ALFWorld和SkillsBench上使用MiniMax-M2.7，SkillDAG达到了67.1%的成功率和27.3%的奖励，超过了最强的报告过的Graph-of-Skills基线，分别高出+12.8和+8.6个点；该优势迁移到了gpt-5.2-codex，并且在匹配查询下，内在的SkillsBench Ret@K从65.5上升到了78.2。这些收益可追溯到可隔离的机制：候选排序在池子扩大10倍时仍然稳健，而固定的种子扩散流程会退化；以及集合单调的在线编辑，它在不驱逐先前命中的情况下扩大了地面真实召回率。

Original abstract: As LLM agents adopt large skill libraries, selecting the right subset becomes a structural problem rather than a similarity-matching one: skills depend on, conflict with, specialize, or duplicate one another, a structure invisible to both full enumeration and embedding similarity. We present SkillDAG, which models inter-skill relationships as a typed directed graph and exposes it to an LLM agent as an inference-time, agent-callable structural retrieval interface, queried and evolved during execution rather than baked into a fixed retrieval pipeline: each search returns vector matches, typed-edge neighbors, and conflict signals, and a propose-then-commit protocol lets the agent register execution-backed edges so the graph accumulates structure across episodes. On ALFWorld and SkillsBench with MiniMax-M2.7, SkillDAG reaches 67.1% success and 27.3% reward, exceeding the strongest reported Graph-of-Skills baseline by +12.8 and +8.6 points; the advantage ports to gpt-5.2-codex, and intrinsic SkillsBench Ret@K rises from 65.5 to 78.2 under matched queries. These gains trace to isolable mechanisms: candidate ranking that stays robust as the pool grows 10x where a fixed seeding-diffusion pipeline degrades, and set-monotone online edits that enlarge ground-truth recall without evicting prior hits.

</details>


### [23] [DELTAMEM: Incremental Experience Memory for LLM Agents via Residual Trees](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03083v1)
*Haoran Tan,Zeyu Zhang,Zhicheng Cao,Rui Li,Xu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: DeltaMem 为 LLM agent 设计增量经验记忆树，减少冗余与冲突，属于通用记忆组织方法，可迁移至 coding agent。

TL;DR: DeltaMem通过将经验组织成残差树结构，使用增量节点和自主整合机制，解决了LLM智能体记忆中冗余和检索冲突的问题，在多种环境中优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体以独立扁平单元存储经验，导致大量冗余和检索时的冲突，因为相似场景重复内容且细微变化引起矛盾指导。

Method: 提出DeltaMem框架，将经验记忆组织为两个独立的残差树（技能树和环境知识树），每个树包含根节点（通用基础）和增量节点（变化），检索时使用失败惩罚相似度扫描和根到匹配链重构，并通过自主整合机制将高频路径提升为新根节点。

Result: 在多种交互环境中的实验表明，DeltaMem持续优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: DeltaMem通过残差树结构有效减少冗余和冲突，实现高效记忆组织与检索，且代码已开源。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体越来越依赖记忆来在持续交互中从经验中学习。然而，将经验存储为独立、扁平的单位会导致大量冗余和检索冲突，因为相似的场景会重复出现重叠内容，而微小的场景变化会导致检索到的记忆提供矛盾的指导。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了残差经验的概念，认为新获得的经验往往是现有知识的增量变化。我们提出了DeltaMem框架，该框架将经验记忆组织成两个独立的残差树，一个存储目标条件任务经验作为可复用技能，另一个存储场景级环境知识。每个树使用一个根节点表示通用的基础经验，以及若干增量节点表示后续的变体，使得相关经验能够共享共同的基础而无需重复。在检索时，一种失败惩罚相似度扫描会定位最佳匹配，并通过从根到匹配的链式组合重构完整经验。一种自主整合机制将高频路径提炼为新的根节点，从而使树能够从通用启发式方法自我组织到专门化变体。在多种交互环境中的实验表明，DeltaMem持续优于现有基线。为了促进未来研究，我们在https://github.com/import-myself/DeltaMem发布了代码。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents increasingly rely on memory to learn from experiences over continual interactions. However, storing experiences as independent, flat units leads to substantial redundancy and retrieval conflicts, as similar episodes repeat overlapping content and subtle scene variations cause retrieved memories to offer contradictory guidance. To address this, we introduce residual experience, positing that newly acquired experience is often an incremental variation of existing knowledge. We propose DeltaMem, a framework that organizes experience memory into two independent residual trees, one storing goal-conditioned task experience as reusable skills and another for scene-level environment knowledge. Each tree uses a root node for generalized base experiences and incremental delta nodes for subsequent variations, allowing related experiences to share a common foundation without duplication. For retrieval, a failure-penalized similarity scan locates the best match, reconstructing the full experience via root-to-match chain composition. An autonomous consolidation mechanism distills high-frequency paths into new root nodes, enabling the trees to self-organize from general heuristics to specialized variants. Experiments across diverse interactive environments show that DeltaMem consistently outperforms existing baselines. To facilitate future research, we release the code at https://github.com/import-myself/DeltaMem.

</details>


### [24] [DeskCraft: Benchmarking Desktop Agents on Professional Workflows and Human-in-the-Loop Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03103v1)
*Wenkai Wang,Tao Xiong,Jingchen Ni,Yunpeng Bao,Xiyun Li,Tianqi Liu,Hongcan Guo,Zilong Huang,Shengyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出桌面GUI agent benchmark，覆盖长程任务和人类协作交互协议，对agent评测有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出了DeskCraft基准，用于评估长时桌面工作流中的人机协作，发现现有代理在标准任务和交互任务上表现不佳，尤其在长时工作流和主动澄清方面存在持续失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有桌面GUI基准测试将真实世界长时工作流简化为短时、预先提供指令的任务，忽略了实际协作中代理主动寻求信息和用户提供反馈的需求。

Method: DeskCraft构建了多级难度的长时任务（超过50步），涵盖设计、视频、音频和3D软件，并定义了包含回合中（代理主动澄清、用户中断）和回合后（用户反馈）的交互协议。在538个任务上评估了18个代理。

Result: GPT-5.4在标准任务和交互任务上分别达到31.6%和27.6%，但分析显示代理在长时工作流交付和主动澄清方面表现不佳。

Conclusion: 当前桌面代理在长时工作流和交互能力上仍有显著不足，需要进一步研究以提升其自主性和协作能力。

中文摘要：在专业创意和工程软件中的实际桌面工作流通常跨越较长时间跨度，并且需要人在环中的协调，即代理主动寻求必要信息，用户随着任务进展提供额外指令、澄清、反馈或修正。然而，现有的桌面GUI基准测试大多将这一场景简化为短时、简化的任务，并且所有用户指令都预先提供。为了解决这一问题，我们引入了 DeskCraft，一个针对长时创意和工程工作流以及主动人机协作的桌面GUI基准测试。DeskCraft 将任务组织成多级难度分类，其中长时任务需要超过50个执行步骤，并涵盖设计、视频、音频和3D创作等专业创意软件。此外，DeskCraft 将人机协作形式化为一个包含回合中和回合后交流的交互协议。回合中交互既捕捉了代理在不确定情况下主动请求澄清，也捕捉了用户在执行过程中主动中断；而回合后交互则容纳了用户驱动的反馈（在代理发出完成信号后），共同覆盖了现实协作模式的全部空间。我们在538个任务上评估了18个专有和开源代理，发现 GPT-5.4 在标准任务上达到31.6%，在交互任务上达到27.6%。进一步分析揭示了在长时工作流交付和主动澄清方面的持续失败。我们将在 https://github.com/mrwwk/DeskCraft 开源所有评估代码、任务和数据。

Original abstract: Real-world professional desktop workflows in specialized creative and engineering software unfold over long horizons and often require human-in-the-loop coordination, where agents proactively seek necessary information and users provide additional instructions, clarifications, feedback, or corrections as the task progresses. Yet existing desktop GUI benchmarks mostly reduce this setting to short, simplified tasks with all user instructions provided upfront. To address this issue, we introduce DeskCraft, a desktop GUI benchmark targeting long horizon creative and engineering workflows and proactive human-agent collaboration. DeskCraft organizes tasks into a multilevel difficulty taxonomy, with long horizon tasks requiring over 50 execution steps, and covers professional creative software across design, video, audio, and 3D creation. Furthermore, DeskCraft formalizes human-agent collaboration into an interaction protocol covering mid-turn and post-turn exchanges. Mid-turn interaction captures both agent-initiated clarification under uncertainty and user-initiated interruption during execution, while post-turn interaction accommodates user-driven feedback after the agent signals completion, together spanning the full space of realistic collaboration patterns. We evaluate 18 proprietary and open source agents on 538 tasks and find that GPT-5.4 reaches 31.6% on standard tasks and 27.6% on interactive tasks. Further analyses reveal persistent failures in long horizon workflow delivery and proactive clarification. We will open-source all evaluation codes, tasks, and data at https://github.com/mrwwk/DeskCraft.

### [25] [EvoTrainer: Co-Evolving LLM Policies and Training Harnesses for Autonomous Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03108v2)
*Guhong Chen,Yingcheng Shi,Yongbin Li,Binhua Li,Xander Xu,Hu Wei,Shiwen Ni,Min Yang,Jieping Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM agent策略与训练harness协同进化框架，在agentic RL和代码生成上验证，直接相关。

TL;DR: EvoTrainer通过共同进化LLM策略和训练控制机制，在数学推理、代码生成和软件工程任务上匹配或超越人工设计的RL方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主LLM训练框架将训练控制机制视为静态，尤其是agentic RL中，标量奖励掩盖了多种失败模式，需要更动态的进化方法。

Method: EvoTrainer框架通过诊断轨迹级证据、修正诊断、回溯测试干预并积累可重用技能，实现策略与训练控制机制的共同进化。

Result: 在数学推理、竞赛编程代码生成和仓库级软件工程上，EvoTrainer匹配或超过人工RL基线，尤其在长周期agentic SWE上提升最大；轨迹分析显示策略分化、诊断防止无效高分分支、可重用技能影响后续搜索。

Conclusion: 自主LLM RL应超越配方搜索，走向策略与解释它们的训练控制机制的联合进化。

中文摘要：自主LLM训练通常被框架化为配方搜索，这使得训练控制机制在很大程度上是静态的。这一局限在基于agent的RL中更为突出，因为不断变化的瓶颈和标量奖励掩盖了多种失败模式。我们引入EvoTrainer，一个自主训练框架，通过经验反馈共同进化LLM策略和训练侧控制机制：它诊断轨迹级证据，修正诊断，回溯测试干预措施，并积累可重用技能。在数学推理、竞赛编程代码生成和仓库级软件工程上的评估表明，在相同的数据、代码库和评估协议下，EvoTrainer匹配或超过了人工设计的RL参考方法，其中在长周期agentic SWE上提升最大。轨迹分析表明，保留的策略在不同领域间分化，进化的诊断阻止了无效的高分分支被推广，可重用技能塑造了后续搜索。自主LLM RL应超越配方搜索，迈向策略与解释它们的训练控制机制的联合进化。

Original abstract: Autonomous LLM training is often framed as recipe search, which leaves the training harness largely static. This limitation sharpens in agentic RL, where shifting bottlenecks and scalar rewards mask diverse failure modes. We introduce EvoTrainer, an autonomous training framework that co-evolves LLM policies and training-side harnesses through empirical feedback: it diagnoses rollout-level evidence, revises diagnostics, backtests interventions, and accumulates reusable skills. Evaluated on mathematical reasoning, competitive-programming code generation, and repository-level software engineering, EvoTrainer matches or exceeds the human-engineered RL references under the same data, codebase, and evaluation protocol, with the largest gain on long-horizon agentic SWE. Trajectory analyses show that retained strategies diverge across domains, evolving diagnostics prevent invalid high-scoring branches from being promoted, and reusable skills shape later search. Autonomous LLM RL should move beyond recipe search toward joint evolution of policies and the training harnesses that interpret them.

### [26] [Uncertainty-Aware Clarification in LLM Agents with Information Gain](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03135v1)
*Mengyi Deng,Zhiwei Li,Xin Li,Tingyu Zhu,Ying Zhao,Zhijiang Guo,Wei Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出信息增益奖励的agent澄清框架，可减少不确定性，适用于coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出基于信息增益奖励的目标导向澄清框架，在τ-Bench上提升任务成功率3.7%，仅增加0.3交互步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理在模糊用户指令下常因意图不确定性导致工具操作错误。

Method: 构建信息增益奖励度量澄清问题的效用，并用该奖励训练LLM澄清器，以生成高信息增益的澄清问题。

Result: 在τ-Bench环境中跨五个骨干模型验证，成功率比无澄清基线提高3.7%，平均交互步仅增加0.3。

Conclusion: 所提方法能有效减少不确定性并提升任务完成，同时额外交互成本极低。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理通常在指定不明确的用户指令下运行，其中用户意图的潜在不确定性会导致错误的工具操作。为了解决这一挑战，我们提出了一种目标导向的澄清框架，将澄清行为与歧义消解对齐。我们方法的核心是信息增益奖励，这是一个通过测量由澄清交换引起的对真实目标的贝叶斯信念更新来量化澄清问题效用的指标。我们使用该奖励训练澄清器（LLM），以优化高信息增益，确保澄清有效减少不确定性并提高代理-工具-用户环境中的任务完成率。我们在一个增强澄清的τ-Bench环境中验证了我们的框架，跨五个异构骨干进行了跨代理评估。实验结果表明，我们的方法在无澄清基线上持续提高了3.7%的成功率，同时平均仅增加了0.3个总交互步骤。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents often operate under underspecified user instructions, where latent uncertainty over user intent leads to erroneous tool actions. To address this challenge, we propose a goal-oriented clarification framework that aligns clarification behavior with ambiguity resolution. Central to our approach is the Information Gain Reward, a metric that quantifies the utility of clarification questions by measuring the Bayesian belief update towards the ground-truth goal induced by the clarification exchange. We train the clarifier (LLM) using this reward to optimize for high information gain, ensuring that clarifications effectively reduce uncertainty and improve task completion within the agent-tool-user environment. We validate our framework within a clarification-enhanced $τ$-Bench environment, conducting cross-agent evaluations across five heterogeneous backbones. Empirical results demonstrate that our method consistently improves the success rate by 3.7\% over the no-clarification baseline, while adding only 0.3 total interaction steps on average.

### [27] [Think-Before-Speak: From Internal Evaluation to Public Expression in Multi-Agent Social Simulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03137v2)
*Kaiqi Yang,Tai-Quan Peng,Sanguk Lee,Hui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent社会模拟的内外推理框架，可迁移至协作coding agent设计。

TL;DR: TBS是一个基于间隔的多智能体模拟框架，通过分离私人推理和公开表达，使内部评估过程可观察，并在气候政策讨论中验证了其对沉默、记忆和轮次分配等机制的敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话模拟框架难以考察沉默、发言意图和公开表达背后的内部评估过程，因此需要一种能分离内部推理与公开表达的框架。

Method: 提出TBS框架，每个间隔内智能体更新包含失调、感知舆论氛围等的内部状态，协调器解决发言冲突，使内部评估与公共互动共同演化。

Result: TBS产生连贯的内部状态轨迹，失调增加发言意愿，沉默压力降低发言意愿，公开表达受轮次分配主导。

Conclusion: TBS支持机制敏感的社会模拟，使从内部评估到公开表达的路径可观察和分析。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体模拟为研究社会互动、讨论和集体舆论动态提供了一种有前景的方式。然而，许多现有的对话模拟框架主要将互动表示为可观察的对话轮次或聚合输出，使得沉默、发言意图和公开表达背后的内部评估过程难以考察。我们提出了TBS（Think-Before-Speak），一种基于间隔的多智能体模拟框架，将智能体的私人推理与公开话语生成分离。在每个间隔内，所有智能体基于共享对话历史和自身记忆更新结构化内部状态。这些状态包括失调相关评估、感知舆论氛围、感知孤立风险、回应策略和发言意愿。协调器随后解决冲突的发言意图，并将一个话语提交到公开对话中，使得内部评估和公共互动随时间共同演化。我们在模拟关于气候相关政策议题的市政厅讨论中评估TBS。结果表明，TBS产生连贯的内部状态轨迹，并且这些轨迹在轮次分配、沉默和记忆条件下系统性地变化。失调相关评估增加了智能体的发言意愿，而沉默压力评估则降低了它。一旦发言意图形成，公开表达主要由轮次分配规则塑造。这些发现表明，TBS通过使从内部评估到公开表达的路径可观察和可分析，支持机制敏感的社会模拟。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent simulation offers a promising way to study social interaction, deliberation, and collective opinion dynamics. However, many existing dialogue simulation frameworks represent interaction mainly as observable turn exchange or aggregated outputs, leaving the internal evaluative processes behind silence, speaking intention, and public expression difficult to examine. We introduce TBS (Think-Before-Speak), an interval-based multi-agent simulation framework that separates agents' private reasoning from public utterance generation. At each interval, all agents update structured internal states based on the shared dialogue history and their own memory. These states include dissonance-related appraisal, perceived opinion climate, perceived isolation risk, response strategy, and willingness to speak. The orchestrator then resolves competing speaking intentions and commits one utterance to the public dialogue, allowing internal evaluation and public interaction to co-evolve over time.
  We evaluate TBS in simulated town hall discussions on a climate-related policy issue. Results show that TBS produces coherent internal-state traces and that these traces vary systematically across turn-allocation, silence, and memory conditions. Dissonance-related appraisal increases agents' willingness to speak, whereas silence-pressure appraisal decreases it. Once speaking intention is formed, public expression is shaped mainly by turn-allocation rules. These findings suggest that TBS supports mechanism-sensitive social simulation by making the pathway from internal evaluation to public expression observable and analyzable.

### [28] [MedCUA-Bench: A Screenshot-Only Benchmark for Clinical Computer-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03203v1)
*Jia Yu,Zilong Wang,Xinyang Jiang,Dongsheng Li,Shuo Wang*

Method: 构建了覆盖10个医疗领域18个场景的交互式基准，从真实手册和开源系统重建，提供意图和步骤级目标，并使用确定性检查器评估任务完成和五个安全维度。

Original abstract: Computer-use agents could automate repetitive screen-based clinical work, but their reliability in medical graphical user interfaces remains largely unvalidated. Existing benchmarks focus on general web or desktop tasks and underrepresent medical software, which requires domain knowledge, exhibits markedly different UI design from mainstream applications, lacks public testing environments, and demands safety validation beyond task completion. We introduce MedCUA-Bench, an interactive benchmark for clinical computer-use agents. It covers 18 clinical scenarios across 10 medical domains, reconstructed from real product manuals and open-source medical systems to capture authentic clinical interfaces while avoiding licensing and privacy constraints. Each task ships with paired intent- and step-level goals to disentangle clinical reasoning from UI execution, and is evaluated by a deterministic checker over task completion and five clinical safety dimensions. Across 23 agents, the best closed-source model reaches 54.2% strict success, while all models remain below 9% on the real OpenEMR. Open-source agents average only 2.5%, with the best reaching 16.2%. MedCUA-Bench exposes the gap between current agents and reliable clinical software use, providing a reproducible testbed for future research.

### [29] [SkillHarness: Harnessing Safe Skills for Computer-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20636v1)
*Yurun Chen,Biao Yi,Keting Yin,Shengyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出安全技能学习框架，可迁移至coding agent的技能复用与安全约束。

TL;DR: 提出SkillHarness框架，通过安全约束和选择性技能复用，使CUA在动态环境中安全学习技能，降低不安全率57.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能学习方法假设静态安全环境，忽视动态环境中的对抗交互和环境变化风险，导致CUA可靠性不足。

Method: 将技能学习建模为安全约束交互过程，引入技能边界利用多源监督识别安全技能，并构建自改进安全约束；采用选择性技能复用，根据上下文分解任务并激活技能子集。

Result: 学习技能不安全率降低57.1%，在动态变化下执行稳定性优于现有基线。

Conclusion: SkillHarness有效提升CUA在动态环境中技能学习与使用的安全性及稳定性。

中文摘要：计算机使用智能体（CUA）越来越多地部署在动态交互环境中，这产生了在交互过程中持续学习技能的日益增长的需求。最近的方法通过从成功的轨迹中学习可重用的技能来应对这一挑战。然而，这些技能学习方法大多假设静态且安全的环境，忽视了来自对抗性交互（例如提示注入）和环境动态（例如弹窗）的风险。在动态环境中，此类假设可能导致危险的技能学习和不稳定的执行，削弱CUA的可靠性。这引出了一个问题：CUA如何在动态环境中安全地学习和使用技能？为解决这一问题，我们提出了SkillHarness，一个用于在动态环境中安全利用技能的框架。SkillHarness超越了静态技能抽象，将技能学习与利用建模为受安全约束的交互过程。具体而言，我们引入了技能边界，利用多源监督信号从交互轨迹中识别安全技能，并在整个技能生命周期中构建自我改进的安全约束。此外，SkillHarness引入了选择性技能复用，其中任务根据上下文被引导分解，并通过技能子集的选择性激活完成。我们的实验表明，SkillHarness将学习技能的不安全率降低了57.1%，并在动态环境变化下持续提高执行稳定性，优于现有基线。

Original abstract: Computer-Use Agents (CUAs) are increasingly deployed in dynamic interactive environments, creating a growing need for continual skill learning during interaction. Recent approaches address this challenge by learning reusable skills from successful trajectories. However, these skill learning methods largely assume static and safe environments, overlooking risks from adversarial interactions (e.g., prompt injections) and environmental dynamics (e.g., pop-ups). In dynamic settings, such assumptions can lead to risky skill learning and brittle execution, undermining the reliability of CUAs. This raises the question: how can CUAs learn and use skills safely in dynamic environments? To address this problem, we propose SkillHarness, a framework for safe skill harnessing in dynamic environments. SkillHarness moves beyond static skill abstractions by modeling skill learning and utilization as a safety-constrained interaction process. Specifically, we introduce the skill boundary that leverages multi-source supervision signals to identify safe skills from interaction trajectories, and construct self-improving safety constraints throughout the skill lifecycle. In addition, SkillHarness introduces selective skill reuse, where tasks are guided to decompose according to context and completed through the selective activation of skill subsets. Our experiments demonstrate that SkillHarness significantly reduces the unsafe rate of learned skills by 57.1% and consistently improves execution stability under dynamic environmental changes, outperforming existing baselines.
