### [30] [Perceive Before Reasoning: A Pre-Reasoning Perception Framework for Efficient and Reliable Proactive Mobile Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03236v1)
*Zhijie Ding,Weinan Hong,Zicheng Zhu,Lei Li,Dezhi Kong,Hao Wang,Peng Zhou,Xuchu Jiang,Jiaming Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 两阶段感知-推理框架用于主动干预，可迁移至agent何时介入决策。

TL;DR: PRPF通过两阶段先感知后推理框架，使用轻量级MPP进行干预门控和上下文压缩，仅在有需要时激活PAR，从而在降低误触发率的同时提升成功率和推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统将干预时机决策和协助生成统一在MLLM流水线中，导致干预过滤与辅助生成目标不一致，以及不需要干预时的冗余推理。

Method: 提出预推理感知框架（PRPF），包含两个阶段：第一阶段使用轻量级多模态主动感知器（MPP）进行干预门控和上下文压缩，第二阶段仅在需要干预时激活主动智能体推理器（PAR）进行协助生成。

Result: 在ProactiveMobile基准上，PRPF相比基线显著降低误触发率（FTR），同时提高成功率（SR）和推理效率。

Conclusion: PRPF通过分离干预决策和协助生成，有效解决了目标错位和冗余推理问题，提升了主动移动辅助的性能和效率。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）已大幅推进了移动智能体，但主动式移动辅助仍然具有挑战性，因为智能体必须在决定“如何”协助之前先判断“何时”进行干预。现有系统通常将这两个决策统一实现在基于MLLM的流水线中，导致保守的干预过滤与全面的辅助生成之间的目标错位，以及在智能体应保持静默时的冗余推理。为解决这些限制，我们提出了**预推理感知框架（PRPF）**，这是一个基于“先感知后推理”的两阶段框架。PRPF引入了一个轻量级的多模态主动感知器（MPP）用于干预门控和上下文压缩，并仅在需要干预时激活主动智能体推理器（PAR）。在ProactiveMobile基准上的实验表明，与ProactiveMobile基线相比，PRPF显著降低了误触发率（FTR），同时提高了成功率（SR）和推理效率。

Original abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have substantially advanced mobile agents, yet proactive mobile assistance remains challenging because agents must decide \emph{when} to intervene before determining \emph{how} to assist. Existing systems often implement these two decisions within a unified MLLM-based pipeline, leading to goal misalignment between conservative intervention filtering and comprehensive assistance generation, as well as redundant inference when the agent should remain silent. To address these limitations, we propose the \textbf{Pre-Reasoning Perception Framework (PRPF)}, a two-stage framework built on perceiving before reasoning. PRPF introduces a lightweight Multimodal Proactive Perceptor (MPP) for intervention gating and context compression, and activates the Proactive Agent Reasoner (PAR) only when intervention is warranted. Experiments on the ProactiveMobile benchmark show that PRPF substantially reduces false trigger rates (FTR) while improving success rates (SR) and inference efficiency over the ProactiveMobile baseline.

</details>


### [31] [Solipsistic Superintelligence is Unlikely to be Cooperative](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03237v1)
*Rakshit S Trivedi,Natasha Jaques,Logan Cross,Alexander Sasha Vezhnevets,Joel Z Leibo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 探讨AI合作性，对agent设计有启发，但非具体方法。

TL;DR: 本文批判AI唯我论范式，指出其导致合作困难与部署失效，提出非唯我论研究范式，将相互依赖作为核心设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI孤立优化导致部署时分布偏移与性能下降，缺乏与人类和其他系统的合作能力。

Method: 提出构建动态评估测试平台、将制度作为设计原语、保留人类能动性等非唯我论设计方法。

Result: 论证了单边优化的自我破坏属性，并指出合作是缩小训练-测试-部署差距的关键。

Conclusion: 呼吁转向非唯我论范式，将相互依赖作为核心设计原则，以促进AI与人类共存。

中文摘要：人工智能的核心挑战正从能力转向共存。当前AI研究的主导范式侧重于开发强大的智能体，这些智能体将世界视为外生的、静止的反馈源。我们认为，源于这种唯我论AI设计方法的超级智能（一种极其强大的任务解决者）不太可能具有合作性。部署AI系统会引发内生的非平稳性，导致训练-测试-部署差距，即历史分布与部署环境相偏离。我们将其称为单边优化的自我破坏属性。缩小这一差距需要参与合作的AI：即多个行为体相互依赖的均衡选择过程。我们呼吁一种非唯我论的研究范式，将这种相互依赖视为核心设计原则，而不是将合作视为一个待解决的任务。这包括构建涉及适应性对手的动态评估测试平台，将制度视为设计原语，以及保留人类能动性作为我们构建系统的结构特征。

Original abstract: AI's central challenge is shifting from capability to coexistence. The dominant paradigm in AI research focuses on developing powerful agents that treat the world as an exogenous and stationary source of feedback. We contend that superintelligence, an extremely capable task solver, born out of such a solipsistic approach to AI design, is unlikely to be cooperative. Deploying AI systems induces endogenous non-stationarity, resulting in a train-test-deploy gap where historical distributions diverge from the deployment context. We refer to this as the self-undermining property of unilateral optimization. Closing this gap requires AI that participates in cooperation: the equilibrium-selection process through which multiple actors navigate their interdependence. We call for a non-solipsistic research paradigm that treats this interdependence as a core design principle rather than approaching cooperation as a task to solve. This entails building dynamic evaluation testbeds involving adaptive counterparties, treating institutions as design primitives, and preserving human agency as a structural feature of the systems we build.

</details>


### [32] [Distilling Answer-Set Programming Rules from LLMs for Neurosymbolic Visual Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03269v3)
*Thomas Eiter,Nelson Higuera Ruiz,Johannes Oetsch*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM蒸馏ASP规则，可视为agent利用LLM生成结构化知识。

TL;DR: 提出从LLM蒸馏规则来扩展VQA推理理论，利用示例和ASP求解器反馈，仅需少量示例即可获得有效规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模块化VQA方法虽具有可解释性，但任务需求变化时规则扩展困难，开发者负担重。因此需要一种自动从LLM获取规则的方法。

Method: 通过提示LLM扩展初始回答集程序，利用VQA示例指导LLM，并使用ASP求解器的反馈验证和纠正规则。

Result: 在多个VQA数据集上有效，仅需少量示例即可从LLM引出正确规则，性能优于传统数据驱动方法。

Conclusion: 规则蒸馏从LLM中获取规则是一种有前景的替代传统规则学习的方法。

中文摘要：视觉问答（VQA）是回答关于图像问题的任务，需要整合多模态输入和推理。将基于逻辑的表示纳入推理组件的模块化方法，相比端到端训练的系统具有明显优势，特别是在可解释性方面。然而，当任务需求变化时，调整或扩展这些表示可能会给开发者带来沉重负担。为了解决这一挑战，我们提出了一种从大型语言模型（LLM）中蒸馏规则的方法。我们的方法提示LLM扩展一个初始的VQA推理理论（表示为回答集程序），以满足任务的新需求。VQA数据集中的示例引导LLM，验证结果，并通过利用ASP求解器的反馈帮助纠正错误规则。我们证明了该方法在多种VQA数据集上有效。值得注意的是，仅需少量示例即可从LLM中引出正确规则。我们的实验表明，从LLM中蒸馏规则是传统数据驱动规则学习方法的一个有前景的替代方案。正在考虑发表于《逻辑编程理论与实践》（TPLP）。

Original abstract: Visual Question Answering (VQA) is the task of answering questions about images, requiring the integration of multimodal input and reasoning. Modular approaches that incorporate logic-based representations into the reasoning component offer clear advantages over end-to-end trained systems, particularly in terms of interpretability. However, adapting or extending these representations when task requirements change can place a significant burden on developers. To address this challenge, we present an approach for distilling rules from Large Language Models (LLMs). Our method prompts an LLM to extend an initial VQA reasoning theory, expressed as an answer-set program, to meet new requirements of the task. Examples from VQA datasets guide the LLM, validate the results, and help correct erroneous rules by leveraging feedback from the ASP solver. We demonstrate that our approach is effective across diverse VQA datasets. Notably, only a few examples are needed to elicit correct rules from LLMs. Our experiments suggest that rule distillation from LLMs is a promising alternative to traditional data-driven rule learning approaches. Under consideration in Theory and Practice of Logic Programming (TPLP).

</details>


### [33] [A Negative Result on Cross-Model Activation Transfer in a Pythia Multi-Hop Setting](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03280v2)
*Peiyan Zhang,Jason Xin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 跨模型激活转移负结果，对agent间通信有参考。

TL;DR: 研究语言模型间通过激活桥传递推理状态的可能性，发现线性映射虽能对齐表示，但注入激活无益，得出负面结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索语言模型间是否可以通过非文本的激活通道（线性激活桥）在推理时传递中间推理状态，以替代传统的文本或结构化令牌中继。

Method: 在Pythia-160M到Pythia-410M的多跳推理任务中，训练线性翻译层学习发送方和接收方隐藏状态的映射，然后在推理时以加法或替换方式注入翻译后的激活，评估下游回答性能。

Result: 线性翻译层达到高余弦相似度（0.97），但注入激活未提升性能，加法注入无改善，替换注入有破坏性，重缩放无效。

Conclusion: 在该设置下，离线表示对齐不足以实现有用的因果通信，即激活桥通道无效。

中文摘要：最近的研究表明，语言模型可以在训练过程中通过生成数据中的隐藏信号传递行为特征。我们探究另一种激活介导的通道是否可行：一个语言模型能否在推理时通过事后线性激活桥（而非文本或结构化令牌中继）将有用的中间推理状态传递给另一个语言模型？我们在受控的Pythia-160M到Pythia-410M多跳推理设置中测试这一问题。线性翻译层学习了一个发送方和接收方隐藏状态之间的强归一化空间映射，各随机种子下的归一化余弦相似度接近0.97。然而，当翻译后的激活在推理时注入接收方时，它们并未改善下游回答。低强度加法注入仍接近无注入基线，置信区间跨越零。替换式注入始终具有破坏性，将翻译向量重新缩放到接收方隐藏状态范数也无法挽救性能。因此，这是一个有范围的负面结果：在此设置中，离线表示对齐不足以在接收方内部实现有用的因果通信。

Original abstract: Recent work shows that language models can transmit behavioural traits through hidden signals in generated data during training. We ask whether a different activation-mediated channel is viable: can one language model communicate a useful intermediate reasoning state to another at inference time through a post-hoc linear activation bridge, rather than through a textual or structured-token relay? We test this question in a controlled Pythia-160M to Pythia-410M multi-hop reasoning setting. A linear translation layer learns a strong normalized-space map between sender and receiver hidden states, with normalized cosine similarity near 0.97 across seeds. However, when the translated activations are injected into the receiver at inference time, they do not improve downstream answering. Low-strength additive injection remains near the no-injection baseline, with confidence intervals that cross zero. Replacement-style injection is consistently destructive, and rescaling translated vectors to the receiver hidden-state norm does not rescue performance. The result is therefore a scoped negative result: in this setting, offline representational alignment is not sufficient for useful causal communication inside the receiver.

</details>


### [34] [LEAP: Supercharging LLMs for Formal Mathematics with Agentic Frameworks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03303v2)
*Po-Nien Kung,Linfeng Song,Dawsen Hwang,Jinsung Yoon,Chun-Liang Li,Simone Severini,Mirek Olšák,Edward Lockhart,Quoc V Le,Burak Gokturk,Thang Luong,Tomas Pfister,Nanyun Peng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出了一个用于形式定理证明的agentic框架，包含分解和自改进，可迁移到coding agent的规划与验证。

TL;DR: 提出了LEAP框架，利用基础模型的非形式化推理、指令遵循和迭代自我改进能力，通过问题分解和与Lean编译器交互，在自动化形式定理证明中达到最先进性能，并在新基准和普特南竞赛上取得突破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLMs在形式化证明中表现不佳，需要一种能发挥其非形式化推理能力的框架，并引入更严格、尚未饱和的基准以推动进展。

Method: LEAP是一个智能体框架，将复杂问题分解为子问题，通过持续与Lean编译器交互，将非形式化蓝图转化为可验证的形式证明，并引入Lean-IMO-Bench作为评估基准。

Result: 在2025年普特南竞赛中解决所有12个问题；在Lean-IMO-Bench上将通用LLMs的一次性解决率从低于10%提升至70%，超越金牌水平IMO系统的48%；成功形式化开放组合学挑战中的关键子问题。

Conclusion: LEAP证明了通用基础模型在自动形式定理证明中的巨大潜力，能够达到甚至超越专门系统，并具备研究级实用性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）展现出强大的非形式化数学推理能力，但在生成像Lean这样的形式语言中的机器可验证证明方面存在困难。我们提出了LEAP，一个智能体框架，使通用基础模型能够在自动化形式定理证明中达到最先进的性能。LEAP利用基础模型的能力，如非形式化推理、指令遵循和迭代自我改进。通过将复杂问题分解为更小的单元，该系统通过持续与Lean编译器交互，将形式证明构建与非形式化蓝图联系起来。为了在日益饱和的基准测试之外提供严格的评估，我们引入了Lean-IMO-Bench，一个用Lean形式化的IMO风格问题基准，其陈述简短但证明非例行且多步骤，涵盖广泛的难度级别。实验上，在最近2025年普特南竞赛（一项面向北美本科生的年度数学竞赛）中，LEAP解决了所有12个问题，与前沿形式化数学模型的最新突破相当。在Lean-IMO-Bench上，LEAP将通用LLMs的一次性形式化解决率从低于10%提升到70%，显著超过了专门的金牌水平IMO系统设定的48%基准。此外，我们通过自主形式化开放组合学挑战的复杂证明，包括克努特偶阶凯莱图哈密顿分解中一个关键子问题的验证证明，展示了LEAP的研究级别实用性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) exhibit strong informal mathematical reasoning but struggle to generate mechanically verifiable proofs in formal languages like Lean. We present LEAP, an agentic framework that enables general-purpose foundation models to achieve state-of-the-art performance on automated formal theorem proving. LEAP leverages foundation model capabilities, such as informal reasoning, instruction following, and iterative self-refinement. By decomposing complex problems into smaller units, the system bridges formal proof construction with informal blueprints through continuous interaction with the Lean compiler. To provide a rigorous evaluation beyond increasingly saturated benchmarks, we introduce Lean-IMO-Bench, a benchmark of IMO-style problems formalized in Lean, with short statements yet highly non-routine and multi-step proofs across a wide range of difficulty levels. Empirically, on the latest 2025 Putnam Competition, an annual mathematics competition for undergraduate students in North America, LEAP solves all 12 problems, matching recent breakthroughs by frontier formal mathematical models. On Lean-IMO-Bench, LEAP boosts the one-shot formal solve rate of general-purpose LLMs from below 10% to 70%, notably surpassing the 48% benchmark set by a specialized, gold-medal-caliber IMO system. Furthermore, we demonstrate LEAP's research-level utility by autonomously formalizing complex proofs for open combinatorial challenges, including a verified proof for a key subproblem in Knuth's Hamiltonian decomposition of even-order Cayley graphs.

### [35] [InfoMem: Training Long-Context Memory Agents with Answer-Conditioned Information Gain](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03329v1)
*Tiancheng Han,Yong Li,Wuzhou Yu,Qiaosheng Zhang,Wenqi Shao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出训练长上下文记忆agent的方法（InfoMem），使用信息增益奖励，对agent记忆机制有直接启发。

TL;DR: 提出InfoMem奖励机制，通过评估最终记忆对答案的对数似然提升来训练分块记忆代理，显著提升长上下文任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL代理的奖励信号（稀疏最终奖励或词法中间奖励）不能直接评估最终记忆是否支持真实答案，导致记忆优化不充分。

Method: InfoMem使用答案条件信息衡量最终记忆增加模型对真实答案逐词对数似然的程度，仅应用于成功轨迹并在奖励组合前归一化以稳定RL优化。

Result: 在相同GRPO框架和训练预算下，InfoMem在长上下文记忆代理性能上优于可比基线。

Conclusion: 有效的最终记忆奖励应作用于成功轨迹、归一化并以答案为条件，而非查询。

中文摘要：长上下文任务要求LLM识别并保留与答案相关的大上下文信息。分块记忆代理通过顺序读取文档块、更新紧凑记忆并从累积记忆生成最终答案来解决这一问题。然而，现有的基于RL的分块代理要么依赖稀疏的最终答案奖励，要么使用词法中间奖励来监督记忆和检索动作。这些信号监督任务成功或局部重叠，但不直接评估最终记忆是否支持真实答案。我们提出InfoMem，一种用于训练分块记忆代理的奖励机制，该机制使用答案条件信息评估最终记忆的效用。InfoMem衡量最终记忆增加模型对真实答案的逐词对数似然的程度。为稳定RL优化，InfoMem仅将该信号应用于成功轨迹并在奖励组合前对其进行归一化。在相同的GRPO框架和训练预算下，InfoMem在长上下文记忆代理性能上优于可比的记忆代理RL基线。分析表明，有效的最终记忆奖励应作用于成功轨迹，在奖励组合前归一化，并以答案而非查询为条件。我们的代码位于https://github.com/GenSouKa1/InfoMem。

Original abstract: Long-context tasks require LLMs to identify and preserve answer-relevant information from large contexts. Chunk-wise memory agents address this issue by sequentially reading document chunks, updating a compact memory, and generating the final answer from the accumulated memory. However, existing RL-based chunk-wise agents either rely on sparse final-answer rewards or use lexical intermediate rewards for memory and retrieval actions. These signals supervise task success or local overlap, but do not directly evaluate whether the final memory supports the ground-truth answer. We propose InfoMem, a reward mechanism for training chunk-wise memory agents that evaluates final-memory utility using answer-conditioned information. InfoMem measures how much the final memory increases the model's per-token log-likelihood of the ground-truth answer. To stabilize RL optimization, InfoMem applies this signal only to successful trajectories and normalizes it before reward composition. Under the same GRPO framework and training budget, InfoMem improves long-context memory-agent performance over comparable memory-agent RL baselines. Analyses show that effective final-memory rewards should operate on successful trajectories, be normalized before reward composition, and be conditioned on the answer rather than the query. Our code is available at https://github.com/GenSouKa1/InfoMem.

</details>


### [36] [CP-Agent: Context-Aware Multimodal Reasoning for Cellular Morphological Profiling under Chemical Perturbations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03435v1)
*Yuxin Zhang,Yiyao Li,Ping Shu Ho,Simon See,Zhenqin Wu,Kevin Tsia*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Cell Painting工作流缓慢、成本高且难以解释，且药物筛选建模忽略实验上下文，限制了泛化能力和机制分辨率。

Method: CP-Agent利用CP-CLIP模块联合嵌入高内涵图像和实验元数据，实现鲁棒处理与机制判别，再结合智能工具使用和推理生成结构化报告。

Result: CP-CLIP在治疗和机制判别上达到最大F1分数0.896，CP-Agent通过结构化报告指导实验设计与假设优化。

Conclusion: CP-Agent通过更可解释、可扩展和上下文感知的表型筛选，有望加速药物发现中的假设生成迭代循环。

中文摘要：Cell Painting结合了多重荧光染色、高内涵成像和定量分析，生成高维表型读数，以支持多种下游任务，如作用机制推断、毒性预测和药物-疾病图谱构建。然而，现有工作流程缓慢、成本高且难以解释。药物筛选建模方法主要集中在分子表征学习上，而忽略了实际实验背景（如细胞系、给药方案等），限制了泛化能力和机制分辨率。我们提出了CP-Agent，一种能够为药物扰动下的细胞形态变化生成机制相关、人类可解释理由的智能多模态大语言模型。其核心是利用一个上下文感知对齐模块CP-CLIP，该模块联合嵌入高内涵图像和实验元数据，以实现稳健的处理和机制判别（最大F1分数达到0.896）。通过将CP-CLIP输出与智能工具使用和推理相结合，CP-Agent将理由编译成结构化报告，以指导实验设计和假设优化。这些能力凸显了CP-Agent在加速药物发现方面的潜力，通过实现更可解释、可扩展和上下文感知的表型筛选，简化药物发现中的假设生成迭代循环。

Original abstract: Cell Painting combines multiplexed fluorescent staining, high-content imaging, and quantitative analysis to generate high-dimensional phenotypic readouts to support diverse downstream tasks such as mechanism-of-action (MoA) inference, toxicity prediction, and construction of drug-disease atlases. However, existing workflows are slow, costly and difficult to interpret. Approaches for drug screening modeling predominantly focus on molecular representation learning, while neglecting actual experimental context (e.g., cell line, dosing schedule, etc.), limiting generalization and MoA resolution. We introduce CP-Agent, an agentic multimodal large language model (MLLM) capable of generating mechanism-relevant, human-interpretable rationales for cell morphological changes under drug perturbations. At its core, CP-Agent leverages a context-aware alignment module, CP-CLIP, that jointly embeds high-content images and experimental metadata to enable robust treatment and MoA discrimination (achieving a maximum F1-score of 0.896). By integrating CP-CLIP outputs with agentic tool usage and reasoning, CP-Agent compiles rationales into a structured report to guide experimental design and hypothesis refinement. These capabilities highlight CP-Agent's potential to accelerate drug discovery by enabling more interpretable, scalable, and context-aware phenotypic screening -- streamlining iterative cycles of hypothesis generation in drug discovery.

### [37] [What Makes Interaction Trajectories Effective for Training Terminal Agents?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03461v1)
*Sidi Yang,Chaofan Tao,Jierun Chen,Tiezheng Yu,Ruoyu Wang,Yuxin Jiang,Yiming Du,Wendong Xu,Jing Xiong,Taiqiang Wu,Lifeng Shang,Xiaohui Li,Ngai Wong,Haoli Bai*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Terminal-Lego流水线生成环境可验证任务，对比不同智能体轨迹的微调效果，并分析环境基础监督（EGS）的作用。

Result: 弱智能体轨迹导致更强泛化；15.3k数据达到此前30倍数据量的性能。

中文摘要：更强的代码智能体通常被认为是后训练的更好教师，然而这一假设与任务难度、工具设计和学生能力之间的关联尚未被充分厘清。我们使用Terminal-Lego（一个可扩展的流水线，将多领域现实问题转化为环境可验证的智能体任务）来研究这种教学联系。令人惊讶的是，独立表现并不决定教学效果：尽管Claude Opus 4.6在Terminal-Bench 2.0上取得了更高分数，但基于DeepSeek-V3.2（一个得分较低的智能体）的轨迹进行微调的学生，展现出显著更强的泛化能力。我们将这种“教学悖论”归因于环境基础监督（EGS）：通过工具可见的交互明确展示“检查-行动-验证”行为的轨迹，使学生能够内化稳健的问题解决流程，而非脆弱的动作序列。规模分析揭示了卓越的数据效率：例如，仅使用15.3k条Terminal-Lego轨迹，Qwen3-32B就在Terminal-Bench 2.0上取得了24.3%的分数，与先前使用30倍以上数据量达到的最优性能相媲美。我们的结果表明，智能体后训练的前沿超越了单纯的结果匹配，将焦点转向“工具工程”，其中环境基础交互结构的系统设计成为可复现且可泛化的智能体智能的主要催化剂。

Original abstract: Stronger code agents are commonly assumed to be superior teachers for post-training, yet this assumption remains poorly disentangled from task difficulty, harness design, and student capacity. We investigate this pedagogical link using Terminal-Lego, a scalable pipeline that transforms multi-domain real-world issues into environment-verified agentic tasks. Surprisingly, standalone performance does not dictate teaching efficacy: while Claude Opus 4.6 achieves higher scores on Terminal-Bench 2.0, students fine-tuned on trajectories from DeepSeek-V3.2, a lower-scoring agent, exhibit significantly stronger generalization. We attribute this "pedagogical paradox" to Environment-Grounded Supervision (EGS): trajectories that explicitly expose inspect-act-verify behaviors through harness-visible interactions allow students to internalize robust problem-solving routines rather than fragile action sequences. Scaling analysis reveals exceptional data efficiency: with only 15.3k Terminal-Lego trajectories, for example, Qwen3-32B achieves a 24.3% score on Terminal-Bench 2.0, rivaling previous SOTA performance established with over 30x the data volume. Our results suggest that the frontier of agent post-training lies beyond mere outcome-matching, shifting the focus toward "Harness Engineering", where the systematic design of environment-grounded interaction structures serves as the primary catalyst for reproducible and generalizable agentic intelligence.

### [38] [DMF: A Deterministic Memory Framework for Conversational AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03463v1)
*Matteo Stabile,Enrico Zimuel*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 确定性记忆框架，通用agent记忆方法，可迁移

TL;DR: DMF是一种确定性记忆框架，通过经典NLP和数学评分消除LLM调用，在零标记成本下达到与Mem0相当的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的摘要方法存在非确定性、高标记成本和剪枝决策不透明的问题，需要一种确定性、低成本且可扩展的记忆管理方法。

Method: DMF采用CPU优先的全确定性管道，为每个交互计算生存分数Ω，结合内容信号和对话线索，并使用交互计数衰减律Ω_eff(Δn)控制相关性演变。

Result: 在LoCoMo和LongMemEval数据集上，DMF与Mem0准确率相当，但使用零标记准备记忆上下文，整段对话中标记减少5到242倍。

Conclusion: 可以消除LLM调用，将标记成本降至几乎为零，实现用于对话式AI代理的确定性记忆系统。

中文摘要：对话式AI代理需要可扩展且语义连贯的记忆系统以处理长时间交互。现有方法主要依赖基于大语言模型（LLM）的写入时摘要，引入了非确定性、不断增加的标记成本以及剪枝决策的不透明性。我们提出了确定性记忆框架（DMF），一种CPU优先的方法，用完全确定性的管道替代生成式记忆压缩，该管道基于经典NLP分析、向量几何和数学评分。DMF为每次对话交互分配一个生存分数Ω，该分数由确定性内容信号、对话线索和结构化来源通过逻辑投影计算得出。交互计数衰减律，记为Ω_eff(Δn)，控制相关性随着新轮次的到来而演变，其中Δn是较新交互的数量而非实际时间，从而保持完全确定性。我们介绍了DMF的数学公式、结构化召回管道、剪枝决策程序以及评估协议。实验在专为LoCoMo和LongMemEval数据集构建的基准上进行。我们将DMF与Mem0（一种流行的AI代理记忆层）进行比较。DMF在零标记准备记忆上下文的情况下实现了相当的准确率，并且在整段对话中使用的标记数量减少了5到242倍。这些结果表明，从记忆管理循环中消除LLM调用是可能的，从而将标记成本降至几乎为零，并为对话式AI代理启用确定性记忆系统。

Original abstract: Conversational AI agents require memory systems that are both scalable and semantically coherent across long interaction horizons. Existing approaches rely predominantly on large language model (LLM)-based summarisation at write time, which introduces non-determinism, escalating token costs, and opacity in pruning decisions. We present the Deterministic Memory Framework (DMF), a CPU-first approach that replaces generative memory compression with a fully deterministic pipeline grounded in classical NLP analysis, vector geometry, and mathematical scoring. DMF assigns each conversational interaction a Survival Score $Ω$ computed from deterministic content signals, conversational cues, and structured provenance, combined through a logistic projection. An interaction-count decay law, denoted as $Ω_{\mathrm{eff}}(Δn)$, governs how relevance evolves as new turns arrive, where $Δn$ is the number of newer interactions rather than wall-clock time, preserving full determinism. We present the mathematical formulation of DMF, its structured recall pipeline, the pruning decision procedure, and the evaluation protocol. Experiments are conducted on a purpose-built benchmark using the LoCoMo and LongMemEval datasets. We compare DMF against Mem0, a popular memory layer for AI agents. DMF achieves comparable accuracy while using zero tokens to prepare the memory context and 5x to 242x fewer tokens over the entire conversation. These results show that it is possible to eliminate LLM calls from the memory-management loop, reducing token costs to nearly zero and enabling deterministic memory systems for conversational AI agents.

### [39] [StepFinder: A Temporal Semantic Framework for Failure Attribution in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03467v1)
*Taiyu Zhu,Yifan Wu,Weilin Jin,Ying Li,Gang Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多Agent系统故障归因框架，涉及协作与错误追溯，对Agent可靠性设计有启发。

TL;DR: StepFinder通过仅在特征构建阶段使用LLM编码日志，并结合时间建模和注意力模块，实现了高效准确的步级故障归因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有故障归因方法依赖LLM对原始执行轨迹进行推理，成本高、延迟大，且受冗余和噪声日志干扰，难以准确识别根本原因。

Method: StepFinder在特征构建阶段使用LLM将执行日志编码为时间语义序列，然后应用参数高效的时间建模和注意力模块捕捉序列演化和跨步依赖，最后通过多尺度差异和位置偏差细化步级错误分数。

Result: 在Who&When基准上，StepFinder在步级故障归因上优于基于LLM的方法，推理时间减少79%，无文本生成开销。

Conclusion: StepFinder是一种轻量级、高效的故障归因框架，能准确识别根因步骤并大幅提升推理效率。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统在复杂的多步任务中展现出显著的协作能力。然而，这些系统对单步执行错误高度敏感，错误会通过智能体间的交互传播并导致级联故障。为了理解故障原因并提高系统可靠性，故障归因被引入为一个任务，旨在自动识别导致故障的根本原因步骤。现有的故障归因方法主要依赖LLM对原始执行轨迹进行推理，这不仅会产生高昂的推理成本和延迟，还会受到冗余和嘈杂的执行日志的干扰，导致LLM难以准确识别真正的根本原因步骤。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了StepFinder，一个轻量级的故障归因框架。我们仅在特征构建阶段使用LLM，将执行日志编码为时间语义序列。随后，应用参数高效的时间建模和注意力模块组合来捕捉轨迹的顺序演化和跨步依赖。最后，通过多尺度差异和位置偏差细化步级错误分数，实现精确的根本原因识别。在Who&When基准上的实验结果表明，StepFinder在步级故障归因上优于基于LLM的方法，同时实现了更高的推理效率，与最快的基于LLM的方法相比，推理时间减少了79%，且没有文本生成开销。我们的代码可在https://github.com/taiyu-zhu/StepFinder获取。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems exhibit remarkable collaborative capabilities in complex multi-step tasks. However, these systems are highly sensitive to single-step execution errors that can propagate through agent interactions and lead to cascading failures. To understand the causes of failure and improve system reliability, failure attribution has been introduced as a task that aims to automatically identify the root cause step responsible for a failure. Existing failure attribution methods mainly rely on LLMs to reason over original execution trajectories, which not only incur high inference costs and latency, but also suffer from interference caused by redundant and noisy execution logs, causing LLMs to struggle in accurately identifying the true root cause step. To address this, we propose StepFinder, a lightweight failure attribution framework. We use LLMs solely during the feature construction phase to encode execution logs into temporal semantic sequences. Subsequently, a parameter-efficient combination of temporal modeling and attention modules is applied to capture the sequential evolution and cross-step dependencies of the trajectories. Finally, the step-level error score is refined through multi-scale differences and position bias, enabling precise root cause identification. Experimental results on the Who&When benchmark demonstrate that StepFinder outperforms LLM-based methods in step-level failure attribution while achieving substantially higher inference efficiency, reducing inference time by 79% compared with the fastest LLM-based method, with no text generation overhead. Our code is available at https://github.com/taiyu-zhu/StepFinder.

### [40] [Overlaying Governance: A Compositional Authorization Framework for Delegation and Scope in Agentic AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03518v1)
*Amjad Ibrahim,Yong Li*

TL;DR: 提出一个组合治理框架，通过引入递归委托、范围衰减等原语，为代理AI系统提供可问责的授权形式化基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有授权与委托框架（如IAM、OAuth 2.0）缺乏对代理AI中递归委托、动态范围和上下文边界的支持，无法治理自主代理的协作与任务委托。

Method: 定义了委托类型和权限问责模型，引入资源范围衰减概念，并设计了一个组合算子将代理语义覆盖到现有关系策略上。

Result: 通过形式化证明和实证评估，验证了框架在代理AI系统中提供可问责授权的有效性和实用性。

Conclusion: 该框架为代理AI提供了形式化且实用的授权基础，支持递归委托和动态范围，无需重写现有策略。

中文摘要：随着AI系统从被动模型演变为能够主动发起行动、协作和委派任务的自主主动代理，传统软件系统的边界变得模糊。传统的授权和委托框架围绕固定主体、显式请求和静态范围构建，不足以治理代理系统。代理AI需要更丰富的授权语义：代理必须能够继承和委托权限，在时间限制的授权下行动，并通过共享协议进行协调。现有的身份与访问管理（IAM）系统未能完全捕捉这种代理概念，缺乏递归委托、上下文边界和动态范围作为可执行治理原语的机制。与OAuth 2.0等访问委托标准不同，我们将委托视为合同条款，而不仅仅是基于静态令牌的同意凭证。本文提出一个组合治理框架，引入了对代理AI不可或缺的原语。我们定义了委托类型及其权限和问责影响，并引入了资源范围衰减的概念来约束代理访问范围。这些概念被表达为通用的关系定义，可以组合到现有授权域（例如金融系统）中。为了操作化这种组合，我们定义了一个组合算子，将新的代理语义（如递归委托链）覆盖到现有关系策略上，而无需重写它们。我们通过形式化证明和实证评估来证实该框架，表明它为代理AI系统中的可问责授权提供了形式化且实用的基础。

Original abstract: As AI systems evolve from passive models into autonomous active agents capable of initiating actions, collaborating, and delegating tasks, the traditional boundaries of software systems blur. Traditional authorization and delegation frameworks, built around fixed principals, explicit requests, and static scopes, are insufficient to govern agentic systems. Agentic AI demands richer authorization semantics: agents must inherit and delegate permissions, act under time-limited authority, and coordinate through shared protocols. Existing Identity and Access Management (IAM) systems fail to fully capture this notion of agency, lacking mechanisms for recursive delegation, contextual boundaries, and dynamic scoping as executable governance primitives. Unlike access delegation standards such as OAuth 2.0, we treat delegation as a contractual term rather than merely a static token-based consent credential. This paper proposes a compositional governance framework that introduces primitives indispensable for agentic AI. We define types of delegation and their permissions and accountability implications, and we introduce a notion of resource scope attenuation to bound agentic access envelopes. These concepts are expressed as general relational definitions that can be composed into existing authorization domains (e.g., financial systems). To operationalize this composition, we define a compositional operator that overlays new agentic semantics, such as recursive delegation chains, onto existing relational policies without rewriting them. We substantiate this framework through formal proofs and empirical evaluation, showing that it provides a formal yet practical foundation for accountable authorization in agentic AI systems.

### [41] [SAGE: A Quantitative Evaluation of Socialized Evolution in Agent Ecosystems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03544v1)
*Linyue Pan,Yaoming Zhu,Lin Qiu,Xuezhi Cao,Xunliang Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多Agent社交进化评估框架，研究共享经验对Agent改进的影响，通用Agent方法。

TL;DR: SAGE框架比较社交进化与自我进化，发现同伴经验能帮助停滞的代理突破，但效果取决于代理、领域和知识抽象能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我改进语言代理的研究忽略了共享经验可能带来的额外好处，需要探究何时以及如何从同伴历史中获益。

Method: 提出SAGE评估框架，在三个领域（ML研究、经济规划、多人游戏）中对比SocialEvo（共享同伴历史）和SelfEvo（仅自身历史）的进化表现。

Result: 最强代理未超越自我进化上限，但停滞的代理通过同伴经验实现突破；竞争环境中代理普遍改进而非针对对手；过滤和总结比原始日志更有效。

Conclusion: 同伴历史收益是代理特定、领域依赖的，依赖于从公共轨迹中抽象可转移知识的能力。

中文摘要：自我改进的语言代理通常在孤立环境中进行评估：代理尝试任务，接收反馈，并迭代地优化自身行为。然而，代理越来越多地与同伴一起操作，同伴的策略和结果是公开可见的。这引发了一个研究不足的问题：共享体验何时能产生仅靠自我改进无法实现的改进？我们提出了SAGE（社交代理群体进化），一个比较两种计算匹配条件的评估框架：SocialEvo，其中来自五个不同模型家族的代理共同进化，并可访问所有同伴的历史；以及SelfEvo，其中每个代理获得相同数量的任务尝试，但只能看到自己的过去，这是自我改进代理研究中的惯例。我们在三个领域实例化SAGE：开放式机器学习研究、长期经济规划和战略多人游戏，并在多个进化轮次中进行评估。我们发现群体历史并非普遍放大器：最强的代理并未超过其自我进化上限。然而，在自我改进下停滞不前的代理在拥有同伴经验时可以实现显著突破。在竞争性环境中，反事实控制显示代理是普遍改进，而不是发展针对对手的策略。在不同形式的共享历史中，过滤后的同伴轨迹和反思性总结通常优于原始日志，表明社交收益依赖于抽象而非曝光量。这些发现表明，同伴历史收益是代理特定的、领域依赖的，并且取决于从公共轨迹中抽象可转移知识的能力。

Original abstract: Self-improving language agents are typically evaluated in isolation: an agent attempts a task, receives feedback, and iteratively refines its own behavior. Yet agents increasingly operate alongside peers whose strategies and outcomes are publicly visible. This raises an under-studied question: when does shared experience produce improvements that self-improvement alone cannot achieve? We introduce SAGE (Social Agent Group Evolution),an evaluation framework that compares two compute-matched conditions: SocialEvo, where agents from five distinct model families co-evolve with access to all peers' histories; and SelfEvo, where each agent receives the same number of task attempts but sees only its own past, which is conventional in self-improving agent studies. We instantiate SAGE in three arenas: open-ended ML research, long-horizon economic planning, and strategic multiplayer play, evaluated across multiple evolutionary rounds. We find that group history is not a universal amplifier: the strongest agent does not exceed its self-evolution ceiling. However, agents that plateau under self-improvement can achieve significant breakthroughs when peer experience is available. In competitive settings, counterfactual controls reveal that agents improve generally rather than developing opponent-specific strategies. Across different forms of shared history, filtered peer traces and reflective summaries often outperform raw logs, indicating that social gains depend on abstraction rather than exposure volume. These findings reveal that peer-history gains are agent-specific, arena-dependent, and contingent on the capacity to abstract transferable knowledge from public traces.

### [42] [From Prompt to Service: An SLM-Based Agent Orchestration Gateway for AI-Driven Virtual Worlds](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03557v1)
*Louis Nisiotis,Aimilios Hadjiliasi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出SLM-based Agent Orchestration Gateway，涉及意图路由、服务编排等agent架构，可迁移至coding agent的轻量级协调。

TL;DR: 提出基于SLM的代理编排网关，通过意图路由解耦虚拟世界客户端与AI后端，在边缘硬件上实现高效AI服务编排。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚拟世界中的多模态交互需要多种AI后端服务，直接嵌入导致系统扩展性差、维护复杂且难以协调边缘和云资源。

Method: 设计SLM-based Agent Orchestration Gateway，包括边缘SLM进行意图分类、服务注册表验证路由、透明调用后端。在InterwovenXR虚拟博物馆中实现并评估。

Result: 紧凑SLM可可靠路由，微调后的小模型（<1B参数）成为低延迟路由器；分层配置（小模型路由+大模型生成）在中端边缘硬件上高效。

Conclusion: SLM能够支持虚拟世界中的实用AI服务编排，提供了可扩展、边缘支持的架构，使虚拟代理成为分布式生成式AI服务的访问点。

中文摘要：随着生成式人工智能能力的扩展，AI驱动的虚拟世界面临着日益增长的架构挑战。用户通过世界内界面以多模态方式进行交互，但他们的请求需要根本不同的AI后端模型和计算资源。将这些能力直接嵌入虚拟世界系统会降低可扩展性，使维护复杂化，并限制协调分布在边缘和云基础设施上的服务的能力。本文提出了一种基于SLM的代理编排网关，这是一种轻量级的运行时协调机制，通过意图驱动的服务路由将虚拟世界客户端与异构AI后端解耦。边缘部署的SLM对每个用户提示的语义意图进行分类，可配置的服务注册表验证并解析路由决策，然后透明地调用所选后端，从而无需修改客户端应用程序即可在虚拟世界中引入新的AI能力。该网关在InterwovenXR虚拟博物馆测试平台上实现并评估。评估结果表明，紧凑型SLM可以在边缘硬件上作为可靠的意图路由器，并且任务特定的微调可以将参数低于十亿的模型转化为实用的低延迟路由器。一种分层配置，将微调后的参数低于十亿的模型作为路由器，与较大的SLM进行对话响应生成，被证明可以在中端边缘硬件上部署，并且比将两个职责都委托给单个模型更高效。研究结果表明，SLM可以支持虚拟世界中实用的AI服务编排，这项工作为可扩展、可扩展且边缘支持的AI交互提供了一个经过评估的架构，使虚拟代理成为分布式生成式AI服务的访问点。

Original abstract: As generative AI capabilities expand, AI-driven virtual worlds face a growing architectural challenge. Users interact through in-world interfaces in multimodal ways, yet their requests demand fundamentally different AI backend models and computational resources. Embedding these capabilities directly into virtual world systems reduces extensibility, complicates maintenance, and limits the ability to coordinate services distributed across edge and cloud infrastructure. This paper presents an SLM-based Agent Orchestration Gateway, a lightweight runtime coordination mechanism that decouples a virtual world client from heterogeneous AI backends through intent-driven service routing. An edge-deployed SLM classifies the semantic intent of each user prompt, a configurable service registry validates and resolves the routing decision, and the selected backend is invoked transparently, enabling new AI capabilities to be introduced in the virtual world without modifying the client application. The gateway is implemented and evaluated within the InterwovenXR virtual museum testbed. The evaluation shows that compact SLMs can serve as reliable intent routers on edge hardware, and that task-specific fine-tuning can transform sub-billion-parameter models into practical, low-latency routers. A layered configuration pairing a fine-tuned sub billion-parameter model as router with a larger SLM for conversational response generation is shown to be deployable on mid-range edge hardware and more efficient than delegating both responsibilities to a single model. The findings show that SLMs can support practical AI service orchestration in virtual worlds and the work contributes an evaluated architecture for scalable, extensible, and edge-supported AI interaction, enabling virtual agents become access points to distributed generative AI services.

</details>


### [43] [Cross-Lingual Token Arbitrage: Optimizing Code Agent Context Windows via Local LLM Preprocessing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03618v1)
*Mehmet Utku Colak*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接优化代码agent上下文窗口的本地LLM预处理，减少token成本，对coding agent实用性强。

TL;DR: 提出了一种预检提示重写中间件，通过本地模型进行翻译和结构优化，在减少令牌消耗的同时保持编码质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有做法被动处理已膨胀的提示，效率低下；输入令牌成本是瓶颈，尤其非英语文本和对话结构导致高开销。

Method: 在开发者和云代理之间部署预检中间件，使用本地Llama 3.2模型进行跨语言翻译、结构重写和正则回滚保护，确保提示不被增大。

Result: 在OMH-Polyglot基准上，提示减少34-47%，总令牌最多减少18.8%，准确率保持或提升；消融实验证明重写阶段是关键，且优于LLMLingua-2。

Conclusion: 主动提示优化可显著降低推理成本而不牺牲编码质量。

中文摘要：AI辅助编码代理的瓶颈在于输入令牌成本。原始人类输入的两种病理导致了这种开销的大部分：非英语文本的标记化低效和对话提示的结构熵。现有方法被动地压缩已经膨胀的上下文或在失败发生后进行干预。我们引入了一种预检、边缘侧提示重写中间件，它位于开发者和云代理之间。一个本地Llama 3.2 (3B)模型执行跨语言翻译为英语、结构重写为紧凑的任务导向格式，以及正则验证的重写加回退保护，以确保优化后的提示永远不会比原始提示大。我们在OMH-Polyglot上评估，这是一个涵盖土耳其语、阿拉伯语、中文和代码切换规范的多语言编码基准。在三个商业LLM后端上，该中间件将提示令牌减少34-47%，总令牌减少高达18.8%，同时保持或提高任务准确率。消融研究表明，收益主要来自重写阶段，而不是简单的函数名称提取。与匹配压缩率的LLMLingua-2相比，我们的方法在所有评估后端上始终获得更优的OckScore性能。这些结果表明，主动提示优化可以显著降低推理成本而不牺牲编码质量。

Original abstract: AI-assisted coding agents are bottlenecked by input-token cost. Two pathologies of raw human input drive much of this overhead: tokenization inefficiency for non-English text and structural entropy in conversational prompts. Existing approaches act reactively by compressing already-bloated contexts or intervening after failures occur.
  We introduce a pre-flight, edge-side prompt-rewriting middleware that operates between the developer and the cloud agent. A local Llama 3.2 (3B) model performs cross-lingual translation into English, structural rewriting into a compact task-oriented format, and regex-validated rewrite-with-fallback safeguards to ensure the optimized prompt is never larger than the original.
  We evaluate on OMH-Polyglot, a multilingual coding benchmark spanning Turkish, Arabic, Chinese, and code-switched specifications. Across three commercial LLM backends, the middleware reduces prompt tokens by 34-47 percent and total tokens by up to 18.8 percent while preserving or improving task accuracy. Ablation studies show that gains arise primarily from the rewriting stage rather than simple function-name extraction. Compared with LLMLingua-2 at matched compression rates, our method consistently achieves superior OckScore performance across all evaluated backends. These results demonstrate that proactive prompt optimization can substantially reduce inference costs without sacrificing coding quality.

### [44] [Bridging Auxiliary Constraints to Resolve Instruction Following in Large Reasoning Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03624v1)
*Zhengyi Zhao,Shubo Zhang,Huimin Wang,Zezhong Wang,Yutian Zhao,Yefeng Zheng,Binyang Li,Yulan He,Kam-Fai Wong,Xian Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通过桥接约束改进指令遵循，对agent的约束满足有潜在启发，但偏向LLM推理。

TL;DR: CRGC通过显示建模约束关系图并利用桥梁约束，将大型推理模型的指令约束违反率降低39%，同时保持推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型难以可靠遵循多个指令约束，现有方法不能有效解决约束竞争和缺失问题。

Method: 将指令表示为约束知识图，通过约束关系图补全（CRGC）建模约束间关系，识别并引入桥梁约束以增强主要约束的兼容性。

Result: 在三个指令遵循数据集上，CRGC相比标准提示减少39%的约束违反，且不降低推理性能。

Conclusion: CRGC无需通用训练即可显著提升约束满足能力，为大型推理模型的指令遵循提供了一种有效途径。

中文摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）在许多任务中展现了令人印象深刻的能力，但在可靠地遵循多个指令方面仍存在困难，要么未能满足单个约束，要么难以同时平衡竞争约束。我们将这一挑战形式化为约束遵循问题（CAP）。本文介绍了一种新颖的框架，通过将指令表示为约束的结构化知识图来解决CAP。我们的方法，约束关系图补全（CRGC），显式建模约束之间的关系，识别遵循挑战，并发现有助于模型更好关注和协调需求的“桥梁约束”。桥梁约束作为辅助指令，使主要约束更加突出和兼容。与通过通用训练方法增强指令遵循的现有方法不同，CRGC通过利用模型自身知识创建更好的生成路径来专门改进约束满足。在三个流行的指令遵循数据集上的实验表明，与标准提示相比，我们的方法在保持大型推理模型推理能力的同时，将约束违反减少了39%。

Original abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have demonstrated impressive capabilities in many tasks, yet they struggle with reliably following multiple instructions, either by failing to satisfy individual constraints or by struggling to balance competing constraints simultaneously. We formalize this challenge as the Constraint Adherence Problem (CAP). This paper introduces a novel framework that addresses CAP by representing instructions as a structured knowledge graph of constraints. Our approach, Constraint Relationship Graph Completion (CRGC), explicitly models relationships between constraints, identifies adherence challenges, and discovers ``bridge constraints'' that help the model better focus on and reconcile requirements. Bridge constraints act as auxiliary instructions that make primary constraints more salient and compatible. Unlike existing approaches that enhance instruction following through general training methods, CRGC specifically improves constraint satisfaction by leveraging the model's own knowledge to create better pathways for generation. Experiments across three popular instruction following datasets demonstrate that our approach reduces constraint violations by 39% compared to standard prompting while maintaining reasoning abilities of large reasoning models.

### [45] [TSQAgent: Rating Time Series Data Quality via Dedicated Agentic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03629v1)
*Shunyu Wu,Dan Li,Haozheng Ye,Weibin Feng,Jian Lou,Bo Zhang,Wenjie Feng,Chenjuan Guo,See-Kiong Ng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多角色agent框架用于时间序列质量评估，含推理工具与工作流，可迁移至coding agent的精细评估。

TL;DR: 提出TSQBench基准和TSQAgent框架，提升LLMs在时间序列质量评估中的维度识别和定量比较能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based TS质量评估方法依赖人工预定义维度和纯文本推理，无法自动识别相关维度或进行定量比较。

Method: 构建TSQBench基准评估LLM的两种能力；提出TSQAgent框架，包含Perceiver、Inspector、Adjudicator三个角色，并引入智能体推理策略和外部分析工具。

Result: 在TSQBench和11个真实数据集上，TSQAgent显著提升了质量理解和定量比较能力，并改善了质量感知的数据选择。

Conclusion: TSQAgent框架有效克服了LLM在维度识别和定量比较上的局限，并能提升下游性能和数据效率。

中文摘要：评估时间序列（TS）数据的质量是基础但极具挑战性的，因为质量维度具有多面性。最近，大语言模型（LLMs）通过成对比较和逐维度评估成为TS质量评估的一种有前景的范式。然而，现有方法依赖于人工预定义的质量维度和纯文本推理，尚不清楚LLMs能否识别真正相关的质量维度或进行基于证据的定量质量比较。为此，我们构建了TSQBench，这是一个专用基准，用于评估LLMs在两种渐进能力上的表现：（i）理解和识别相关质量维度，（ii）在特定维度下进行质量比较。我们的分析表明，当前LLMs在维度识别和基于证据的质量比较方面始终存在困难。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了TSQAgent，一种新型的TS质量评分的智能体推理框架，包含三个协作角色：感知器（Perceiver）用于聚焦维度选择，检查器（Inspector）用于逐维度定量分析，以及裁决者（Adjudicator）用于聚合和细化最终判断。特别是，我们引入了一种智能体推理策略，灌输识别和优先考虑最相关质量维度的能力，并进一步提出一个配备外部分析工具的智能体工作流，以在选定维度上进行精确的定量比较。在提出的基准和11个真实世界数据集上的实验表明，我们的框架不仅显著提高了LLMs在质量理解和定量比较方面的能力，而且有效地将这些改进转化为更好的质量感知数据选择，从而提升下游性能和数据效率。

Original abstract: Assessing the quality of time series (TS) data is fundamental yet inherently challenging due to the multifaceted nature of quality dimensions. Recently, large language models (LLMs) have emerged as a promising paradigm for TS quality assessment via pairwise comparison and per-dimension evaluation. However, existing approaches rely on manually predefined quality dimensions and purely text-based reasoning, leaving it unknown whether LLMs can identify truly relevant quality dimensions or perform grounded and quantitative quality comparisons. To investigate this, we construct TSQBench, a dedicated benchmark for evaluating LLMs on two progressive capabilities: (i) understanding and identifying relevant quality dimensions, and (ii) performing quality comparison under specific dimensions. Our analysis reveals that current LLMs consistently struggle with both dimension identification and evidence-grounded quality comparison. To address these limitations, we propose TSQAgent, a novel agentic reasoning framework for TS quality rating consisting of three collaborative roles: Perceiver for focused dimension selection, Inspector for dimension-wise quantitative analysis, and Adjudicator that aggregates and refines the final judgment. In particular, we introduce an agentic reasoning strategy that instills the ability to identify and prioritize the most relevant quality dimensions, and further propose an agent workflow equipped with external analytical tools to enable precise quantitative comparisons over selected dimensions. Experiments on both the proposed benchmark and eleven real-world datasets demonstrate that our framework not only substantially improves LLMs' capabilities in quality understanding and quantitative comparison but also effectively translates these improvements into better quality-aware data selection, leading to enhanced downstream performance and data efficiency.

### [46] [Diagnosing Knowledge Gaps in LLM Tool Use: An Agentic Benchmark for Novel API Acquisition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03657v1)
*Jinnuo Liu,Yue Peng,Jinhan Niu,Hongyi Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 构建agent基准诊断LLM工具使用中的知识差距，直接涉及agent的API获取与评测。

TL;DR: 提出NovelAPIBench动态基准，发现知识组件不可互换，检索与微调互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有新API基准静态、依赖粗粒度指标或使用合成API，无法真实反映库演化，需要更全面评估。

Method: 构建自动动态基准NovelAPIBench，发现新API、分解知识包、生成任务并分类失败样本，比较检索与参数适应。

Result: 使用示例是最强独立信号；最佳两组件依赖领域；添加上下文可能有害；微调不能替代检索但教授包的使用。

Conclusion: 检索和调优互补：检索提供API内容，调优改进程序性整合。

中文摘要：用于代码生成的大型语言模型通常需要使用预训练数据中未出现的API。这不仅需要回忆函数名称：模型还必须协调签名、模块路径、输入输出契约、语义和可执行的使用模式。现有的新API基准通常是静态的，依赖粗略的通过/失败指标，或使用可能无法反映真实库演化的合成API。我们引入了NovelAPIBench，这是一个全自动的动态基准，对于任何基础模型和目标库，它能够发现新API，提取分解的知识包，生成可执行的编码任务，并将失败的样本分配到六个诊断类别。在大约1.9K个任务、四个基础模型和五个领域中，我们比较了通过检索注入的知识与通过参数适应内化的知识。我们发现知识组件不可互换：使用示例是最强的独立信号，而最佳的两组件设置将签名与机制或示例配对，具体取决于领域和主干。添加更多上下文，尤其是源代码，可能会通过增加导入路径错误而损害性能。一旦外部知识被移除，参数适应也不能替代检索；相反，微调主要教会模型如何使用提供的包，并且这种能力可以转移到未见的库。这些结果表明，检索和调优发挥着互补的作用：检索提供易变的API内容，而调优改进程序性整合。

Original abstract: Large language models for code generation often need to use APIs that are absent from their pretraining data. This requires more than recalling a function name: models must coordinate signatures, module paths, input-output contracts, semantics, and executable usage patterns. Existing novel-API benchmarks are typically static, rely on coarse pass/fail metrics, or use synthetic APIs that may not reflect real library evolution. We introduce NovelAPIBench, a fully automated dynamic benchmark that, for any base model and target library, discovers novel APIs, extracts decomposed knowledge bundles, generates executable coding tasks, and assigns failed samples to six diagnostic categories. Across about 1.9K tasks, four base models, and five domains, we compare knowledge injected through retrieval with knowledge internalized through parametric adaptation. We find that knowledge components are not interchangeable: usage examples are the strongest standalone signal, while the best two-component setting pairs signatures with either mechanisms or examples depending on the domain and backbone. Adding more context, especially source code, can hurt by increasing import-path errors. Parametric adaptation also does not replace retrieval once external knowledge is removed; rather, fine-tuning mainly teaches models how to use provided bundles, and this ability transfers to held-out libraries. These results suggest that retrieval and tuning play complementary roles: retrieval supplies volatile API content, while tuning improves procedural integration.

</details>


### [47] [From Answers to States: Verifiable Process-Level Evaluation of Chemical Reasoning in Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03660v2)
*Hongyu Guo,Hao Li,He Cao,Gongbo Zhang,Li Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出可验证的过程级化学推理评估方法，其模板化可验证思路可迁移至agent轨迹评估。

TL;DR: 提出ChemCoTBench-V2，一个规则可验证的化学推理基准，通过确定性规则检查中间步骤，揭示模型在最终答案正确性与推理逻辑一致性之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有化学基准只评估最终答案，忽略推理过程中的化学逻辑错误；过程级评估器成本高、不一致且易幻觉。

Method: 构建基于专家模板的结构化推理轨迹，用确定性化学规则（及参考轨迹）检查中间步骤，报告最终答案、模板遵循度和步骤验证正确性三个信号。

Result: 前沿模型在最终答案成功与结构化推理状态一致性之间存在显著差距，如格式正确但化学步骤错误，或答案正确但推理薄弱。

Conclusion: ChemCoTBench-V2提供了低成本、可审计的细粒度评估，能定位具体违反验证器的步骤，推动可靠化学推理模型的发展。

中文摘要：大语言模型越来越多地被用作化学助手，然而大多数化学基准仍然只对最终答案进行评分。这掩盖了一个关键的失败模式：模型可能输出正确的分子、产物或选项，但其推理过程违反了化学逻辑。现有的过程级评估器难以扩展，因为LLM评判者和人类步骤级过程标注成本高、不一致且容易产生幻觉。我们提出了ChemCoTBench-V2，一个规则可验证的诊断基准，用于低成本、可审计的结构化、可验证的化学推理轨迹评估。它涵盖分子理解、分子编辑、分子优化和反应预测，包含18个报告任务的5,620个评估样本。模型必须在专家设计的模板中暴露关键的中间步骤，这些步骤通过确定性化学规则进行检查，对于闭式答案任务，还使用参考轨迹而非另一个LLM评判者。开放式分子优化通过预言机可验证的状态约束进行评估，而非严格的轨迹匹配。该基准报告三个独立的信号：最终答案正确性、模板遵循度以及经过专家精炼的中间承诺上的逐步验证器正确性。在前沿模型上的实验揭示了最终答案成功与结构化推理状态一致性之间的持续差距：模型通常遵循要求的格式但未能通过化学步骤检查，或者正确回答但支持性推理薄弱。ChemCoTBench-V2支持细粒度模型比较，并识别轨迹首次违反验证器的具体步骤。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly used as chemistry assistants, yet most chemistry benchmarks still score only final answers. This masks a critical failure mode: a model may output the correct molecule, product, or option while its reasoning violates chemical logic. Existing process-level evaluators are hard to scale because LLM judges and human step-level process annotation are costly, inconsistent, and vulnerable to hallucination. We introduce ChemCoTBench-V2, a rule-verifiable diagnostic benchmark for low-cost, auditable evaluation of structured, verifier-addressable chemical reasoning traces. It spans molecular understanding, molecule editing, molecular optimization, and reaction prediction, with 5,620 evaluation samples across 18 reporting tasks. Models must expose key intermediate steps in expert-designed templates, and those steps are checked with deterministic chemistry rules and, for closed-answer tasks, reference traces rather than another LLM judge. Open-ended molecular optimization is evaluated with oracle-verifiable state constraints rather than strict trace matching. The benchmark reports three separate signals: final-answer correctness, template adherence, and step-wise verifier correctness over expert-refined intermediate commitments. Experiments on frontier models reveal a persistent gap between final-answer success and structured-reasoning-state consistency: models often follow the requested format while failing chemical-step checks, or answer correctly with weak supporting reasoning. ChemCoTBench-V2 enables fine-grained model comparison and identifies the concrete step at which the trace first violates the verifier.

</details>


### [48] [EvoDrive: Pareto Evolution for Safety-Critical Autonomous Driving via Self-Improving LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03678v1)
*Tong Nie,Yuewen Mei,Yihong Tang,Junlin He,Jie Deng,Jian Sun,Wei Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自改进LLM agent框架用于安全关键场景生成，包含记忆、多目标优化、actor-critic架构，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: EvoDrive是一个基于LLM的智能体演化框架，用于自动驾驶多目标安全关键场景生成，通过模拟器基础和帕累托档案优化攻击性与真实性的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖手工启发式，限制在已知先验中，而开放式的智能体演化缺乏模拟器基础且易将多目标退化为单目标。

Method: 采用模拟器基础的演员-评论家架构：记忆驱动演员迭代改进，评论家过滤不可行候选，自演化世界评估器路由方案，并维护帕累托档案。

中文摘要：生成安全关键场景对于验证和改进自动驾驶系统至关重要，但它本质上要求最大化对抗性以暴露故障，同时保持真实性。现有方法通常通过手工设计的启发式方法来管理这种权衡，将生成限制在已知的先验知识中，并忽略了未充分探索的模式。虽然最近开放的基于智能体的演化可以突破这一限制，但不受约束的通用智能体缺乏严格的模拟器基础，并且倾向于将多目标紧张关系退化为单标量最大化。本文提出了EvoDrive，这是首个自动化的、基于LLM的智能体演化框架，用于多目标场景生成。EvoDrive采用了一种基于模拟器的演员-评论家架构，其中记忆驱动的演员迭代地提出改进方案，评论家过滤掉不可行的候选方案，而自演化的世界评估器将具有前景的方案路由到优化模拟预算。EvoDrive还维护了一个评估候选方案的帕累托档案，以保留多样化的攻击-真实性权衡，并通过模拟反馈指导未来的演化。在MetaDrive和CARLA上的基准测试结果表明，EvoDrive不仅在各种生成器上显著扩展了帕累托前沿，而且为策略训练产生了有价值的场景。

Original abstract: Generating safety-critical scenarios is essential for validating and improving autonomous driving systems, yet it inherently requires maximizing adversariality to expose failures while preserving realism. Existing methods usually manage this trade-off with handcrafted heuristics, confining generation to known priors and overlooking underexplored patterns. While recent open-ended agentic evolution can push this limit, unconstrained general agents lack strict simulator grounding and tend to collapse the multi-objective tension into single-scalar maximization. Here we present EvoDrive, the first automated, LLM-based agentic evolution framework for multi-objective scenario generation. EvoDrive employs a simulator-grounded actor-critic architecture where a memory-driven actor iteratively proposes improvements to the generators and critics filter out implausible candidates, and a self-evolving world evaluator routes promising proposals to optimize simulation budgets. EvoDrive further maintains a Pareto archive of evaluated candidates to preserve diverse attack-realism trade-offs and guide future evolution via simulation feedback. Benchmark results on MetaDrive and CARLA show that EvoDrive not only significantly expands the Pareto frontier across various generators, but also produces valuable scenarios for policy training.

Original abstract: Recent AI agents can flexibly invoke skills to solve complex tasks, but their long-term improvement is fundamentally constrained by a lack of systematic skill construction, accumulation, and transfer. To address this limitation, we propose SkillPyramid, a skill consolidation framework that reuses existing skill experience for broader task generalization. Operating on a hierarchical skill topology, SkillPyramid further introduces a self-evolution mechanism that enables agents to compose, validate, and incorporate new skills during task execution. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and ScienceWorld across four backbone models show that SkillPyramid substantially increases the average reward by 38.0% and reduces execution steps by 27.7%. Overall, our method transforms a skill collection from a static resource pool into a dynamic evolution system.

### [50] [DiBS: Diffusion-Informed Branch Selection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06518v1)
*Bo Liu,Yuan Xie,Yuan Gao,Xiaolong Luo,Peng Ye,Tao Chen,Fujun Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 扩散模型引导的搜索分支选择，方法可迁移至agent的搜索与规划。

TL;DR: 提出DiBS，一种结合扩散模型与符号求解器的方法，通过扩散模型指导分支选择，显著降低数独求解的搜索成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学习求解器缺乏正确性保证，符号求解器易陷入长尾搜索，需要结合两者优点的方法。

Method: DiBS保持符号求解器完备，使用扩散模型对候选值排序，结合轻量级一致性信号进行分支选择。

Result: 在Royle 17-clue基准上，DiBS在节点数、回溯次数和长尾百分位数上显著优于强启发式基线。

Conclusion: DiBS证明了学习到的全局指导在困难数独实例上的有效性，降低了搜索成本。

中文摘要：数独是一个典型的约束满足问题，需要严格的离散约束下的全局结构性推理。现有解决数独的工作主要集中在两种主流方法上，即传统启发式和深度学习求解器。然而，它们存在两个互补的局限性：基于学习的求解器缺乏硬正确性保证，而完全符号求解器仍然容易陷入长尾搜索。为了解决这些缺点，我们提出了一种新颖的扩散模型引导方法，称为DiBS，用于分支选择搜索过程。具体来说，DiBS保持符号求解器的完备性，并使用扩散模型作为分支排序指导。核心方法是在当前部分赋值和轻量级一致性信号下对候选值进行排序。此外，我们提供了深入的理论证明来揭示它是如何工作的以及为什么有效。在具有挑战性的Royle 17线索数独基准上的实验表明，我们的DiBS相对于强启发式基线显著降低了搜索成本，特别是在节点、回溯和长尾百分位数方面。此外，这些结果证实了学习到的全局指导在分支顺序错误代价最高的困难实例上是有效的。所有代码可在https://github.com/shanxierdan/DiBS获取。

Original abstract: Sudoku is a representative constraint satisfaction problem that requires global structural reasoning under strict discrete constraints. The existing works of solving Sudoku mainly focus on two dominant approaches, i.e., traditional heuristic and deep learning solver. However, they suffer from two complementary limitations: learning-based solvers lack hard correctness guarantees, while complete symbolic solvers are still prone to long-tail search. To address these shortcomings, we propose a novel diffusion model-guided approach, termed as DiBS, for the branch selection search process. Specifically, DiBS keeps the symbolic solver complete and uses the diffusion model as a branch-ordering guide. The core method is ranking candidate values under the current partial assignment and lightweight consistency signal. Furthermore, we provide an in-depth theoretical proof to reveal how it works and why it works. Experiments on the challenging Royle 17-clue Sudoku benchmark show that our DiBS substantially reduces search cost relative to strong heuristic baselines, especially in nodes, backtracks, and long-tail percentiles. Besides, these results confirm that learned global guidance is effective on hard instances where branch-order mistakes are most expensive. All codes are available at https://github.com/shanxierdan/DiBS.

### [51] [Dynamic Objective Selection with Safeguards and LLM Oversight for Financial Decision-Making](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03704v1)
*Keigo Sakurai,Takahiro Ogawa,Miki Haseyama,Anjyu Anan,Kei Nakagawa*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 动态目标选择与LLM监督机制用于金融决策，包含安全控制与置信度门控，可启发agent的决策与安全设计。

TL;DR: 提出DOSS，一种动态目标选择器，通过分类选择优化目标，并引入置信度门控和LLM监督来减少错误切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定目标在不同市场条件下表现不佳，而制度切换方法有噪声和延迟，增加交易成本。

Method: 将目标选择作为分类问题，用滚动窗口更新，输出置信度分数；采用置信度感知门控和故障安全机制，并用LLM作为监督组件进行覆盖。

Result: 提供了一种稳健的动态目标选择方法，减少错误选择和过度切换。

Conclusion: DOSS能有效选择目标函数，提升性能并降低操作风险。

中文摘要：金融决策任务，如股票推荐和投资组合配置，通常估计未来收益和风险，然后为投资者选择交易或配置，而选择的优化目标往往决定实际表现。然而，由于市场条件随时间演变，固定的目标可能在不同制度下表现不佳，而依赖潜在制度估计的制度转换管道可能嘈杂或延迟，频繁转换可能增加交易成本和操作不稳定性。在本文中，我们提出DOSS（带安全保护的动态目标选择器），一种基于学习的选择器，直接从近期回报的可解释统计摘要中在每个时间点选择与决策相关的目标函数，从一小部分候选（例如，追求收益、厌恶损失和风险调整）中选择，而不引入中间制度变量。DOSS将目标选择表述为一个关于目标的分类问题，并使用滚动窗口进行顺序更新，以进行前瞻性选择而不产生时间泄漏，同时为每个提议输出置信度分数。为了缓解部署中的错误选择和过度切换，DOSS应用了置信度感知的门控，带有故障安全机制，将低置信度的提议覆盖为保守默认值，并实施与切换频率相关的显式控制。我们进一步通过将大型语言模型（LLM）定位为监督组件而非新目标的生成器来整合治理：LLM被限制为接受提议的目标或将其覆盖为预定义的安全默认值，确定性规则约束在需要时触发覆盖。

Original abstract: Financial decision-making tasks such as stock recommendation and portfolio allocation typically estimate future return and risk and then select trades or allocations for an investor, and the chosen optimization objective often determines realized performance. However, because market conditions evolve over time, a fixed objective can be suboptimal across regimes, while regime-switching pipelines that rely on latent regime estimates can be noisy or delayed and frequent switching can increase turnover and operational instability. In this paper, we propose DOSS (Dynamic Objective Selection with Safeguards), a learning-based selector that directly chooses the decision-relevant objective function at each time point from interpretable statistical summaries of recent returns, selecting among a small set of candidates (e.g., return-seeking, loss-averse, and risk-adjusted) without introducing intermediate regime variables. DOSS formulates objective selection as a classification problem over objectives and performs sequential updates with a rolling window to make forward-looking selections without temporal leakage, while also outputting a confidence score for each proposal. To mitigate misselection and excessive switching in deployment, DOSS applies confidence-aware gating with a fail-safe that overrides low-confidence proposals to a conservative default and enforces explicit controls tied to switching frequency. We further integrate governance by positioning a Large Language Model (LLM) as an oversight component rather than a generator of new objectives: the LLM is restricted to accept a proposed objective or override it to a predefined safe default, with deterministic rule-based constraints triggering overrides when needed.

### [52] [Code-on-Graph: Iterative Programmatic Reasoning via Large Language Models on Knowledge Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03705v1)
*Weiwei Ding,Zixuan Li,Long Bai,Zhuo Chen,Kun Su,Fei Wang,Xiaolong Jin,Jin Zhang,Jiafeng Guo,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于知识图谱的代码生成推理框架，对coding agent中知识整合与程序推理有参考。

TL;DR: 提出CoG框架，通过将KG模式表示为Python类并生成可执行代码，实现灵活且可扩展的LLM-KG集成，在多个基准上超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-KG集成框架使用预定义操作符，导致不灵活和不可扩展。

Method: CoG将检索到的KG模式表示为Python类，生成基于这些类的可执行代码，将事实实例化为对象，避免直接注入大量知识。

Result: 在WebQSP、CWQ和GrailQA上，CoG超越SOTA高达10.5%。

Conclusion: CoG程序化推理框架有效解决了LLM-KG集成的灵活性和可扩展性问题。

中文摘要：知识图谱（KG）被广泛用于缓解大语言模型（LLM）的局限性，如知识过时和幻觉。现有的LLM-KG集成框架通常依赖预定义操作符从KG检索事实知识并将其注入提示中以生成答案。这种范式面临两个关键瓶颈：1）不灵活：预定义操作符范围有限，因此缺乏足够的组合表达能力来完全捕捉KG问题所需的复杂语义。2）不可扩展：将事实知识直接注入提示限制了处理大规模事实知识的可扩展性。为了解决这两个瓶颈，我们提出了CoG（Code-on-Graph），一个用于LLM-KG集成的程序化推理框架。具体来说，给定每个推理步骤检索到的事实知识，CoG首先识别相应的KG模式，并将这些模式表示为Python类，这些类作为检索到的事实的抽象接口。然后它生成基于这些类的可执行代码，在执行过程中将检索到的事实实例化为相应类的对象。这种设计实现了灵活的基于代码的推理，同时避免将大规模事实知识直接注入提示。在WebQSP、CWQ和GrailQA上的实验表明，CoG相比之前的最先进模型性能提升高达10.5%。

Original abstract: Knowledge Graphs (KGs) are widely used to mitigate the limitations of Large Language Models (LLMs), such as outdated knowledge and hallucinations. Existing LLM-KG integration frameworks typically rely on predefined operators to retrieve factual knowledge from KGs and inject it into prompts for answer generation. This paradigm faces two critical bottlenecks: 1) Inflexibility: The predefined operators are limited in scope and thus lack sufficient compositional expressiveness to fully capture the complex semantics required by KG questions. 2) Unscalability: Direct injection of factual knowledge into prompts limits scalability in handling large-scale factual knowledge. To address these two bottlenecks, we propose Code-on-Graph (CoG), a programmatic reasoning framework for LLM-KG integration. Specifically, given the factual knowledge retrieved at each reasoning step, CoG first identifies the corresponding KG schemas and represents these schemas as Python classes, which serve as abstract interfaces to the retrieved facts. It then generates executable code grounded in these classes, with the retrieved facts instantiated as objects of the corresponding classes during execution. This design enables flexible code-based reasoning while avoiding the direct injection of large-scale factual knowledge into prompts. Experiments on WebQSP, CWQ, and GrailQA demonstrate that CoG outperforms prior state-of-the-art models by up to 10.5%.

</details>


### [53] [RIZZ: Routing Interactions to Near Zero-Interference Zones for Continual Adaptation of Black-Box Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20638v1)
*Sonali Goel,Pranav Vaidhyanathan,Lucas Schorling,Natalia Ares,Maike Osborne*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 黑盒agent持续适应框架，包含记忆、路由、反馈驱动更新，直接贡献于通用agent方法。

TL;DR: RIZZ是一个通过验证器门控记忆和上下文感知路由实现低干扰持续适应的黑箱框架，在基准测试中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑箱适应方法处理非平稳输入流、稀疏反馈和任务间干扰时效果不佳，需要一种能在线适应且显式控制干扰的框架。

Method: RIZZ将输入流组织成动态内存分支，推理时通过上下文感知路由器选择或创建分支，检索多类记忆并编译成有界提示；模型输出经任务验证器评分后，仅验证通过的交互更新记忆、调整规则或创建反模式。

Result: 在竞争性基准测试中，RIZZ优于最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: RIZZ框架实现了在上下文预算下在线适应，并通过自然语言反馈持续改进，有效控制任务干扰，验证了其有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地被部署为长期存在的智能体，必须跨越用户、任务、领域、模态和反馈机制进行适应，同时无法访问模型权重。现有的黑箱适应方法通常优化单个提示词、维护无差异的记忆，或依赖重复的繁重搜索。然而，当输入流是非平稳的、反馈稀疏且一个任务族的失败会污染另一个任务族的行为时，这些设计会遇到困难。我们引入了RIZZ（路由交互至近零干扰区），这是一个用于复合语言模型系统的持续适应框架，完全通过验证器门控记忆、路由和提示词编译来学习。RIZZ将输入流组织为动态生成的内存分支。在推理时，无论在线还是离线，一个上下文感知的路由器选择或创建一个分支，该分支检索分支本地、全局、图结构和工作记忆上下文，并与检索到的任务证据一起编译成一个有界提示词。在模型行动后，任务验证器对输出进行评分，只有经过验证的交互才能更新记忆、提升可重用规则、降级有害规则或创建反模式。这产生了一个黑箱智能体，通过持续的自然语言反馈进行改进，同时明确控制干扰。RIZZ针对的是在上下文预算下必须在线适应的场景。最后，我们在竞争性基准测试中展示了我们的框架相对于最先进基线的有效性。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as long-lived agents that must adapt across users, tasks, domains, modalities, and feedback regimes without access to model weights. Existing black-box adaptation methods typically optimize a single prompt, maintain an undifferentiated memory, or rely on repeated rollout-heavy search. However, these designs struggle when streams of input are nonstationary, feedback is sparse, and failures from one task family can contaminate behavior on another. We introduce RIZZ (Routing Interactions to Near Zero-interference Zones), a continual adaptation framework for compound language-model systems that learns entirely through verifier-gated memory, routing, and prompt compilation. RIZZ organizes input streams into dynamically spawned memory branches. At inference time, either while online or offline, a context-aware router selects or creates a branch that retrieves branch-local, global, graph-structured, and working-memory context, which is compiled into a bounded prompt together with retrieved task evidence. After the model acts, task verifiers score the output, and only verified interactions can update memory, promote reusable rules, demote harmful rules, or create anti-patterns. This yields a black-box agent that improves through persistent natural-language feedback while explicitly controlling interference. RIZZ targets the regime where adaptation must occur online under context budgets. Finally, we demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework against state-of-the-art baselines on competitive benchmarks.

</details>


### [54] [When to Re-Plan: Subgoal Persistence in Hierarchical Latent Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03741v2)
*Ayushi Chadha*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究层次潜在推理中的子目标持久性，涉及长期规划与manager-worker架构，可迁移至agent规划方法。

TL;DR: 在潜在推理中，中等持续性（P≈3-6）的子目标比频繁或过长的子目标更有效，且对齐权重存在窄最优值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视距推理需要平衡稳定性与适应性，但现有方法难以在重新规划频率和承诺长度之间找到最佳点。

Method: 扩展层次推理模型（HRM），引入封建式管理者-工作者接口：高层模块周期性发出归一化方向性子目标，持续P步，通过余弦对齐损失偏置低层隐藏状态更新。

Result: 在ARC和ConceptARC上，P=3时LM损失最低（1.544），比P=1（1.674）和基线（1.640）更优；对齐权重λ≈0.05为最优；消融表明学习到的方向性结构是干扰来源。

Conclusion: 潜在推理系统的组合规划应使中等视距意图在足够多的计算步骤上保持一致，以形成组合结构。

中文摘要：长视距推理要求系统致力于中等视距意图而不变得僵化：过于频繁地重新规划会导致计算无法凝聚成多步结构；承诺时间过长则计划会过时。我们在潜在推理设置中研究这种稳定性-适应性权衡，其中多步计算发生在隐藏状态内部而非外部化的令牌轨迹。我们扩展了层次推理模型（HRM），采用封建风格的管理者-工作者接口：一个缓慢的高层模块定期发出一个归一化的方向性子目标，该子目标持续P个低层步骤，偏置工作者的隐藏状态更新并提供内在的余弦对齐损失。在ARC和ConceptARC上，我们发现子目标持续性——而非单纯子目标注入——是核心旋钮：中等周期P在[3,6]范围内始终优于非常频繁（P=1）和非常长的视距，在P=3处有明显的LM损失最小值（1.544对P=1时的1.674，基线1.640；在5个种子上重复，均值1.595，标准差0.045）。内在对齐权重lambda显示出互补的狭窄最优值（lambda约0.05）。在过去的甜蜜点lambda处进行的受控消融分离出学习到的方向性结构——而非仅架构容量或辅助损失——作为当对齐信号超过其最优值时干扰的来源。这些发现共同暗示了潜在推理系统中组合规划的设计原则：中等视距意图必须在足够多的计算步骤上保持一致，以便形成组合结构。

Original abstract: Long-horizon reasoning requires a system to commit to medium-horizon intent without becoming rigid: re-plan too often and computation never coheres into multi-step structure; commit too long and the plan goes stale. We study this stability-adaptivity tradeoff in the latent reasoning setting, where multi-step computation occurs inside hidden state rather than externalized token traces. We extend the Hierarchical Reasoning Model (HRM) with a feudal-style manager-worker interface: a slow high-level module periodically emits a normalized directional subgoal that persists for P low-level steps, biasing the worker's hidden-state updates and supplying an intrinsic cosine alignment loss. On ARC and ConceptARC, we find that subgoal persistence -- not subgoal injection alone -- is the central knob: moderate periods P in [3, 6] consistently outperform both very frequent (P=1) and very long horizons, with a clear minimum LM loss at P=3 (1.544 vs. 1.674 at P=1, 1.640 baseline; replicated over 5 seeds at mean 1.595, std 0.045). The intrinsic alignment weight lambda shows a complementary narrow optimum (lambda approximately 0.05). A controlled ablation at past-sweet-spot lambda isolates learned directional structure -- not architectural capacity or auxiliary loss alone -- as the source of interference when the alignment signal exceeds its optimum. Together these findings implicate a design principle for compositional planning in latent reasoning systems: medium-horizon intent must be coherent across enough computational steps for compositional structure to form.

</details>


### [55] [Proof-Refactor: Refactoring Generated Formal Proofs into Modular Artifacts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03743v1)
*Yiming Fu,Peixuan Liu,Zichen Wang,Kun yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Proof-Refactor agent框架自动化形式证明重构，属于coding agent范畴，可直接借鉴。

TL;DR: 提出了Proof-Refactor，一个过程引导的证明重构框架，通过四个阶段提升LLM生成证明的可读性和模块化，在PutnamBench和Putnam2025上优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的证明缺乏可读性、模块化等库质量，现有方法依赖基于长度的优化，难以捕捉高级质量属性。

Method: 提出Proof-Refactor框架，将证明重构分解为四个阶段：提取候选证明片段、设计辅助声明、形式化证明提取和设计的组件、使用验证过的组件修复原始证明。

Result: 在PutnamBench和Putnam2025的生成Lean证明上，Proof-Refactor在基于评分标准的重构分数上优于Claude Code基线，尤其在签名质量和人类可读性方面提升最大。

Conclusion: 过程引导的重构可以在不主要优化证明长度的情况下改进证明结构，提升可读性和模块化。

中文摘要：尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在生成形式化证明方面展现了强大的性能，但它们的输出往往不如成熟形式化数学库中的证明那样可读、模块化、可维护和可重用。我们认为，这一差距部分源于大多数证明生成流程中隐含的“先编译”目标，该目标鼓励使用单一或临时的证明脚本，而非库质量的工件。现有的证明质量改进方法通常依赖于显式的、可计算的优化目标。然而在实践中，最易处理且经过实验验证的目标主要是基于长度的，而更高级的质量如可读性、模块化、可维护性和可重用性很难简化为可靠的自动度量。我们不是针对单一的代理度量来优化证明改进，而是采用受人类证明重构工作流启发的过程引导方法。我们提出了一个智能体框架Proof-Refactor，将证明重构分解为四个阶段：提取候选证明片段、设计辅助声明、形式化证明提取和设计的组件、以及使用验证过的组件修复原始证明。在来自PutnamBench和Putnam2025的生成Lean证明上，Proof-Refactor在基于评分标准的重构分数上优于强大的Claude Code重构基线，其中在签名质量和人类可读性方面提升最大。这些结果表明，过程引导的重构可以在不将证明长度作为主要目标的情况下改进证明结构。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown strong performance in generating formal proofs, their outputs often remain less readable, modular, maintainable, and reusable than proofs in mature formal mathematics libraries. We argue that this gap stems in part from the compile-first objective implicit in most proof-generation pipelines, which encourages monolithic or ad hoc proof scripts rather than library-quality artifacts. Existing approaches to proof-quality improvement often rely on explicit, computable optimization objectives. In practice, however, the most tractable and experimentally validated objectives are largely length-based, while higher-level qualities such as readability, modularity, maintainability, and reusability are difficult to reduce to reliable automatic metrics. Instead of optimizing proof improvement against a single proxy metric, we take a process-guided approach inspired by human proof-refactoring workflows. We propose an agentic framework $\textbf{Proof-Refactor}$ that decomposes proof refactoring into four phases: extracting candidate proof fragments, designing helper declarations, formally proving the extracted and designed components, and repairing the original proof using the verified components. On generated Lean proofs from PutnamBench and Putnam2025, Proof-Refactor improves rubric-based refactoring scores over a strong Claude Code refactoring baseline, with the largest gains in signature quality and human readability. These results suggest that process-guided refactoring can improve proof structure without treating proof length as the primary objective.

</details>


### [56] [LAP: An Agent-to-Instrument Protocol for Autonomous Science](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03755v1)
*Linwu Zhu,Liqiang Gao,Yan Chen,Dan Zhu,Jian Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent到仪器协议LAP，包含状态管理、安全握手等通用agent设计元素，但领域垂直。

TL;DR: 实验室代理协议(LAP)是一个填补代理到仪器边缘空白的协议，通过添加物理世界原语实现自主科学实验中仪器与代理的安全、可重现交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主科学系统需从头重建推理代理与物理仪器的连接，且现有互操作性协议(MCP、A2A)未考虑代理到仪器边缘的有状态、安全关键、物理体现特性。

Method: LAP基于A2A结构，引入仪器卡片、保留锁定、安全围栏握手和测量结果模式等物理世界原语，并定义六层架构、JSON-RPC方法集、状态机及错误模型。

Result: LAP实现了与A2A/MCP生态兼容的代理-仪器交互，支持仪器能力发现、独占锁定、安全门控操作及可重现的物理有类型测量结果，并通过闭环自主实验验证。

Conclusion: LAP封装而非替换现有设备标准，为自主科学实验提供了统一的代理到仪器接口，加速了从演示到基础设施的转变。

中文摘要：自动化科学正从演示走向基础设施。大型语言模型代理现在规划实验，自动驾驶实验室执行实验。然而，每个这样的系统都从头重建推理代理与物理仪器之间的连接，面对碎片化的供应商SDK和专为确定性软件客户端而非概率性、目标导向代理设计的标准。最近的代理互操作性协议明确了代理生态系统的三个边中的两个（Anthropic的模型上下文协议(MCP)标准化了代理到工具的边，Google的Agent2Agent (A2A)标准化了代理到代理的边），但两者都没有建模代理到仪器的边，该边的操作是有状态的、安全关键的、独占的、物理体现的，并产生带有单位、校准和不确定性的测量结果。我们提出了实验室代理协议(LAP)，一种填补这一空白的协议设计。LAP保留了A2A的点对点、发现优先、任务生命周期结构，并增加了四个物理世界原语：(i)仪器卡片，一种签名的能力和物理极限描述；(ii)用于独占仪器和样本锁定的一类保留；(iii)安全围栏握手，与特定任务及其参数加密绑定的操作者确认令牌，用于门控危险和不可逆操作；(iv)测量结果模式，使每个结果在物理上是有类型的(QUDT/UCUM)、校准锚定、携带不确定性且可重现的。我们指定了角色、六层架构、JSON-RPC方法集、任务和安全状态机、错误模型以及跨实验室联邦，并端到端地演示了一个闭环自主实验活动。LAP与A2A/MCP生态系统传输兼容，并封装而不是替换现有设备标准如SiLA 2和OPC-UA。

Original abstract: Autonomous science is moving from demonstration to infrastructure. Large language model agents now plan experiments, and self-driving laboratories execute them. Yet every such system rebuilds the link between the reasoning agent and the physical instrument from scratch, against fragmented vendor SDKs and standards built for deterministic software clients rather than probabilistic, goal-directed agents. Recent agent-interoperability protocols clarify two of the three edges of an agentic ecosystem (Anthropic's Model Context Protocol (MCP) standardizes the agent-to-tool edge, and Google's Agent2Agent (A2A) the agent-to-agent edge), but neither models the agent-to-instrument edge, where operations are stateful, safety-critical, exclusively owned, physically embodied, and produce measurements with units, calibration, and uncertainty. We present the Lab Agent Protocol (LAP), a protocol design that fills this gap. LAP retains A2A's peer-to-peer, discovery-first, task-lifecycle structure and adds four physical-world primitives: (i) the InstrumentCard, a signed capability and physical-limit description; (ii) first-class reservation for exclusive instrument and sample locking; (iii) a safety-fence handshake with operator-confirmation tokens cryptographically bound to a specific task and its parameters, gating hazardous and irreversible operations; and (iv) a MeasurementResult schema that makes every result physically typed (QUDT/UCUM), calibration-anchored, uncertainty-bearing, and reproducible by construction. We specify roles, a six-layer architecture, the JSON-RPC method set, the task and safety state machines, the error model, and cross-laboratory federation, and walk a closed-loop autonomous campaign through the protocol end-to-end. LAP is transport-compatible with the A2A/MCP ecosystem and encapsulates rather than replaces existing device standards such as SiLA 2 and OPC-UA.

</details>


### [57] [From Control Boundary to Insurance Claim: Reconstructing AI-Mediated Losses Through the CER Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03777v1)
*Alex Leung,Rex Zhang,Kentaroh Toyoda,SiewMei Loh*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: CER框架分析AI系统损失重建与保险，涉及agent系统安全与控制边界，有一定启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出CER框架，通过控制边界、证据重建和保险响应三个维度诊断AI残余风险转移，解决AI系统导致损失时需要的状态重建问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI系统造成的损失需要状态重建而非仅事件重建，但现有方法无法有效支持保险索赔追偿，因此需要新的诊断框架。

Method: 提出了CER（控制边界、证据重建、保险响应）用例级诊断框架，分别评估系统的操作范围、状态重建能力和保险可理赔性。

Result: 定义了AI特定的重建问题，通过CER将其操作化，并指定了索赔级证据要求，提供了公开案例验证。

Conclusion: CER框架能够系统性地评估AI残余风险转移，为AI保险索赔提供结构化诊断和证据标准。

中文摘要：通过被保险组织的生成式或智能体AI系统产生的AI损失需要状态重建，而不仅仅是事件重建，因为相关状态随着系统推理、检索、调用工具和行动而变化。相关的问题不仅是发生了什么损失，还包括系统被允许做什么、它实际做了什么，以及重建的损失是否能支持保险索赔追偿。本文讨论了被保险人的AI系统处于因果链条中的损失，包括外部触发的故障，如提示注入、检索增强生成（RAG）投毒、恶意工具输出、凭据滥用和数据投毒。具体而言，本文引入了CER，一种用于AI残余风险转移的用例级诊断方法。C（控制边界）询问系统是否具有可执行的操作范围。E（证据重建）询问系统状态和因果链是否可以从保留的工件中重建。R（保险响应）询问重建的损失是否被保险：即在市场上是否有保险覆盖并已为被保险人投保，以及支持保险索赔追偿所需的证据。本文做出了三个贡献：定义了AI特定的重建问题，通过CER将问题操作化，并指定了用于AI重建的索赔级证据。公开示例包括报道的PocketOS和Replit智能体数据库删除事件，以及Moffatt诉加拿大航空公司的裁决输出/依赖案例。关键词：AI系统；CER框架；残余风险转移；智能体AI；生成式AI；AI保险；证据重建。

Original abstract: AI losses that arise through an insured organization's generative or agentic AI system require state reconstruction, not merely event reconstruction, because the relevant state changes as the system reasons, retrieves, calls tools, and acts. The relevant question is not only what loss occurred, but what the system was allowed to do, what it actually did, and whether that reconstructed loss can support insurance claim recovery. This paper addresses losses in which the insured's AI system is in the causal chain, including externally triggered failures such as prompt injection, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) poisoning, malicious tool output, credential misuse, and data poisoning.
  Specifically, this paper introduces CER, a use-case-level diagnostic for AI residual risk transfer. C (control boundary) asks whether the system had an enforceable operating envelope. E (evidence reconstruction) asks whether the system state and causal chain can be reconstructed from retained artifacts. R (insurance response) asks whether the reconstructed loss is insured: whether insurance coverage is available in the market and placed for the insured, together with the proof needed to support insurance claim recovery.
  The paper makes three contributions: it defines the AI-specific reconstruction problem, operationalizes that problem through CER, and specifies claim-grade evidence for AI reconstruction. Public examples include the reported PocketOS and Replit agentic database-deletion incidents and Moffatt v. Air Canada as an adjudicated output/reliance case.
  Keywords: AI systems; CER framework; residual risk transfer; agentic AI; generative AI; AI insurance; evidence reconstruction.

Original abstract: Operational safety in high-stakes domains such as industrial process control, autonomous, and safety-critical systems, demand reliable hazard identification. While large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in automating safety analysis tasks, single-turn, monolithic inference is brittle: it lacks the self-correction, deliberation, and contextual refinement that safety engineers apply iteratively. In this paper, we introduce HAZDIAL, a framework that investigates whether structured agentic dialogue-multi-agent, multi-turn interactions improves the quality of NLP- based hazard identification over single-pass baselines. We systematically compare two dialogue modalities: adversarial debate and constructive discussion, and propose an algorithm-based agentic interaction optimization. We evaluate all configurations against a curated golden dataset using standard classification metrics (accuracy, precision, recall, F1) and novel dialogue metrics. This work advances the intersection of dialogue systems, multi-agent reasoning, and AI safety, providing an empirical evidence for dialogue-driven hazard analysis.

### [59] [BigFinanceBench: A Workflow-Grounded Benchmark for Financial-Research Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03829v1)
*Alex Wang,Georg Meinhardt,Jacob Katz,Joseph H. Kim,Pratyush K. Chaudhary,Chase Blagden,Eric Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有金融基准只评估最终答案或孤立子技能，忽略了可审计的推导过程，而这对决策至关重要。

Method: 构建一个包含928个专家编写任务的基准，每个任务有真实答案和点加权评分标准，将推导分解为独立可检查步骤，共36,241个评分点。

Result: 评估10个前沿AI系统，最佳系统仅得到58.8%评分得分；最终答案准确率是推导质量的有损代理；模型能力在金融工作流中非均匀分布。

Conclusion: 当前AI系统在金融研究推导任务上存在很大改进空间，BigFinanceBench为全面评估和定位失败提供了基础。

中文摘要：金融研究答案只有在另一位分析师能够审计其产生过程时才具有决策相关性：选择了哪个来源、使用了哪个时期和会计定义、做出了哪些假设以及如何执行计算。现有金融基准主要评估孤立的子技能或最终答案，而忽略了可审计的推导过程。我们引入了BigFinanceBench，这是一个由928个专家编写的开放式金融研究任务基准，每个任务都配有一个真实参考答案和一个按点加权的评分标准，该标准将推导过程分解为独立可检查的步骤。BigFinanceBench以工作流程为基础，评估完整的推导过程而不仅仅是最终输出。通过36,241个评分点，该基准支持部分评分和跨分析师工作流的故障定位。评估了十个当前前沿和开放权重的智能体后，我们发现有很大的改进空间：最佳系统仅达到58.8%的评分得分，最终答案准确率是有用但损失性的推导质量替代指标，并且模型能力在金融工作流中非均匀变化。

Original abstract: Financial-research answers are decision-relevant only when another analyst can audit how they were produced: which source was chosen, which period and accounting definition were used, which assumptions were made, and how the calculation was performed. Existing finance benchmarks largely evaluate isolated subskills or final answers, leaving the auditable derivation itself under-measured. We introduce BigFinanceBench, a 928-item expert-authored benchmark of open-ended financial-research tasks in which each item pairs a ground-truth reference answer with a point-weighted rubric that decomposes the derivation into independently checkable steps. BigFinanceBench is workflow-grounded in that it evaluates the full derivation rather than only the final output. Across 36,241 rubric points, the benchmark supports partial-credit evaluation and localization of failures across the analyst workflow. Evaluating ten current frontier and open-weight agents, we find substantial headroom: the best system reaches only 58.8% rubric score, final-answer accuracy is a useful but lossy proxy for derivation quality, and model capability varies non-uniformly across financial workflows.

</details>


### [60] [EvoDS: Self-Evolving Autonomous Data Science Agent with Skill Learning and Context Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03841v1)
*Zherui Yang,Fan Liu,Yansong Ning,Hao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 数据科学agent具备技能学习与上下文管理，通用agent方法可迁移

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理受限于静态动作集和缺乏原则性长期上下文管理，无法跨任务积累可复用经验，且在多阶段迭代流程中可靠性不足。

Method: 提出EvoDS，包含自主技能获取（ASA）机制和自适应上下文压缩（ACC）策略，采用两阶段多代理训练方案，将上下文管理建模为学习控制问题。

Conclusion: 理论证明分层设计减少工具选择误差，优化目标符合信息瓶颈原则；实验验证了方法的有效性，实现了高效上下文使用和自主改进。

中文摘要：近期在大语言模型（LLM）代理方面的进展使得自动化数据科学取得了有希望的进步。然而，现有方法仍然受限于静态动作集和缺乏原则性的长期上下文管理，阻碍了它们在任务间积累可复用经验以及在多阶段、迭代式数据科学流程中可靠运行的能力。为应对这些挑战，我们引入了EvoDS，一个通过代理强化学习来扩展自身技能并自适应管理长期上下文的自我进化自主数据科学代理。具体而言，EvoDS引入了两个关键策略：（1）自主技能获取（ASA）机制，使代理能够合成、验证和重用可执行技能；（2）自适应上下文压缩（ACC）策略，将上下文管理视为一个学习到的控制问题而非被动截断。这些策略在一个两阶段多代理训练方案中协调，使EvoDS能够随着时间自主改进。理论上，我们证明了EvoDS的分层设计减少了工具选择误差，其优化目标与信息瓶颈原则一致，确保了上下文的高效使用。实证上，EvoDS在四个不同基准测试上平均优于最先进的开源数据科学代理28.9%，同时消除了超出token限制的失败。我们的代码和数据可在https://github.com/usail-hkust/EvoDS获取。

Original abstract: Recent progress in Large Language Model (LLM) agents has enabled promising advances in automated data science. However, existing approaches remain fundamentally limited by their static action sets and lack of principled long-horizon context management, hindering their ability to accumulate reusable experience across tasks and operate reliably in multi-stage, iterative data science pipelines. To address these challenges, we introduce EvoDS, a self-evolving autonomous data science agent that learns to expand its skills and adaptively managing long-term context through agentic reinforcement learning. Specifically, EvoDS introduces two key strategies: (1) Autonomous Skill Acquisition (ASA) mechanism, which enables agents to synthesize, validate, and reuse executable skills; and (2) Adaptive Context Compression (ACC) strategy, which treats context management as a learned control problem rather than passive truncation. These strategies are orchestrated within a two-stage multi-agent training scheme, enabling EvoDS to autonomously improve over time. Theoretically, we prove that EvoDS's hierarchical design reduces tool-selection error, and its optimization objective aligns with an information bottleneck principle, ensuring efficient context use. Empirically, EvoDS outperforms state-of-the-art open-source data science agents by an average of 28.9% across four diverse benchmarks while eliminating out-of-token failures. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/usail-hkust/EvoDS.

Original abstract: Despite the pivotal role of numerical reasoning as the cornerstone of mathematical capabilities in large language models (LLMs) across applications, few benchmarks evaluate LLMs by integrating numerical processing and mathematical reasoning, hindering the interpretability of failures in math tasks. We introduce PyraMathBench, a comprehensive hierarchical benchmark with 32,505 questions derived from 7,404 math word problems, spanning 4 key cognitive aspects, 14 subcategories, and 2 modalities. Experiments reveal that LLMs' performance is severely compromised by inadequate numerical computation and weak handling of abstract numerical questions. To address this, we propose the Smart Optimization & Learning-based VErsatile module (SOLVE) and Interactive Relative Policy Optimization (IRPO), which enhance LLMs' numerical-mathematical synergy via efficient tool calls (fuzzy matching and low-quality call rejection). Comparative experiments show Qwen-2.5 achieves a 5.0 score improvement with SOLVE and IRPO training.

Original abstract: AI agents can increasingly handle the mechanical tasks of financial analysis: retrieving documents, calculating formulas, updating spreadsheets.
