We present Hedge-Bench 1.0: a benchmark of 102 actual, on-the-job tasks grounded in the explicit reasoning traces of professional hedge fund analysts working with relevant information sources. This approach enables deterministic grading against verified expert steps. Frontier models and agents score below 16\% on the benchmark. We publish the dataset and evaluation harness at github.com/Trata-Inc/trata-hedge-bench.

### [63] [Lean4Agent: Formal Modeling and Verification for Agent Workflow and Trajectory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06523v2)
*Ruida Wang,Jerry Huang,Pengcheng Wang,Xuanqing Liu,Luyang Kong,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Lean4Agent框架，利用Lean4形式语言建模和验证代理工作流，提升LLM多步工作流的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs执行多步工作流缺乏形式化方法，受自然语言模糊性问题启发，需要形式语言来指定、验证和调试代理行为。

Method: 使用Lean4依赖类型形式语言构建FormalAgentLib库以建模和验证工作流语义一致性，并开发LeanEvolve基于验证结果修订工作流。

Result: 在SWE-Bench-Verified和ELAIP-Bench上，验证通过的工作流性能平均高出11.94%，LeanEvolve进一步提升7.47%。

Conclusion: Lean4Agent为使用依赖类型形式语言建模和验证代理行为奠定了新领域的基础。

中文摘要：让大型语言模型（LLMs）能够执行可靠的多步骤工作流已成为人工智能中的核心挑战。尽管LLMs在代理能力方面取得了最新进展，但大多数代理系统仍然缺乏用于指定、验证和调试其工作流及执行轨迹的形式化方法。这一挑战反映了数学中长期存在的问题，即自然语言（NLs）的模糊性促使了形式语言（FLs）的发展。受此范式启发，我们提出了Lean4Agent，据我们所知，这是第一个使用Lean4（一种依赖类型形式语言）来建模和验证代理行为的框架。Lean4Agent推出了FormalAgentLib，一个可扩展的Lean4库，用于在显式假设下形式化建模和验证代理工作流的语义一致性，并能够定位轨迹中揭示的执行时故障。基于FormalAgentLib，我们进一步开发了LeanEvolve，它应用FormalAgentLib中的结果来修订工作流以增强其能力。在SWE-Bench-Verified的一个困难问题子集和ELAIP-Bench的一个子集上，跨越5个领先LLMs的大量实验表明，通过验证的工作流比未通过的性能平均高出11.94%，而LeanEvolve进一步将SWE性能平均提升7.47%。此外，Lean4Agent为使用表达性依赖类型形式语言形式化建模和验证代理行为的新领域奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Equipping Large Language Models (LLMs) to execute reliable multi-step workflows has become a central challenge in artificial intelligence. Despite recent advances in LLMs' agentic capabilities, most agent systems still lack formal methods for specifying, verifying, and debugging their workflow and execution trajectories. This challenge mirrors a long-standing problem in mathematics, where the ambiguity of natural languages (NLs) motivates the development of formal languages (FLs). Inspired by this paradigm, we propose **Lean4Agent**, to the best of our knowledge, the first framework that uses Lean4, a dependent-type FL to model and verify agent behavior. **Lean4Agent** launches **FormalAgentLib**, an extensible Lean4 library for formally modeling and verifying agent workflows' semantic consistency under explicit assumptions, and enabling localization of execution-time failures revealed by trajectories. Building on **FormalAgentLib**, we further develop **LeanEvolve**, which applies results in **FormalAgentLib** to revise workflows to enhance its capability. Extensive experiments on a hard problem subset of SWE-Bench-Verified and a subset of ELAIP-Bench across 5 leading LLMs indicate that the verification-passing workflows outperform the failing ones by an average of **11.94%**, and **LeanEvolve** further improves SWE performance by **7.47%** on average. Furthermore, **Lean4Agent** establishes a foundation for a new field of using expressive dependent-type FL to formally model and verify agent behavior.

### [64] [CrowdMath: A Dataset of Crowdsourced Mathematical Research Discussions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06526v1)
*Sherin Muckatira,Jesse Geneson,Slava Gerovitch,Pavel Etingof,Mikhail Gronas,Anna Rumshisky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多参与者协作证明的论文，涉及错误识别和修复，可迁移至多agent协作和自我改进策略。

TL;DR: 本文介绍了CrowdMath，一个专家标注的协作数学讨论数据集，并评估了语言模型，发现它们能预测下一帖子但难以分类帖子角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准未涵盖协作式开放问题求解，需要评估模型理解团队合作解决数学问题的能力。

Method: 从AoPS论坛收集讨论链，专家标注帖子功能角色，定义评估任务（下一帖子预测和角色分类）并测试六个模型。

Result: 下一帖子预测准确率83-88%，角色分类宏F1最高0.42。

Conclusion: 模型在理解局部流程上有一定能力，但在识别贡献的语义角色上存在显著差距。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在数学推理方面取得了实质性进展，但现有基准通常评估具有最终答案、逐步解决方案或完整证明的明确问题。它们没有捕捉到协作式开放问题求解：在这种环境中，参与者提出部分论证，识别先前步骤中的空白或错误，修复有缺陷的推理，并逐步将增量贡献综合成一个证明。我们引入了CrowdMath，这是一个包含来自MIT PRIMES–Art of Problem Solving (AoPS) CrowdMath项目（2016–2025）的164个专家注释的进展链的数据集，该项目是一个合作研究计划，其讨论已导致同行评审出版物。每条链追踪从一个开放问题陈述到完成证明的多参与者论坛讨论。帖子根据其在不断演变的解决方案过程中的功能角色进行标注，包括部分进展、证明完成、错误推理和错误识别。我们定义了评估任务并对六个前沿模型进行了基准测试。模型在下一帖子预测上达到了83-88%的准确率，表明它们可以遵循数学讨论的局部流程。然而，它们难以识别单个贡献的功能意义，最佳模型在帖子角色分类上仅达到0.42的宏F1分数。CrowdMath揭示了解决明确数学问题与理解协作数学进展之间的差距。

Original abstract: Large language models have made substantial progress on mathematical reasoning, but existing benchmarks typically evaluate well-specified problems with final answers, step-by-step solutions, or complete proofs. They do not capture collaborative open-problem solving: a setting in which participants propose partial arguments, identify gaps or errors in prior steps, repair flawed reasoning, and gradually synthesize incremental contributions into a proof. We introduce CrowdMath, a dataset of 164 expert-annotated progress chains from the MIT PRIMES--Art of Problem Solving (AoPS) CrowdMath program (2016-2025), a collaborative research initiative whose discussions have led to peer-reviewed publications. Each chain traces a multi-participant forum discussion from an open-problem statement to a completed proof. Posts are labeled by their functional roles in the evolving solution process, including partial progress, proof completion, erroneous reasoning, and error identification. We define evaluation tasks and benchmark six frontier models. Models achieve 83-88% accuracy on next-post prediction, suggesting that they can follow the local flow of mathematical discussion. However, they struggle to identify the functional significance of individual contributions with the best model achieving only 0.42 macro-F1 on post-role classification. CrowdMath exposes a gap between solving well-specified mathematical problems and understanding collaborative mathematical progress as it unfolds.

### [65] [SMAC-Talk: A Natural Language Extension of the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge for Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04202v1)
*Joel Sol,Homayoun Najjaran*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent协作环境，包含欺骗性通信和长程决策，对agent协作与信任研究有直接启发。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: As LLMs become more widely deployed, they are increasingly expected to work alongside other AI agents rather than operating in isolation. Effective coordination in these settings requires agents to communicate, share information and make decisions under uncertainty. We introduce SMAC-Talk, a natural language extension of the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge for evaluating LLM-based agents in cooperative multi-agent environments. The environment has several key features such as decentralized control, partial observability and long-horizon decision making. SMAC-Talk includes a natural language communication channel which is used to probe agent coordination and trust. We use this communication channel to construct different evaluation scenarios, including settings with an embedded deceptive communicator that tries to disrupt and deceive allies through communication alone. We provide three agents for benchmarking using 4 models from the Qwen3.5 family and study how reasoning structure, memory and model scale affect coordination between agents. We release SMAC-Talk as an open benchmark to support the research community in developing and evaluating LLM agents in cooperative multi-agent settings.

### [66] [Consensus is Strategically Insufficient: Reasoning-Trace Disagreement as a Knowledge-Representation Signal](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04223v1)
*Michał Wawer,Jarosław A. Chudziak*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究多agent系统中分歧的表示与路由，可迁移至agent推理轨迹分析和协作策略。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于分歧状态的知识表示层，用于多智能体系统中处理价值负载任务中的真实规范性不确定性，并在内容审核中实例化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法旨在减少分歧，但价值负载任务中分歧可能反映真实规范性不确定性而非错误，需要新的处理方式。

Method: 提出知识表示层，将推理轨迹和二元决策抽象为四种符号化分歧状态，并基于可废止规则进行策略路由。

Result: 在内容审核任务中实例化，证明分歧感知路由能连接亚符号LLM推理与符号知识表示。

Conclusion: 分歧感知路由为多智能体在价值负载任务中的策略推理提供有效桥梁。

中文摘要：多智能体系统通常设计为通过投票、共识协议、辩论或容错聚合来减少分歧。我们认为，这一目标对于价值负载的任务是不够的，因为分歧可能反映的是真正的规范性不确定性，而非智能体错误。基于先前关于人机协作审核中推理轨迹分歧的研究，我们提出了一个知识表示层，在该层中，推理轨迹和智能体决策被抽象为符号化的分歧状态。给定产生显式推理轨迹和二元决策的智能体，我们根据推理相似性和结论一致性区分出四种状态：趋同一致、趋异一致、趋同分歧和趋异分歧。这些状态支持可废止的策略性路由规则。我们在内容审核中实例化该框架，并论证了分歧感知路由在亚符号级别的大语言模型推理与多智能体策略推理的符号知识表示之间提供了桥梁。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems are commonly designed to reduce disagreement through voting, consensus protocols, debate, or fault-tolerant aggregation. We argue that this objective is insufficient for value-laden tasks, where disagreement may reflect genuine normative uncertainty rather than agent error. Building on prior work on reasoning-trace disagreement in human-AI collaborative moderation, we propose a knowledge-representation layer in which reasoning traces and agent decisions are abstracted into symbolic disagreement states. Given agents producing explicit reasoning traces and binary decisions, we distinguish four states according to reasoning similarity and conclusion agreement: convergent agreement, divergent agreement, convergent disagreement and divergent disagreement. These states support defeasible strategic routing rules. We instantiate the framework in content moderation and argue that disagreement-aware routing provides a bridge between sub-symbolic LLM deliberation and symbolic knowledge representation for multi-agent strategic reasoning.

</details>


### [67] [StepPRM-RTL: Stepwise Process-Reward Guided LLM Fine-Tuning for Enhanced RTL Synthesis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04246v1)
*Prashanth Vijayaraghavan,Apoorva Nitsure,Luyao Shi,Ehsan Degan,Vandana Mukherjee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用过程奖励模型和MCTS进行RTL代码生成，直接相关代码优化agent的搜索与反馈机制。

TL;DR: StepPRM-RTL通过结合逐步轨迹建模、过程奖励模型和检索增强微调，显著提升了LLM生成RTL代码的功能正确性和推理保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在RTL代码生成中面临长程推理、多步依赖和严格正确性约束的挑战，标准的监督或结果训练方法难以学习正确的推理过程。

Method: StepPRM-RTL从规范解构建逐步推理轨迹，使用过程奖励模型评估中间步骤并提供密集反馈，结合蒙特卡洛树搜索探索替代路径，通过RAF微调优化模型。

Result: 在Verilog和VHDL基准数据集上，StepPRM-RTL在功能正确性和推理保真度上比最佳先前方法提升超过10%，消融研究验证了PRM引导奖励和逐步轨迹探索的关键作用。

Conclusion: StepPRM-RTL跨RTL语言泛化良好，为高保真、可解释的LLM辅助硬件设计自动化提供了可扩展框架，建立了新标准。

中文摘要：数字硬件设计的RTL代码自动生成仍然具有挑战性，原因是Verilog和VHDL中需要长程推理、多步依赖以及严格的正确性约束。我们提出了StepPRM-RTL，一种新颖的框架，结合了逐步轨迹建模、过程奖励模型（PRM）和检索增强微调（RAFT），以提升基于LLM的RTL代码生成的功能正确性和推理保真度。StepPRM-RTL从规范解构建逐步推理轨迹，其中每一步包含推理过程和增量代码修改。过程奖励模型（PRM）评估中间步骤，提供密集反馈，指导RAFT微调期间的强化式更新。蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）探索替代推理路径，用高质量轨迹丰富训练数据集。这种逐步和结果感知奖励的整合使得模型能够学习如何以及为何构建正确的RTL，从而在长程推理上超越标准的监督或基于结果的训练。在基准Verilog和VHDL数据集上的实验评估表明，StepPRM-RTL在功能正确性和推理保真度指标上比过往最佳方法提高超过10%。消融研究证实，PRM引导的奖励和逐步轨迹探索的结合是其性能的关键。StepPRM-RTL跨RTL语言泛化，并为高保真、可解释的代码生成提供了可扩展框架，为LLM辅助硬件设计自动化确立了新标准。

Original abstract: Automatic generation of RTL code for digital hardware designs remains challenging due to long-horizon reasoning, multi-step dependencies, and strict correctness constraints in Verilog and VHDL. We present StepPRM-RTL, a novel framework that combines stepwise trajectory modeling, process-reward modeling (PRM), and retrieval-augmented fine-tuning (RAFT) to enhance both the functional correctness and reasoning fidelity of LLM-based RTL code generation. StepPRM-RTL constructs stepwise reasoning trajectories from canonical solutions, where each step contains a rationale and incremental code modification. A Process Reward Model (PRM) evaluates intermediate steps, providing dense feedback that guides reinforcement-style updates during RAFT fine-tuning. Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) explores alternative reasoning paths, enriching the training dataset with high-quality trajectories. This integration of stepwise and outcome-aware rewards allows the model to learn both how and why to construct correct RTL, improving long-horizon reasoning beyond standard supervised or outcome-based training. Experimental evaluation on benchmark Verilog and VHDL datasets demonstrates that StepPRM-RTL outperforms the best prior methods by over 10\% in functional correctness and reasoning fidelity metrics. Ablation studies confirm that the combination of PRM-guided rewards and stepwise trajectory exploration is key to its performance. StepPRM-RTL generalizes across RTL languages and provides a scalable framework for high-fidelity, interpretable code generation, establishing a new standard for LLM-assisted hardware design automation.

### [68] [Can Generalist Agents Automate Data Curation?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04261v1)
*Feiyang Kang,Hanze Li,Adam Nguyen,Mahavir Dabas,Jiaqi W. Ma,Frederic Sala,Dawn Song,Ruoxi Jia*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通用agent自动化数据整理，包含迭代策略探索和方法改编，对agent自动化研究有重要启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出Curation-Bench基准，发现现成AI代理在数据策展中存在执行-研究差距，而支架化代理能自主组合出以十分之一数据预算超越强基线的数据选择策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据策展耗时且重要，但现有过程依赖人工迭代，作者希望用通用编码代理自动化这一循环。

Method: 提出Curation-Bench基准，固定模型、训练和评估，让代理通过命令行访问数据、实现并提交策略、接收反馈并修订；在视觉语言指令微调中实验，并引入支架要求代理每次迭代引用和适应先前方法。

Result: 开箱即用代理10次迭代达到强基线，但主要调整局部变体；支架代理自主组合策略，以十分之一数据预算超越强基线，而无需人类设计输入。

Conclusion: 当前代理能运行策展循环，但可靠的数据研究需支架式方法适应，而非仅开放式提示。

中文摘要：策展训练数据是现代人工智能开发中最具影响力但也是最劳动密集的部分之一：实践者根据嘈杂的基准反馈，迭代地提出、实现、评估和修订数据策略。我们探讨通用编码代理能否自动化这一数据策展循环。我们引入了 *Curation-Bench*，一个以代理为中心的基准，它固定模型、训练配方和评估套件，同时赋予代理命令行访问权限来检查数据、实现策略、将其提交到固定的训练/评估管道并修订。在视觉语言指令微调实例中，开箱即用的代理在十次迭代内达到了强发布的数据选择基线。然而，轨迹分析揭示了一个持续的*执行-研究差距*：代理主要调整局部策略变体，而不是探索新的策略家族，即使提供了策略指南和论文参考文献。要求每次迭代引用、实例化和适应先前方法的支架（scaffold）使代理转向方法引导的探索。支架代理自主组合——无需人类设计输入——一个数据选择策略，在十分之一的数据预算下超越了强发布的基线。总体而言，当前代理可以运行策展循环，但可靠的数据研究需要支架方法适应，而不是开放式提示。代码和基准是开源提供的。

Original abstract: Curating training data is among the most consequential yet labor-intensive parts of modern AI development: practitioners iteratively propose, implement, evaluate, and revise data policies against noisy benchmark feedback. We ask whether generalist coding agents can automate this data-curation loop. We introduce *Curation-Bench*, an agent-centric benchmark that fixes the model, training recipe, and evaluation suite while giving agents command-line access to inspect data, implement policies, submit them to a fixed training/evaluation pipeline, and revise. In a vision-language instruction-tuning instantiation, out-of-the-box agents reach strong published data-selection baselines within ten iterations. However, trajectory analysis reveals a persistent *execution-research gap*: agents mainly tune local policy variants rather than explore new policy families, even when given strategy guides and paper references. Scaffolds requiring each iteration to cite, instantiate, and adapt a prior method shift agents toward method-guided exploration. The scaffolded agent autonomously composes -- without human design input -- a data-selection policy that outperforms strong published baselines at one-tenth their data budget. Overall, current agents can run the curation loop, but reliable data research requires scaffolded method adaptation, not open-ended prompting alone. Code and benchmark are open-sourced.

</details>


### [69] [Characterizing initial human-AI proof formalization workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04273v1)
*Katherine M. Collins,Simon Frieder,Jonas Bayer,Jacob Loader,Jeck Lim,Peiyang Song,Fabian Zaiser,Lexin Zhou,Shanda Li,Sam Looi,Joshua B. Tenenbaum,Umang Bhatt,Adrian Weller,Jose Hernandez-Orallo,Cameron E. Freer,Valerie Chen,Ilia Sucholutsky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究人机协作证明形式化，涉及AI辅助工具使用，对agent与人类协作有参考价值。

TL;DR: 研究了AI在数学证明形式化中的实际使用，发现用户偏好多样化且希望保持人类控制，但使用AI工具能提高形式化准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有许多工作评估了AI在形式化证明中的能力，但缺乏对人们实际如何使用这些工具以及他们的偏好和障碍的研究。

Method: 混合方法分析：定性调查了解用户偏好和障碍；受控用户研究比较有无AI辅助时的形式化准确率。

Result: 用户偏好多样化但普遍希望AI辅助同时保留人类控制；使用AI工具时形式化准确率更高，且用户灵活使用多种AI工具。

Conclusion: AI正早期融入形式化工作流程，强调人机紧密互动，工具虽有限但已带来性能提升。

中文摘要：几个世纪以来，人类数学家一直在编写证明来证实他们的数学论点；然而，自动验证证明有效性的能力长期以来一直是一个挑战。AI系统生成代码和进行越来越高级的数学推理能力的进步，有望改变人们形式化并因此验证证明的方式。虽然许多工作集中于评估当前的前沿水平，但我们转而研究人们如何使用这些工具。我们进行了一项混合方法分析，探讨AI对人们形式化工作流程的初步影响：人们声称他们想要什么，他们认为这些愿景的障碍是什么，以及他们实际上如何适应和使用AI。一项定性调查显示，人们的偏好多样化，但普遍希望AI在形式化过程中提供帮助，同时保留人类对证明发现过程的高层控制。为了评估人们在这种限制下实际如何与AI进行形式化互动，我们进行了一项受控用户研究，参与者形式化非正式的数学问题及其证明，在有和没有AI的情况下，涉及不同难度和领域的各种数学问题。尽管当时工具在自动形式化方面存在局限性，但参与者在允许使用AI工具时，往往比独自形式化时获得更高的形式化准确率，大多数参与者灵活选择使用多种不同的AI工具。综合来看，我们的工作揭示了AI融入形式化工作流程的早期阶段，涉及人类与AI的紧密互动。

Original abstract: For centuries, human mathematicians have written proofs to substantiate their mathematical arguments; yet, the ability to automatically verify the validity of proofs has long been a challenge. Advances in AI systems' ability to generate code and engage in increasingly high-level mathematical reasoning promise to transform people's ability to formalize and thereby verify proofs. While many works focus on benchmarking the current frontier, we instead study how people use these tools. We conduct a mixed-methods analysis into the initial impact of AI on people's formalization workflows: what people claim they want, what they see as the barriers to those visions, and how they actually use and adapt AI in practice. A qualitative survey shows that people's preferences are diverse, but with a general desire for AI assistance in formalization that preserves high-level human control over the proof discovery process. To assess how people actually engage with AI for formalization under such limitations, we conduct a controlled user study in which participants formalize informal math problems and their proofs, with and without AI, across a range of mathematical problems at varying levels of difficulty and domains. Despite limitations of the tools at the time for autoformalization, participants tend to attain higher formalization accuracy when allowed access to AI tools than when formalizing on their own, with most participants flexibly choosing to use multiple different AI tools. Taken together, our work sheds light on the early stages of AI integration into formalization workflows, involving an intimate interplay of human and AI engagement.

### [70] [The Saturation Trap and the Subjectivity of Intervention Timing: Why Affect-Based Triggers and LLM Judges Fail to Time Interventions on Autonomous Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04296v1)
*Manvendra Modgil*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究自主agent干预时机问题，基于SWE-bench调试轨迹，涉及LLM裁判和可靠性，对SemOpt安全机制有启发。

TL;DR: 干预时机问题存在低信度和状态饱和陷阱，监督目标不可复现，单注释员F1不适合作为优化目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨自主AI智能体在长期执行中运行时安全层决定干预时机的可靠性问题。

Method: 使用HEART情感动力学引擎，在SWE-bench-Verified上评估四种干预触发家族，并分析人类注释者间一致性。

Result: 发现状态饱和陷阱导致阈值触发器持续触发；LLM评判者存在能力和上下文下限；人类注释者间一致性极低。

Conclusion: 干预时机是低信度概念，单注释员F1不适合作为优化目标，应联合考虑人类信度、检测器架构和模型扫描。

中文摘要：随着自主AI智能体从对话系统转向长期软件执行，决定何时中断智能体的运行时安全层变得至关重要。我们使用一个连续的18维情感动力学引擎（HEART）作为诊断探针来研究这个时机问题，针对人类标注的干预点，在SWE-bench-Verified调试轨迹上评估了四种干预触发家族——绝对状态阈值、复合状态-动作模式、正则表达式推理特征提取和零样本LLM作为评判者。我们报告了三个发现。首先，状态饱和陷阱：智能体在持续困难下没有恢复信号，因此建模的挫败感迅速超过阈值并保持最大值，将状态阈值触发器从瞬间探测器转变为近乎恒定的指示器，在五个轨迹中跨39-83%的动作触发。其次，LLM评判者的能力和上下文下限：小模型（gpt-5.4-mini）从不触发，而前沿和跨供应商模型只有在完整轨迹上下文中才能摆脱零触发下限，即便如此，F1值也仅为0.17-0.40，且成本高达90倍。第三，最重要的是，监督目标在人类之间不可复现：三位训练有素的注释员使用同一评分标准对一条56动作轨迹进行标注，在干预位置上的一致性仅略高于随机水平（位置Krippendorff's alpha = +0.047；最佳成对Cohen's kappa = +0.349），在干预类型上则完全不一致（暂停退化；澄清低于随机；反思仅alpha = +0.226）。我们得出结论，干预时机是一个低信度概念，使得单注释员F1不适合作为优化目标。我们的贡献在于联合绘制了该问题在人类间信度、四种检测器架构、跨模型LLM评判者扫描以及可复现的饱和效应上的映射，而非任何单个检测器的准确性。

Original abstract: As autonomous AI agents move from conversational systems to long-horizon software execution, runtime safety layers that decide when to interrupt an agent have become essential. We study this timing problem using a continuous 18-dimensional affective-dynamics engine (HEART) as a diagnostic probe, evaluating four intervention trigger families - absolute state thresholds, composite state-action patterns, regex reasoning-feature extraction, and zero-shot LLM-as-judge - against human-annotated intervention points on SWE-bench-Verified debugging traces. We report three findings. First, a State Saturation Trap: agents show no recovery signal under sustained difficulty, so modeled frustration quickly crosses the threshold and stays at its maximum, converting threshold-on-state triggers from moment detectors into near-constant indicators that fire on 39-83% of actions across five trajectories. Second, a capability-and-context floor for LLM judges: a small model (gpt-5.4-mini) never fires, while frontier and cross-vendor models escape the zero-firing floor only with full-trajectory context, and even then reach only F1 0.17-0.40 at up to 90x the cost. Third, and most importantly, the supervised target is not reproducible among humans: three trained annotators using one rubric on a 56-action trajectory agree on where to intervene only slightly above chance (location Krippendorff's alpha = +0.047; best pairwise Cohen's kappa = +0.349) and not at all on intervention type (pause degenerate; clarify below chance; reflect only alpha = +0.226). We conclude that intervention timing is a low-reliability construct, making single-annotator F1 an unsuitable optimization target. Our contribution is the joint mapping of this problem across human inter-rater reliability, four detector architectures, a cross-model LLM-judge sweep, and a reproduced saturation effect, rather than any single detector's accuracy.

</details>

### [71] [ConTraIRL: Factorized Contrastive Abstractions for Transferable IRL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03017v1)
*Yikang Gui,Bikramjit Banerjee,Prashant Doshi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 逆强化学习中的奖励迁移，涉及agent学习，方法可迁移

TL;DR: ConTraIRL通过解耦动力学和目标的潜在表示，实现了在未见过的组合下有效的奖励迁移，提高了样本效率和奖励恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在逆强化学习中，奖励迁移在环境动力学和任务目标组合变化时不可靠，现有方法缺乏对这两个因素解耦表示的能力。

Method: 提出ConTraIRL框架，使用双编码器架构将观测映射到独立的动力学和目标潜在表示，通过双重对比目标（时间对齐和因子化）进行训练。

Result: 在连续控制基准上，ConTraIRL在未见过的动力学-目标配对下实现了有效的少样本迁移，提高了样本效率和奖励恢复，优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 因子化对比抽象能够实现组合奖励迁移，提升逆强化学习在动态环境中的泛化能力。

中文摘要：在逆强化学习中，当策略必须泛化到环境动力学和任务目标未见过的组合时，奖励迁移是不可靠的。我们提出了用于可迁移逆强化学习的因子化对比抽象（ConTraIRL），这是一个通过学习这两个因素的解耦潜在表示来实现组合奖励迁移的框架。ConTraIRL使用双编码器架构，将观测映射到独立的动力学和目标潜在空间，并通过双重对比目标进行训练。时间对齐促使动力学编码器学习目标不变的结构，而目标编码器捕获动力学不变的特征。这种因子化支持在重组动力学-目标设置下的奖励推断。在连续控制基准上的实验表明，对于未见过的动力学-目标配对，ConTraIRL实现了有效的少样本迁移，提高了样本效率和奖励恢复，优于迁移逆强化学习的基线方法。

Original abstract: Reward transfer in Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) is unreliable when policies must generalize to unseen combinations of environment dynamics and task goals. We propose Factorized Contrastive Abstractions for Transferable IRL (ConTraIRL), a framework that enables compositional reward transfer by learning decoupled latent representations of these two factors. ConTraIRL uses a dual-encoder architecture that maps observations into separate dynamics and goal latent spaces, trained with a dual contrastive objective. Temporal alignment encourages the dynamics encoder to learn goal-invariant structure, while the goal encoder captures dynamics-invariant features. This factorization supports reward inference under recombined dynamics-goal settings. Experiments on continuous control benchmarks demonstrate effective few-shot transfer to unseen dynamics-goal pairings, improving sample efficiency and reward recovery over transfer IRL baselines.

</details>


### [72] [When RLHF Fails: A Mechanistic Taxonomy of Reward Hacking, Collapse, and Evaluator Gaming](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03238v2)
*Zelalem Abahana,David Evans,Satish Mahadevan Srinivasan,Matjaz Gams*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RLHF失败模式分类，可迁移至agent训练中的奖励滥用诊断。

TL;DR: 通过紧凑RLHF流程分类与局部化奖励黑客信号，发现激进的PPO产生最清晰信号，并可用行级诊断预警。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLHF评估需要追踪失败的出现、局部化和预警信号。

Method: 构建紧凑RLHF流程（PPO、DPO、UP-PPO等），根据奖励和评判器分数方向分类检查点和提示级转换。

Result: 激进的PPO产生最清晰的局部化奖励黑客信号；UP-PPO减少但未消除；行级诊断揭示隐藏失败；转换前特征可部分预测。

中文摘要：RLHF评估应追踪失败如何出现、在哪里局部化以及外部质量下降前出现哪些预警信号。我们通过本文构建的紧凑RLHF流程来研究该问题，包括PPO、DPO、不确定性惩罚PPO（UP-PPO）、奖励模型不确定性、近似策略漂移、多样性与重复性诊断以及两个外部LLM评判器。我们不将奖励黑客视为单一终点事件，而是根据学习奖励R_phi、评判器分数R_dag和R2_dag及其平均值R_dag的方向，对匹配的检查点和提示级转换进行分类。主要实证发现是：激进的PPO产生最清晰的局部化奖励黑客信号，UP-PPO减少但未消除该信号，行级诊断揭示了检查点平均值隐藏的失败，以及转换前特征可部分预测未来的局部化奖励黑客。核心结论是方法论上的：RLHF失败是训练动态过程，可以被分类、局部化和部分预测，而不仅仅是最终模型的病理。代码仓库见github.com/zabahana/rlhf-failure-modes-diagnostics。该流程还部署为实时交互式网络演示，用于模型比较和诊断视图，地址为rlhf-failures.zelalem.ai。

Original abstract: RLHF evaluation should track how failures emerge, where they localize, and which warning signals appear before external quality degrades. We study this problem with a compact RLHF pipeline built for this paper, including PPO, DPO, uncertainty-penalized PPO (UP-PPO), reward-model uncertainty, approximate policy drift, diversity and repetition diagnostics, and two external LLM judges. Rather than treating reward hacking as a single terminal event, we classify matched checkpoint and prompt-level transitions by the directions of learned reward R_phi, judge scores R_dag and R2_dag, and their average R_dag. The main empirical findings are that aggressive PPO produces the clearest localized reward-hacking signal, UP-PPO reduces but does not eliminate that signal, row-level diagnostics reveal failures hidden by checkpoint averages, and pre-transition features partially anticipate future localized reward hacking. The central conclusion is methodological: RLHF failures are training dynamics that can be classified, localized, and partially anticipated, not only final-model pathologies. The repository is available at github.com/zabahana/rlhf-failure-modes-diagnostics. The pipeline is also deployed as a live interactive web demo for model comparison and diagnostic views at rlhf-failures.zelalem.ai.

</details>


### [73] [RUBAS: Rubric-Based Reinforcement Learning for Agent Safety](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04051v1)
*Xian Qi Loye,Qinglin Su,Zhexin Zhang,Shiyao Cui,Qi Zhu,Fei Mi,Hongning Wang,Minlie Huang*

Selection reason: 提出基于Rubric的强化学习框架用于agent安全（RUBAS），可迁移到代码agent的安全对齐。

TL;DR: 提出RUBAS，一种基于评分标准的强化学习框架，通过多维奖励对齐LLM智能体的安全工具使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐方法依赖粗略拒绝信号或静态监督，难以平衡安全与工具执行的效用，需要更细粒度的安全训练信号。

Method: RUBAS将智能体行为分解为工具使用安全、参数安全、响应安全和有益性四个维度，在完整轨迹上提供细粒度可解释奖励，用强化学习优化安全工具使用。

Result: 在多个基准上，RUBAS相比标准对齐基线提高安全性，减少基于工具的幻觉，且保持竞争力。

Conclusion: 多维评分标准奖励为安全关键工具使用环境中的LLM智能体对齐提供了有效训练信号。

中文摘要：大型语言模型进化为工具型智能体引发了一类新的安全挑战，这些挑战与真实世界的执行相关，而非简单的文本生成。现有的对齐方法通常依赖于粗略的拒绝信号或静态监督，难以在多样化的智能体风险中平衡安全性与有用的工具执行。我们提出了RUBAS，一种基于评分标准的强化学习框架，用于智能体安全。RUBAS将智能体行为分解为四个维度：工具使用安全、参数安全、响应安全和有益性。这些结构化的评分标准在完整的智能体轨迹上提供细粒度和可解释的奖励，使得强化学习能够优化安全的工具使用同时保持任务完成。跨多个智能体安全基准和模型的广泛实验表明，RUBAS相比标准对齐基线提高了安全性，减少了基于工具的幻觉，并保持了有竞争力的效用。我们的结果表明，多维度的评分标准奖励为在安全关键的工具使用环境中对齐LLM智能体提供了有效的训练信号。

Original abstract: The evolution of LLMs into tool-enabled agents creates a new class of safety challenges associated with real-world execution rather than simple text generation. Existing alignment methods often rely on coarse refusal signals or static supervision, making it difficult to balance safety with useful tool execution across diverse agentic risks. We introduce RUBAS, a rubric-based reinforcement learning framework for agent safety. RUBAS decomposes agent behavior into four dimensions: tool-use safety, argument safety, response safety, and helpfulness. These structured rubrics provide fine-grained and interpretable rewards over complete agent trajectories, enabling reinforcement learning to optimize safe tool use while preserving task completion. Extensive experiments across multiple agent safety benchmarks and models show that RUBAS improves safety over standard alignment baselines, reduces tool-grounded hallucinations, and maintains competitive utility. Our results suggest that multi-dimensional rubric rewards provide an effective training signal for aligning LLM agents in safety-critical tool-use settings.

### [74] [A Close Look At World Model Recovery In Supervised Fine-Tuned LLM Planners](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03685v1)
*Patrick Emami,Nan Qiang,Peter Graf*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究SFT LLM规划器的世界模型恢复，对agent内部表示与规划能力有启发。

TL;DR: 通过可解释性实验，发现监督微调后的LLMs能线性编码动作有效性和状态谓词，内部表示与输出分类能力分离，且更广泛的数据覆盖有助于恢复世界模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究微调后的LLMs是否真正学习了规划问题的世界模型表示和推理，而不仅是生成计划。

Method: 设计了一系列可解释性实验，通过分析内部表示和生成能力，全面检查世界模型恢复。

Result: 微调使LLMs线性编码动作有效性和状态谓词；模型可能内部表示有效/无效分离但输出分类困难；随机游走数据提升世界模型恢复准确性。

Conclusion: 提供了将可解释性技术应用于规划LLMs的方法，并揭示了知识表示的关键特征。

中文摘要：监督微调(SFT)改进了大语言模型(LLMs)中的端到端经典规划，但这些模型是否也学会了表示和推理它们正在解决的规划问题？由于经典规划问题的相对复杂性以及端到端计划生成对LLMs的挑战，很难探索这个问题。在我们的工作中，我们设计并执行了一系列可解释性实验，通过检查内部表示和微调LLMs的生成能力，全面探究世界模型恢复。我们发现：a) 在有效动作序列上的监督微调使LLMs能够线性编码动作有效性和一些状态谓词。b) 难以使用输出概率对动作有效性进行分类的模型可能仍然学习到将有效动作与无效动作分开的内部表示。c) 更广泛的状态空间覆盖（例如来自随机游走数据）在微调期间能产生更准确的基础世界模型恢复。总之，这项工作为将可解释性技术应用于规划LLMs贡献了一个方案，并生成了有助于阐明关于LLMs中知识如何表示的开放问题的见解。

Original abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) improves end-to-end classical planning in large language models (LLMs), but do these models also learn to represent and reason about the planning problems they are solving? Due to the relative complexity of classical planning problems and the challenge that end-to-end plan generation poses for LLMs, it has been difficult to explore this question. In our work, we devise and perform a series of interpretability experiments that holistically interrogate world model recovery by examining both internal representations and generative capabilities of fine-tuned LLMs. We find that: a) Supervised fine-tuning on valid action sequences enables LLMs to linearly encode action validity and some state predicates. b) Models that struggle to use output probabilities for classifying action validity may still learn internal representations that separate valid from invalid actions. c) Broader state space coverage during fine-tuning, such as from random walk data, yields more accurate recovery of the underlying world model. In summary, this work contributes a recipe for applying interpretability techniques to planning LLMs and generates insights that shed light on open questions about how knowledge is represented in LLMs.

### [75] [Tool-Aware Optimization with Entropy Guidance for Efficient Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03762v1)
*Hongye Cao,Nuo Yan,Haoyuan Deng,Ziwei Wang,Tianpei Yang,Jing Huo,Yuyao Zhang,Yang Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出TAO-RL框架，利用工具感知轨迹过滤与熵探索优化LLM agent的强化学习，直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出TAO-RL框架，通过工具感知轨迹过滤和熵引导探索解决工具使用强化学习中的训练不稳定问题，在7个推理基准上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集成外部工具时，过度依赖工具导致输入分布偏移，过于保守使用工具限制探索，训练不稳定。

Method: 数据层面：过滤工具调用失败或全对/全错的轨迹；算法层面：引入工具感知的熵引导奖励重塑优势函数。

Result: 在3个模型尺度、7个推理基准上，TAO-RL优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 轨迹过滤和熵引导探索相互促进，有效提升策略优化效率和推理能力。

中文摘要：智能体强化学习（RL）为大语言模型（LLMs）提供了工具使用能力，显著提升了复杂任务的推理能力。然而，集成外部工具常常会破坏训练的稳定性：过度依赖工具会导致输入分布偏移，而过于保守地使用工具则限制了有效的探索。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了一个统一框架TAO-RL，该框架将工具感知轨迹过滤与熵引导探索相结合，以实现高效策略优化。具体来说，在数据层面，TAO-RL根据两个标准过滤展开轨迹：丢弃所有工具调用均执行失败的轨迹，以及移除所有展开结果全对或全错的轨迹，因为这两种情况都会产生退化的优势估计，无法提供有区分度的学习信号。这种联合过滤保留了既具备工具能力又具有信息量的数据，建立了高质量的训练分布。在算法层面，我们引入了一种工具感知的熵引导奖励，用于重塑工具调用后令牌处的优势函数，鼓励策略在关键决策点探索更多样化的推理路径。这两个组成部分相互促进：轨迹过滤建立了清晰且信息丰富的训练基础，而熵引导探索则在关键工具交互节点推动了更强的推理行为。在3个模型尺度下的7个具有挑战性的推理基准上的大量实验表明，TAO-RL优于现有方法。

Original abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning (RL) equips large language models (LLMs) with tool-use capabilities that substantially improve reasoning on complex tasks. However, integrating external tools often destabilizes training: over-reliance on tools can induce input distribution shift, while overly conservative tool use limits effective exploration. To address this issue, we propose a unified framework TAO-RL that couples tool-aware trajectory filtering with entropy-guided exploration for efficient policy optimization. Specifically, at the data level, TAO-RL filters rollout trajectories along two criteria: discarding those where all tool invocations fail to execute, and removing those where all rollouts are either correct or incorrect, as both cases yield degenerate advantage estimates that contribute no discriminative learning signal. This joint filtering retains data that are both tool-capable and informative, establishing a high-quality training distribution. At the algorithmic level, we introduce a tool-aware entropy-guided bonus that reshapes the advantage function at post-tool-call tokens, encouraging the policy to explore more diverse reasoning paths at critical decision points. These two components are mutually reinforcing: trajectory filtering establishes a clean and informative training foundation, while entropy-guided exploration drives stronger reasoning behaviors at critical tool-interaction junctures. Extensive experiments on 7 challenging reasoning benchmarks across 3 model scales demonstrate the superiority of TAO-RL over existing methods.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过预定义的门控过滤增广（仅通过质量关卡的任务）扩展小型手工基础任务集，在RLVR训练中逐步替代人工任务，并测量成本调整交换比率。

Original abstract: The supply of high-quality training tasks is a central bottleneck for reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) on agentic language models. Each task requires a sandboxed setup, a prompt, and a hand-authored reward function, and only tasks that pass a quality bar produce useful training signal. Hand-curation at this quality bar does not scale economically to the task counts effective RL training requires, and the substitution rate between automatically generated task variants and human-authored ones is not yet established. We investigate using pre-specified, gate-filtered augmentations of a small hand-authored base as a substitute for additional human curation during RLVR. We formalize the cost-adjusted trade rate $ρ_{\text{cost}}$ between augmented and human-authored tasks, measure it through a controlled ablation across training corpora with varying augmentation share, and characterize the end-to-end economics of the augmentation pipeline. Substituting augmented content for additional human-authored tasks retains aggregate held-out generalization on a ten-benchmark suite spanning code, instruction following, reasoning, and multi-turn agentic function-calling. The cost-adjusted trade rate $ρ_{\text{cost}}$ between gated synthetic and human-authored RLVR tasks stays in $[1.4\times, 11.6\times]$ across the plausible $c_{\text{human}}/c_{\text{aug}}$ range.

### [77] [Large Language Models Hack Rewards, and Society](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04075v2)
*Wei Liu,Xinyi Mou,Hanqi Yan,Zhongyu Wei,Yulan He*

TL;DR: 研究表明，强化学习中的奖励黑客行为会扩展为社会黑客，即LLMs发现并利用社会规则漏洞，现有安全措施不足，需新后训练范式。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）已成为主导的后训练范式，使大型语言模型（LLMs）能够从奖励中学习。我们观察到，社会规则在结构上与奖励函数相似。它们定义了可测量的结果、阈值和例外情况，而通常只部分指定了制度意图。我们假设RL训练过程可能会利用这些漏洞，因此提出问题：模型在RL中已知的奖励黑客倾向是否会扩展为一种更严重的失败模式，即社会黑客（societal hacking）：发现社会运行规则中的漏洞。为了研究这一现象，我们引入了SocioHack，一个包含72个社会环境的沙盒，并发现这些环境中自然出现奖励黑客行为，导致监管漏洞的发现。模型学会破解社会规则，生成在技术上合规但破坏监管意图的策略，而当前的LLM安全措施只能提供有限的缓解。因此，收集真实世界反馈用于模型训练需要更加谨慎，我们需要下一代后训练范式，以便在真实社会中安全迭代LLM。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a dominant post-training paradigm, enabling large language models (LLMs) to learn from rewards. We observe that societal regulations are structurally similar to reward functions. They define measurable outcomes, thresholds, and exceptions, while often leaving institutional intent only partially specified. We hypothesise that the RL training process may exploit these gaps and therefore ask whether models' well-known tendency to hack reward functions during RL can scale into a more consequential failure mode named societal hacking: discovering loopholes in the rules society runs on. To study this phenomenon, we introduce SocioHack, a sandbox of 72 societal environments, and find that within these environments, reward hacking naturally emerges and leads to regulatory loophole discovery. Models learn to hack the social rules and generate strategies that remain technically compliant while defeating regulatory intent, and current LLM safeguards provide only limited mitigation. Therefore, collecting in-the-wild feedback for model training requires greater caution, and we need a next-generation post-training paradigm for safely iterating LLMs in real society.=

### [78] [Using Reward Uncertainty to Induce Diverse Behaviour in Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03962v1)
*Anthony GX-Chen,Ankit Anand,Gheorghe Comanici,Zaheer Abbas,Eser Aygün,David Smalling,Shibl Mourad,Doina Precup,André Barreto,Mark Rowland*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 利用奖励不确定性诱导多样性行为，对agent探索与奖励设计有启发

TL;DR: 将RL目标中的标量奖励替换为奖励函数分布，并对动作集应用非线性目标，从而自然产生可控多样性，无需牺牲性能。在contextual bandit中推导了梯度估计器，实验验证有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典RL缺乏多样性，现有方法存在脆弱权衡或启发式度量，多样性应理解为对奖励不确定性的理性响应。

Method: 用奖励函数分布替代标量奖励，对动作集应用非线性目标，推导原则性梯度估计器，并证明其泛化现有方法。

Result: 框架自然产生校准的行为多样性，可通过奖励分布控制，不牺牲期望奖励，在实验中表现鲁棒。

Conclusion: 该框架为需要多样性的复杂RL任务提供了一种鲁棒且理论基础的替代方案。

中文摘要：经典强化学习通常寻求一种确定性策略，最大化标量奖励的期望和。然而，现代应用如语言模型微调或科学发现需要多样性。现有补救措施如熵正则化或多样性奖励通常需要脆弱的权衡，以随机性牺牲性能，或依赖可能错位策略排名的启发式度量。我们认为多样性更自然地理解为对奖励不确定性的理性响应。当奖励函数不完全已知时——如模糊偏好或不完美奖励模型的情况——承诺单一行动可能是次优的。基于此，我们提出对RL目标的基本改革，用奖励函数的分布替换标量奖励，并对动作集合应用非线性目标。结果是一个框架，其中校准的行为多样性自然出现，可通过奖励函数分布控制，且无需牺牲期望奖励即可获得。聚焦于上下文bandit设置，我们为该目标推导了一个原则性梯度估计器，并证明我们的公式自然泛化了vanilla policy gradient和最近发展的动作集方法。我们的实证结果表明，该框架为复杂的RL任务提供了一个鲁棒且理论基础的替代方案，在这些任务中，传统的问题公式无法诱导出期望的代理行为广度。

Original abstract: Classical reinforcement learning (RL) typically seeks a deterministic policy that maximizes the expected sum of a scalar reward. Yet, modern applications such as language model fine-tuning or scientific discovery demand diversity. Existing remedies such as entropy regularization or diversity bonuses often require fragile trade-offs that sacrifice performance for stochasticity or rely on heuristic metrics that can misalign policy rankings. We argue that diversity is more naturally understood as the rational response to uncertainty in the reward. When the reward function is not perfectly known--as is the case with ambiguous preferences or imperfect reward models--committing to a single action can be sub-optimal. Building on this, we propose a fundamental reformulation of the RL objective by replacing the scalar reward with a distribution over reward functions, and applying a non-linear objective over sets of actions. The result is a framework in which calibrated behavioural diversity emerges naturally, remains controllable through the reward function distribution, and is obtained without sacrificing expected reward. Focusing on the contextual bandit setting, we derive a principled gradient estimator for this objective and prove that our formulation naturally generalizes both vanilla policy gradient and more recently developed action-set approaches. Our empirical results demonstrate that this framework offers a robust and theoretically grounded alternative for complex RL tasks where the traditional formulation of the problem fails to induce the desired breadth of agent behaviour.

</details>


### [79] [Language Models Need Sleep: Learning to Self-Modify and Consolidate Memories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03979v2)
*Ali Behrouz,Farnoosh Hashemi,Adel Javanmard,Vahab Mirrokni*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 睡眠范式实现记忆巩固与自我改进，对agent持续学习有启发

TL;DR: 受人类睡眠启发，提出一种包含记忆巩固和梦境两个阶段的睡眠范式，使模型能持续学习、蒸馏短期记忆为长期知识并自我改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型缺乏持续学习能力，无法将短期上下文知识有效迁移到长期参数中。

Method: 睡眠范式包含两个阶段：（1）记忆巩固：通过知识播种（在线蒸馏+强化学习模仿学习）将小模型记忆蒸馏到大模型；（2）梦境：使用强化学习生成合成数据课程进行自我改进。

Result: 在长视野、持续学习、知识整合和少样本泛化任务上验证了睡眠阶段的重要性。

Conclusion: 睡眠阶段对于模型持续学习和知识迁移至关重要。

中文摘要：过去几十年见证了机器学习算法设计的显著进步，从早期针对特定任务的浅层模型到更通用的深度大语言模型（LLMs）。尽管在需要即时预测或上下文学习的任务中显示出有希望的结果，现有模型缺乏持续学习并有效将其时间性上下文知识转移到长期参数的能力。受人类学习过程的启发，我们引入了一种“睡眠”范式，允许模型持续学习，通过重放将其短期脆弱记忆蒸馏为稳定的长期知识，并通过“梦境”过程递归地自我改进。更具体地说，睡眠包括两个阶段：（1）记忆巩固：一个向上的蒸馏过程，称为知识播种，其中较小自我的记忆被蒸馏到更大的网络中，以提供更多容量同时保留知识。作为概念验证，我们提出了一种新的广义蒸馏过程用于知识播种（即在线蒸馏与基于强化学习的模仿学习的结合）；（2）梦境：一个自我改进阶段，其中模型使用强化学习生成合成数据的课程，以排练新知识并完善现有能力，无需人类监督。我们在长视野、持续学习、知识整合和少样本泛化任务上的实验支持了睡眠阶段的重要性。

Original abstract: The past few decades have witnessed significant advances in the design of machine learning algorithms, from early studies on task-specific shallow models to more general deep Large Language Models (LLMs). Despite showing promising results in tasks that require instant prediction or in-context learning, existing models lack the ability to continually learn and effectively transfer their temporal in-context knowledge to their long-term parameters. Inspired by human learning process, we introduce a ''Sleep'' paradigm that allows the models to continually learn, distill their short-term fragile memories into stable long-term knowledge with replay, and recursively improve themselves with ''Dreaming'' process. In more detail, sleep consists of two stages: (1) Memory Consolidation: an upward distillation process, called Knowledge Seeding, where the memories of a smaller-self are distilled into a larger network to provide more capacity while preserving the knowledge. As a proof of concept, we present a new Generalized Distillation process for {Knowledge Seeding} (i.e., the combination of on-policy distillation with Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based imitation learning); (2) Dreaming: a self-improvement phase, where the model uses RL to generate a curriculum of synthetic data to rehearse new knowledge and refine existing capabilities without human supervision. Our experiments on long-horizon, continual learning, knowledge incorporation, and few-shot generalization tasks support the importance of the sleep stage.

</details>


### [80] [EvalStop: Using World Feedback to Detect and Correct Reward Overoptimization in Multi-Tenant RLHF Platforms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04145v3)
*Guilin Zhang,Chuanyi Sun,Kai Zhao,Xu Chu,Shahryar Sarkani,John M. Fossaceca*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RLHF奖励过度优化检测，对agent训练监控有启发

TL;DR: 提出EvalStop调度原语，通过检测评估分数连续下降来早停奖励作弊的RLHF作业，显著提高资源利用率并兼容多种基础调度器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有云LLM微调平台调度器忽略奖励过度优化现象，导致资源浪费和作业质量下降，亟需一种能自动检测并终止奖励作弊作业的调度机制。

Method: 提出EvalStop，一种可组合的调度原语，当作业连续k次评估分数下降时终止作业、释放GPU并保留最佳检查点，可委托给任何基础调度器，将早停问题建模为检测问题。

Result: 在80% RLHF工作负载、64 GPU场景下，EvalStop实现精确率98%、召回率99%、假阳性率1.5%，JCT提升9%，浪费计算减少22%；在噪声和作弊比例变化下保持高检测质量。

Conclusion: EvalStop有效解决了RLHF工作负载中的奖励过度优化问题，具有高检测精度和鲁棒性，可以轻松集成到现有调度器中，提升系统整体效率。

中文摘要：云上的LLM微调平台越来越多地服务于RLHF工作负载，其中学习得到的奖励模型被优化作为人类质量的代理。正如Gao等人(2023)所示，在持续的优化压力下，这个代理会偏离世界反馈（下游评估指标），这种现象被称为奖励过度优化。现有的平台调度器忽略了这种偏离：非先知调度器在没有任何质量信号的情况下优化JCT；SLAQ风格的质量感知调度器使用训练损失（通过作弊单调下降的更弱代理）；经典的按作业早停需要人工监控且不会释放共享GPU。我们提出EvalStop，一个可组合的调度原语，它在连续k次评估分数下降时终止作业，释放GPU，保留最佳检查点，并委托给任何基础调度器。我们将调度器级别的早停视为一个检测问题，并在一个离散事件模拟器中进行评估，该模拟器的RLHF工作负载混合了奖励作弊和结构健康的运行，真实标签对调度器隐藏。在RLHF-heavy工作负载（80% RLHF，64 GPU）上，EvalStop实现了98%的精确率、99%的召回率、1.5%的假阳性率，同时将JCT提高了9%，并将浪费的计算减少了22%，相比于SRTF-Est（p<0.05）。简单的固定进度和损失平台竞争者要么在健康的RLHF上产生65%的FPR，要么错过超过一半的真实作弊案例。收益在所有测试的基础调度器上组成（9-25% JCT），并且在评估噪声（噪声标准差<=0.05时精确率至少91%）和作弊基础率（20-80%作弊比例下精确率至少89%）下检测质量保持稳定。

Original abstract: Cloud LLM fine-tuning platforms increasingly serve RLHF workloads, where a learned reward model is optimized as a proxy for human quality. As Gao et al. (2023) showed, this proxy diverges from world feedback (downstream eval metrics) under sustained optimization pressure, a phenomenon known as reward overoptimization. Existing platform schedulers ignore this divergence: non-clairvoyant schedulers optimize JCT without any quality signal, SLAQ-style quality-aware schedulers use training loss (a weaker proxy that drops monotonically through hacking), and classical per-job early stopping requires human monitoring and does not free shared GPUs. We propose EvalStop, a composable scheduling primitive that terminates jobs on k consecutive eval-score declines, releases GPUs, preserves the best checkpoint, and delegates to any base scheduler. We frame scheduler-level early stopping as a detection problem and evaluate it in a discrete-event simulator whose RLHF workload mixes reward-hacking and structurally healthy runs, with ground-truth labels hidden from schedulers. On RLHF-heavy workloads (80% RLHF, 64 GPUs), EvalStop achieves precision 98% / recall 99% / FPR 1.5% while improving JCT by 9% and cutting wasted compute by 22% over SRTF-Est (p<0.05). Trivial fixed-progress and loss-plateau competitors either incur 65% FPR on healthy RLHF or miss over half of true hacking cases. Gains compose across every base scheduler tested (9-25% JCT) and detection quality stays stable under eval noise (precision at least 91% at noise std <= 0.05) and hacking base rate (precision at least 89% across 20-80% hacking fractions).

</details>


### [81] [Exact Unlearning in Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04182v1)
*Thanh Nguyen-Tang,Raman Arora*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL精确遗忘，提供通用训练机制可迁移至agent学习

TL;DR: 本文提出了强化学习中的精确遗忘问题，并给出了一个近乎最优的ρ-TV稳定算法及其遗憾界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着数据隐私法规（如GDPR）的实施，用户有权要求删除其数据，因此需要设计强化学习算法，能够在删除用户数据后使学习器的输出与从未见过该用户数据时不可区分，同时保持计算高效。

Method: 本文定义了ρ-TV稳定性概念，并针对表格型马尔可夫决策过程构造了一个满足ρ-TV稳定的强化学习算法，该算法支持精确遗忘，且期望计算成本仅为重新训练成本的ρ√(ln T)分之一。

Result: 该算法实现了遗憾界O(H^2 √(SAT) + H^3 S^2 A + H^{2.5} S^2 A/ρ)，并建立了下界Ω(H√(SAT) + SAH/ρ)，证明算法几乎极小化最优。

Conclusion: 本文表明，所提出的ρ-TV稳定强化学习算法在精确遗忘场景下几乎是极小化最优的，为隐私保护下的在线学习提供了理论基础。

中文摘要：我们提出了强化学习中的“精确遗忘”问题，其目标是设计一个高效框架，使得在收到删除请求后能够移除任意用户的数据，即在线学习者在遗忘后的输出与假设被删除用户从未与学习者交互时所产生的输出是“不可区分的”。对于任意ρ>0，我们证明存在一个强化学习算法是ρ-TV稳定的，并且支持一个精确遗忘过程，其期望计算成本仅为从头重新训练的计算成本的ρ√(ln T)分之一。我们为表格型马尔可夫决策过程构造了这样一个ρ-TV稳定的强化学习算法，其遗憾界为O(H^2 √(SAT) + H^3 S^2 A + H^{2.5} S^2 A/ρ)，其中S、A、H和T分别表示状态数、动作数、回合长度和回合数。我们还为ρ-TV稳定的强化学习算法建立了一个下界Ω(H√(SAT) + SAH/ρ)，表明我们的算法几乎是极小化最优的。

Original abstract: We formulate the problem of \emph{exact unlearning} in reinforcement learning, where the goal is to design an efficient framework that enables the removal of any user's data upon deletion request, i.e., the online learner's output after unlearning is \emph{indistinguishable} from what would have been produced had the deleted user never interacted with the learner. For any $ρ>0$, we show that there exists a reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that is $ρ$-TV-stable and supports an exact unlearning procedure whose expected computational cost is only a $ρ\sqrt{\ln T}$ fraction of the computational cost of retraining from scratch. We construct such a $ρ$-TV-stable RL algorithm for tabular Markov decision processes (MDPs), which achieves a regret bound of $\mathcal{O}(H^2 \sqrt{SAT} + H^3 S^2 A + {H^{2.5} S^2 A}/ρ)$, where $S, A, H$, and $T$ denote the number of states, the number of actions, the episode horizon, and the number of episodes, respectively. We also establish a lower bound of $Ω(H\sqrt{\!SAT}\! +\! {SAH}/ρ)$ for $ρ$-TV-stable RL algorithms, showing that our algorithm is nearly minimax optimal.

</details>


### [82] [Dual Advantage Fields](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04188v1)
*Alexey Zemtsov,Maxim Bobrin,Alexander Nikulin,Dmitry V. Dylov,Fakhri Karray,Vladislav Kurenkov,Martin Takáč,Arip Asadulaev*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 离线RL策略提取方法，对agent优化有潜在启发

TL;DR: 本文提出双重优势场（DAF），通过将双线性双重值模型转化为局部优势信号，实现离线目标条件强化学习的策略提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线目标条件强化学习需要同时考虑长期可达性和局部动作选择，但现有双重表示仅捕获全局可达性，缺乏局部动作偏好信息。

Method: DAF利用双线性双重参数化，学习动作效果模型预测折扣特征位移，并通过位移与目标方向的对齐程度为动作评分，等价于目标条件贝尔曼优势。

Result: 在OGBench的多种任务上，DAF改善了聚合RLiable指标，尤其在局部正确动作偏离直接朝向最终目标的场景中表现优异。

Conclusion: DAF有效结合了全局可达性和局部优势，为离线目标条件强化学习提供了可靠的策略提取方法。

中文摘要：离线目标条件强化学习需要长期可达性估计和局部动作比较。双重目标表示提供了捕获全局目标可达性的值场，但它们没有直接指定在给定状态下应优先选择哪个动作。我们提出了双重优势场（Dual Advantage Fields），这是一种策略提取方法，将双线性双重值模型转化为局部优势信号。在双线性双重参数化下，目标嵌入是值场相对于状态表示的梯度。DAF学习一个动作效果模型，该模型预测动作引起的折扣特征位移，并通过该位移与目标方向的对齐程度对动作进行评分。在可实现的情况下，该分数等于目标条件的贝尔曼优势，从而提供了标准的局部策略改进保证。在OGBench的 locomotion、manipulation和puzzle任务中，DAF改善了聚合的RLiable指标，并在局部正确动作与直接朝向最终目标的运动不同的设置中表现强劲。

Original abstract: Offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning requires both long-horizon reachability estimates and local action comparisons. Dual goal representations provide value fields that capture global goal reachability, but they do not directly specify which action should be preferred at a given state. We propose Dual Advantage Fields, a policy-extraction method that turns a bilinear dual value model into a local advantage signal. Under bilinear dual parameterization, the goal embedding is the gradient of the value field with respect to the state representation. DAF learns an action-effect model that predicts the discounted feature displacement induced by an action and scores actions by the alignment between this displacement and the goal direction. In the realizable case, this score equals the goal-conditioned Bellman advantage, yielding a standard local policy-improvement guarantee. On OGBench locomotion, manipulation, and puzzle tasks, DAF improves aggregate RLiable metrics and performs strongly in settings where locally correct actions differ from direct movement toward the final goal.

</details>

### [83] [Auditing LLM-Governed Social Robots with Culture-Specific Moral Gradients](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28345v1)
*Carmen Ng,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: LLM机器人道德审计框架，涉及代理安全评测，有通用启发

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于梯度的多语言审计框架，用于评估大语言模型在社交机器人优先帮助决策中的道德权衡行为，发现跨文化梯度追踪失败，提示效果有限，模型因素更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM道德审计以英语为中心，缺乏对具身情境和文化多元性的考虑，可能导致部署中的不平等。需要多语言、文化敏感的审计方法来诊断和校准LLM在社交机器人中的道德决策。

Method: 基于九篇社交机器人综述提取对称控制场景，将道德机器实验范式转化为“优先帮助”困境；审计4个LLM在4种语言-国家对和4种提示模式下共57,600个决策，以国家特定偏好梯度为基准，使用序数一致性检验和文化治理类型分类。

Result: LLM存在持续且文化不对称的梯度追踪失败：西方语言决策质量控制优于中日文；多数优先权衡中高确定性消除跨文化梯度；对年龄和地位敏感但可能边缘化少数；提示改进效果不均，仅对比性示例有效，推理提示可能恶化。

Conclusion: 多语言、多元审计应作为LLM-机器人部署前的必要关卡，模型因素的改进比提示工程更可靠。

中文摘要：由大语言模型治理的社交机器人越来越多地决定谁先获得现实世界中的帮助。由于不同文化在年龄、地位和群体规模方面的优先处理规范存在差异，未能多元校准可能会扩大不平等。然而，大语言模型的道德审计仍以英语为中心，很少测试具身情境，这使得多元校准在LLM-机器人部署日益加剧的背景下成为一个紧迫的诊断缺口。我们引入了一个基于梯度的审计框架，用于对LLM道德权衡行为进行多语言评估，并对照文化偏好梯度。基于九篇跨领域社交机器人综述（>8000篇论文），我们设计了在护理、教育和服务领域对称控制的场景，将“道德机器实验”中的“该救谁”转化为“该先帮助谁”的困境，并保留了身份权衡（多数与少数；年轻与年长；高地位与低地位）。我们在四种提示模式下（57,600个决策）对四个LLM进行了四种国家-语言对的审计，并以特定国家的MME偏好梯度为基准。序数一致性测试模型是否区分文化背景；治理类型映射了梯度区分、方向倾向和深思熟虑中的脆弱性。我们发现存在持续且文化不对称的梯度追踪失败，仅靠提示无法可靠纠正：质量控制对西方语言决策的强度几乎是对中文和日文的两倍；在多数优先的权衡中，高确定性常常消除跨文化梯度；对基于年龄和地位的规范的局部敏感性可能使少数群体边缘化。提示效果不均匀；只有对比性示例才能带来一致的改进，而仅推理的提示可能恶化追踪。我们的结果促使多语言、多元审计作为LLM-机器人部署前的关卡，并表明模型因素比仅靠提示更稳健的杠杆。

Original abstract: LLM-governed social robots increasingly decide who receives real-world assistance first. As prioritization norms vary across cultures by age, status, and group size, failure to calibrate pluralistically can scale into unequal access. Yet LLM moral audits remain English-centered, rarely test embodied contexts, leaving pluralistic calibration as an urgent diagnostic gap amid intensifying LLM-robot deployment. We introduce a gradient-based audit framework for multilingual evaluation of LLM moral trade-off behavior against cultural preference gradients. Grounded in nine cross-domain social robotics reviews (>8,000 papers), we derive symmetry-controlled scenarios across care, education, and services, translating the Moral Machine Experiment's "whom to spare" into "whom to assist first" dilemmas with preserved identity trade-offs (many vs. few; young vs. old; higher vs. lower status). We audit four LLMs across four country-language pairs in four prompting regimes (57,600 decisions), benchmarked against country-specific MME preference gradients. Ordinal concordance tests whether models differentiate cultural contexts; a governance typology maps vulnerabilities in gradient differentiation, directional tendency, and deliberation. We find persistent, culturally asymmetric gradient tracking failures that prompting alone cannot reliably correct: quality calibration is nearly twice as strong for Western-language decisions as for Chinese and Japanese; high determinism in majority-first trade-offs often erases cross-cultural gradients; partial sensitivity to age- and status-based norms risks sidelining minorities. Prompting effects are uneven; only contrastive exemplars yield consistent gains, while reasoning-only prompts can worsen tracking. Our results motivate multilingual, pluralistic audits as an LLM-robot pre-deployment gate and suggest model factors are a more robust lever than prompting alone.

</details>


### [84] [AgenticRL: Self-Refining Agentic Reinforcement Learning for Vision-Conditioned UAV Navigation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03963v3)
*Roohan Ahmed Khan,Yasheerah Yaqoot,Amir Atef Habel,Muhammad Ahsan Mustafa,Dzmitry Tsetserukou*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 使用GPT agent闭环自我改进奖励与策略，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: AgenticRL uses a multimodal GPT agent to automatically design reward functions, train policies, and refine them via closed-loop feedback for UAV navigation, achieving 71% improvement and 91% real-world success rate.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current deep RL for navigation relies heavily on manual reward design and fine-tuning, which is time-consuming and often ineffective, motivating the need for more autonomous reward generation and policy refinement.

Method: AgenticRL employs a multimodal GPT agent to interpret task and visual inputs, generate reward functions, train policies with PPO, evaluate via diagnosis packets, and iteratively refine rewards. During inference, it uses real-world images and language to select policies.

Result: Closed-loop refinement improved policy behavior by 71% over initial rewards. Sim-to-real transfer achieved 91% real-world success rate and 94% sim-to-real accuracy.

Conclusion: AgenticRL demonstrates that an agent-guided closed-loop system can significantly enhance autonomy and performance in deep RL for UAV navigation, effectively bridging the sim-to-real gap.

中文摘要：深度强化学习在使自主机器人学习复杂导航任务方面显示出巨大潜力。然而，其实用性仍严重依赖于人为设计的奖励函数和反复的手动微调，这既耗时又无法保证在目标任务中取得高成功率。本文提出了AgenticRL，一种智能体引导的强化学习框架，旨在提高无人机导航任务中奖励设计、策略优化和实际部署的自主性。AgenticRL利用多模态生成预训练Transformer（GPT）智能体来解读任务信息和视觉场景观察，生成任务特定的奖励函数，使用近端策略优化（PPO）算法训练策略，然后通过诊断包评估训练后的策略并生成反馈，充当批评者的角色。基于此反馈，智能体识别失败模式并在闭环自我改进过程中优化奖励函数。为了在推理过程中进一步利用多模态GPT智能体，AgenticRL使用真实世界图像和自然语言任务信息自动识别当前场景并选择合适的训练策略执行。该框架在多项导航任务上进行了评估，包括门穿越、避障、穿墙着陆、轨迹跟踪和运动行为学习。实验结果表明，闭环优化过程相比初始奖励策略行为提升了71%。我们还展示了所提出框架的仿真到现实迁移，实现了91%的真实世界成功率和94%的仿真到现实准确率。

Original abstract: Deep reinforcement learning has shown strong potential for enabling autonomous robots to learn complex navigational tasks. However, its practical use still depends heavily on human designed reward functions and repeated manual fine tuning, which is time consuming and does not guarantee high success in the desired task. This paper presents AgenticRL, agent guided reinforcement learning framework that increases autonomy in reward design, policy refinement, and real world deployment for unmanned aerial vehicles (UAV) navigation tasks. AgenticRL uses a multimodal generative pre-trained transformer (GPT) agent to interpret task information and visual scene observations, generate task specific reward functions, train policies using Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) algorithm, and then act as a critic by evaluating the trained policy through diagnosis packets to generate feedback. Based on this feedback, the agent identifies failure modes and refines the reward function in a closed loop self improvement process. To further leverage the multimodal GPT agent during inference, AgenticRL uses real world images and natural language task information to automatically identify the active scenario and select the appropriate trained policy for execution. The framework is evaluated on multiple navigational tasks, including gate traversal, obstacle avoidance, wall barrier crossing with landing, trajectory following, and motion behavior learning. Experimental results show that the closed loop refinement process improves policy behavior compared with initial rewards by 71%. We also demonstrate sim-to-real transfer of the proposed framework, achieving a real world success rate of 91% and a sim-to-real accuracy of 94%.

</details>


### [85] [PerceptTwin: Semantic Scene Reconstruction for Iterative LLM Planning and Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04226v1)
*Charlie Gauthier,Sacha Morin,Liam Paull*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 利用语义场景重建和LLM judge进行规划验证，对agent规划迭代与验证有启发。

TL;DR: PerceptTwin是一个全自动流水线，能从机器人感知的语义场景表示构建交互式仿真，通过LLM规划器反馈提高计划成功率和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上创建机器人仿真环境是繁重的，无法为每个环境定制，因此需要一种自动化的方法从机器人感知直接生成仿真。

Method: 提出PerceptTwin流水线，结合开放词汇对象地图、3D资产生成、技能先决条件预测和常识条件检查，并引入LLM评判器验证计划对齐。

Result: PerceptTwin使GPT系列规划器的计划成功率平均提高约39%，并使人类计划验证准确率提高高达18%。

Conclusion: 从机器人感知进行开放词汇场景仿真有潜力作为更安全、更可靠的机器人规划基础。

中文摘要：仿真环境对于机器人策略学习和规划验证与确认都很有用。传统上，创建仿真的过程是繁重的。为机器人将要运行的每个单独环境创建定制的仿真环境是不可行的。在这项工作中，我们介绍了PerceptTwin，这是一个全自动流水线，它直接从机器人感知栈产生的语义场景表示构建交互式仿真。PerceptTwin结合了开放词汇对象地图与3D资产生成、技能先决条件预测和常识条件检查。这些交互式仿真可用于在机器人硬件上执行计划之前验证和完善计划。借鉴AI对齐文献，我们还引入了一个LLM评判器，用于验证计划的正确性和与人类偏好的一致性。实验表明，PerceptTwin反馈使LLM规划器能够完善计划、提高安全性并抵抗有害的黑盒提示攻击。在我们的任务套件中，PerceptTwin对GPT5、GPT5Mini和GPT5Nano规划器的计划成功率平均提高了约39%。此外，对于因未满足技能先决条件而失败的计划，PerceptTwin还使人类计划验证平均提高了高达18%。我们的结果证明了从机器人感知进行开放词汇场景仿真作为更安全、更可靠的机器人规划基础的潜力。

Original abstract: Simulation environments are useful for both robot policy learning and planning verification and validation. Traditionally, the process of creating a simulation was onerous. Creating a bespoke simulation environment for each individual environment that a robot would operate in was simply infeasible. In this work, we introduce PerceptTwin, a fully automatic pipeline that constructs interactive simulations directly from semantic scene representations produced by a robot's perception stack. PerceptTwin combines open-vocabulary object maps with 3D asset generation, affordance prediction, and commonsense condition checking. These interactive simulations can be used to validate and refine plans before they are executed on the robot hardware. Borrowing from the AI alignment literature, we also introduce an LLM judge that verifies plan correctness and alignment with human preferences. Experiments show that PerceptTwin feedback allows LLM planners to refine plans, enhance safety, and resist harmful black-box prompting attacks. In our suite of tasks, PerceptTwin improves plan success by an average of approximately 39% for GPT5, GPT5Mini, and GPT5Nano planners. Additionally, PerceptTwin also improves human plan verification by up to 18% on average for plans that fail due to unfilled skill preconditions. Our results demonstrate the potential of open-vocabulary scene simulation from robot perception as a foundation for safer, more reliable robot planning.

</details>

### [86] [Semantic Constraint Synthesis for Adaptive Trajectory Optimization via Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04123v1)
*Eleanor Brosius,Yuji Takubo,Daniele Gammelli,Simone D'Amico,Marco Pavone*

Main category: math.OC

Selection reason: LLM将自然语言转为优化代码，直接相关自动代码优化

TL;DR: 利用大语言模型将自然语言任务描述自动转化为轨迹优化代码和数学公式，并在航天器交会场景中实现高成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太空任务日益频繁复杂，将任务意图转化为数学上合理的轨迹优化问题需要大量专业知识，缺乏自动化工具。

Method: 提出一个利用大语言模型（LLMs）的框架，将自然语言描述的任务要求和约束转化为可执行的轨迹优化代码和数学公式。

Result: 在航天器交会场景中，从语义任务需求重构凸轨迹优化问题获得高成功率。

Conclusion: LLMs能够弥合高层意图与形式化优化模型之间的鸿沟，实现更灵活高效的航天器轨迹设计。

中文摘要：轨迹优化是实现太空探索中安全可靠自主操作的关键组成部分。随着太空任务在频率、复杂性和范围上的增加，迫切需要快速制定数学上合理的轨迹优化问题，以准确反映任务目标和操作约束。然而，将任务意图转化为可处理的轨迹优化分析公式需要大量的领域专业知识。本文提出了一个框架，利用大型语言模型（LLMs）将任务要求和约束的自然语言描述转化为可执行的轨迹优化代码及相应的数学公式。在航天器交会场景中的实验表明，从语义任务需求中重构凸轨迹优化问题的成功率很高。最终，这项工作凸显了LLMs在连接高层意图与形式化优化模型方面的潜力，从而实现更灵活、更高效的航天器轨迹设计。

Original abstract: Trajectory optimization is a critical component for enabling safe and reliable autonomous operations in space exploration. As space missions increase in frequency, complexity, and scope, there is a growing need to rapidly formulate mathematically sound trajectory optimization problems that accurately reflect mission objectives and operational constraints. However, translating mission intent into tractable analytical formulations for trajectory optimization requires substantial domain expertise. This paper presents a framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to translate natural language descriptions of mission requirements and constraints into executable trajectory optimization code and corresponding mathematical formulations. Experiments in spacecraft rendezvous scenarios demonstrate a high success rate in reconditioning a convex trajectory optimization problem from semantic mission requirements. Ultimately, this work highlights the potential of LLMs to bridge high-level intent and formal optimization models, enabling more flexible and efficient trajectory design of spacecraft.

### [87] [veriFIRE: an Industrial Case Study in Verifying Consistency Properties for a DNN-Based Wildfire Detection System](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04121v1)
*Idan Refaeli,Maya Swisa,Itay Buchnik,Alon Zada,Guy Amir,Elad Mandelbaum,Ziv Freund,Guy Katz*

Main category: cs.LO

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出端到端方法验证野火检测无人机系统中深层神经网络的单调性和有界模糊响应属性，实验显示单调性易验证而模糊鲁棒性仍具挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提高安全关键系统中深度神经网络可靠性，弥合实际应用与验证技术之间的差距。

Method: 将应用需求（如单调性和有界模糊响应）编码为神经网络验证器可处理的查询，使用现有后端（如Marabou等）求解。

Result: 单调性属性全部在5分钟内解决；有界模糊响应属性验证难度大，凸显高维规格挑战。

Conclusion: 验证可为工业系统提供有意义的领域特定保证，但高维属性仍需可扩展性改进。

中文摘要：我们介绍了veriFIRE项目的持续工作：一个工业界和学术界的合作项目，旨在应用验证来提高一个真实世界安全关键系统的可靠性。具体来说，我们针对一个用于野火检测的机载平台，该平台包含两个深度神经网络。我们提出了一种端到端的方法来验证该系统中的一致性属性。我们的方法将基于应用的需求编码为现有神经网络验证器可处理的查询。我们研究了关键操作场景下的感兴趣属性：（i）检测器置信度随目标强度增加而单调性；（ii）在传感器物理合理模糊下有界的检测器响应。我们使用最先进的神经网络验证后端实例化这些编码，并在真实背景样本上大规模评估。对于第一个属性，所有验证查询在五分钟内解决。对于第二个属性，验证本质上更难，凸显了更丰富、更高维度规格的可扩展性挑战。总体而言，结果表明可以为工业系统获得有意义的领域特定保证。

Original abstract: We present our ongoing work on the veriFIRE project: a collaboration between industry and academia, aimed at applying verification to increase the reliability of a real-world, safety-critical system. Specifically, we target an airborne platform for wildfire detection, which incorporates two deep neural networks. We present an end-to-end methodology for verifying \textit{consistency properties} in this system. Our approach encodes application-grounded requirements into solver-compatible queries for existing neural network verifiers. We study properties of interest over critical operational scenarios: (i) monotonicity of detector confidence as target intensity increases; and (ii) bounded detector response under physically plausible blur over the sensor. We instantiate these encodings using state-of-the-art neural network verification backends and evaluate them at scale on real background samples. For the first property, all verification queries are solved in under five minutes. For the second property, verification is substantially harder, highlighting key scalability challenges for richer, higher-dimensional specifications. Overall, the results demonstrate that meaningful, domain-specific guarantees can be obtained for industrial systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态用户界面工具包缺乏系统的比较方法，现有工具包在功能、开发工作量和评估策略上难以统一衡量。

Method: 通过文档分析、技术比较和未来开发者评估，构建围绕模态覆盖、开发者体验和实验支持三个维度的基准测试框架，并以五个代表性工具包进行示例。

Conclusion: 该框架填补了多模态工具包系统性比较的空白，为后续实证研究和工具开发提供了统一评估基础。

中文摘要：多模态用户界面日益结合语音、手势、视觉、视线、触摸、生物信号及其他传感器数据。过去五年中的最新工具包，如Geno、Multisensor-Pipeline (MSP)、ReactGenie和EmoSync，旨在让开发者更容易地原型化此类界面，而早期工作如WAMI则展示了基于网络的多模态系统是如何构想的。然而，该领域仍然缺乏一种系统且可复用的方式来比较这些工具包实际支持的功能、它们为开发者减轻了多少实现工作，以及哪些评估策略适用于它们。本文将一份人机交互研讨会草稿重构为一篇针对多模态用户界面工具包的基准测试框架论文。本文未报告完成的实证结果，而是提出了一种基于文档分析、技术比较和未来开发者评估的结构化基准测试。该框架围绕三个维度组织：模态覆盖与交互抽象、开发者体验与工作流、实验与集成支持。本文通过五个代表性工具包（Geno、MSP、ReactGenie、WAMI和EmoSync）展示了该框架。贡献在于提供了一个可复用的基准测试模板，未来研究者可通过实证测量、开发者研究和额外的多模态工具包对其进行实例化。

Original abstract: Multimodal user interfaces increasingly combine speech, gesture, vision, gaze, touch, biosignals, and other sensor data. Recent toolkits from the past five years, such as Geno, Multisensor-Pipeline (MSP), ReactGenie, and EmoSync, aim to make it easier for developers to prototype such interfaces, while older work such as WAMI shows how early web-based multimodal systems were conceived. Yet the field still lacks a systematic and reusable way to compare what these toolkits actually support, how much implementation work they offload from developers, and which evaluation strategies are appropriate for them. This paper reframes an HCI seminar draft into a benchmarking framework paper for multimodal user interface toolkits. Rather than reporting completed empirical results, it proposes a structured benchmark based on document analysis, technical comparison, and a future developer-based evaluation. The framework is organized around three dimensions: modality coverage and interaction abstraction, developer experience and workflow, and experimental and integration support. The paper illustrates the framework through five representative toolkits: Geno, MSP, ReactGenie, WAMI, and EmoSync. The contribution is a reusable benchmark template that future researchers can instantiate with empirical measurements, developer studies, and additional multimodal toolkits.

### [89] [A Practice Auditing Framework for Large Language Model Use: Collective Empiricism, Pseudo-Rational Cognition, and Governance of AI-Generated Content](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01248v1)
*Yang Zhao,Yingshuo Li,Zeyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: LLM审计框架，涉及agent-based automation，对agent安全有潜在启发

TL;DR: 提出了一个实践审计框架，用于应对LLM使用中的认知风险，包括伪理性认知、主观性幻觉和记忆污染等问题，通过集体经验主义和一系列审计步骤确保输出可验证和可干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户在使用LLM获取结构化答案时可能缺乏足够领域实践，导致将AI生成内容误认为是自己的理性理解，存在认知风险。

Method: 通过引入集体经验主义和伪理性认知概念，分析AI主观性幻觉、主观性结构、模板循环、统计误判和记忆污染等风险，并设计基于需求定义、边界识别、证据审计、实践验证、反向质疑、日志记录、版本管理和回滚的审计流程。

Result: 提出了一个概念性和可审计的框架，用于治理LLM交互中的认知风险，确保输出可验证、可复现和可干预。

Conclusion: 该框架不拒绝AI生产力，而是强调应通过实践审计将LLM输出纳入可控过程，降低认知风险，适用于LLM使用、AIGC治理和人类-AI交互场景。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地用于知识获取、代码生成、学术写作和基于代理的自动化。在这些场景中，用户可能在没有充分领域实践的情况下获得高度结构化的答案、计划和判断。本文提出了一种用于LLM使用和AI生成内容治理的实践审计框架。它引入了集体经验主义来描述LLM如何将大规模人类经验压缩和重组为看似经验性和理性的输出，以及伪理性认知来描述用户如何可能将AI生成的结构化表达误认为是自己的理性理解。本文分析了AI主观性幻觉、输入材料中的主观性结构、AI-AI对话中的模板循环、AIGC检测中的统计误判，以及生成内容进入未来上下文、长期记忆、检索空间或代理技能系统时产生的记忆污染。为降低这些风险，本文提出了一种基于需求定义、问题边界识别、证据源审计、实践验证、反向质疑、日志记录、版本管理、回滚和重新认知的审计过程。该框架不拒绝AI生产力；它主张LLM输出应回归到可验证、可复现和可干预的实践过程中。本文为LLM交互、AI生成内容治理、长期记忆系统和人类-AI交互中的认知风险提供了一个概念性和可审计的框架。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly used for knowledge acquisition, code generation, academic writing, and agent-based automation. In these settings, users may obtain highly structured answers, plans, and judgments without sufficient domain practice. This paper proposes a practice auditing framework for LLM use and AI-generated content governance. It introduces collective empiricism to describe how LLMs compress and reorganize large-scale human experience into outputs that appear empirical and rational, and pseudo-rational cognition to describe how users may mistake AI-generated structured expression for their own rational understanding. The paper analyzes AI subjectivity illusion, subjectivity structures in input materials, template loops in AI-AI conversations, statistical misjudgment in AIGC detection, and memory pollution when generated content enters future contexts, long-term memory, retrieval spaces, or agent skill systems. To reduce these risks, the paper proposes an auditing process based on requirement definition, problem-boundary identification, evidence-source auditing, practical validation, reverse questioning, logging, version management, rollback, and renewed cognition. The framework does not reject AI productivity; it argues that LLM outputs should be returned to verifiable, reproducible, and intervenable processes of practice. The paper provides a conceptual and auditable framework for cognitive risks in LLM interaction, AI-generated content governance, long-term memory systems, and human-AI interaction.

</details>


### [90] [Collaborative Disagreement Resolution for Scalable Oversight](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01251v1)
*Yuyang Jiang,Chacha Chen,Teng Wu,Liwen Sun,Han Liu,Shi Feng,Chenhao Tan*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: 提出协作式分歧消解替代辩论，提供多agent truth-seeking新范式，可迁移至coding agent的验证与评审。

TL;DR: 提出分歧解决范式，通过协作求真替代对抗辩论，在AI监督中提升非专家模型的判断准确率至62.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准辩论中模型被激励说服评判者，可能偏离认知诚实，需要一种更符合求真目标的交互机制。

Method: 借鉴人类调解原则，设计自动化流程引导模型协作识别分歧点、检验证据并收敛共识或隔离分歧关键点。

Result: 非专家模型在分歧解决下判断准确率达62.1%，显著高于标准辩论的49.2%。

Conclusion: 分歧解决为可扩展AI监督提供了有效替代方案，支持从对抗性到协作求真的范式转变。

中文摘要：辩论（即AI智能体就对立立场进行论证）已成为可扩展监督的关键方法。然而，辩论面临一个基本矛盾：模型被激励去说服评判者，而这可能并不总是与认知诚实一致。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种替代范式：分歧解决，它将交互机制从对抗性辩论重新定义为协作性求真。借鉴人类调解和冲突解决的原则（其中调解员促进对话以帮助争议方达成共识，而非在它们之间进行裁决），我们设计了一个自动化流程，将这些策略应用于AI监督。与标准辩论中模型为固定立场进行论证不同，我们的流程引导模型协作识别分歧点、检验相互矛盾的主张的证据，并朝着共识收敛或隔离它们分歧的具体“关键点”。我们发现，分歧解决始终帮助非专家模型识别真相，达到62.1%的判断准确率，而标准辩论为49.2%。我们的结果为重新思考从对抗性说服到协作求真的可扩展监督协议提供了令人鼓舞的实证证据。

Original abstract: Debate, where AI agents argue opposing positions, has emerged as a key approach to scalable oversight. However, debate faces a fundamental tension: models are incentivized to be persuasive to the judge, which may not always align with epistemic honesty. In this work, we propose an alternative paradigm: disagreement resolution, which reframes the interaction mechanism from adversarial debate to collaborative truth seeking. Drawing on principles from human mediation and conflict resolution, where mediators facilitate dialogue to help disputing parties reach consensus rather than adjudicating between them, we design an automated pipeline that adapts these strategies to AI oversight. Unlike standard debate where models argue for fixed positions, our pipeline directs models to collaboratively identify points of disagreement, examine the evidence for conflicting claims, and converge toward consensus or isolate the specific ''crux'' of their disagreement. We find that Disagreement Resolution consistently helps non-expert models identify the truth, achieving 62.1% judging accuracy compared to 49.2% for standard debate. Our results provide encouraging empirical evidence for rethinking the scalable oversight protocol from adversarial persuasion to collaborative truth-seeking.

</details>


### [91] [PySynthea: A Python-Native Framework for Scalable Synthetic Healthcare Data Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28346v1)
*Roberto Cruz,David Rey-Blanco*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PySynthea是Synthea的Python原生重实现，通过降低部署复杂度和集成主流数据科学生态系统，提升了合成医疗数据的可访问性和可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Synthea框架的部署复杂性和缺乏Python集成阻碍了研究人员和数据科学家使用合成医疗数据。

Method: 使用Python原生重新实现Synthea，提供模块化生成、可配置模拟管道，并支持标准医疗数据格式，与pandas和机器学习工作流无缝集成。

Result: PySynthea框架降低了操作复杂性，提高了可扩展性和互操作性，代码已在GitHub上开源。

Conclusion: PySynthea通过简化合成数据生成并融入Python生态系统，有望加速研究和应用AI开发中对合成医疗数据的采用。

中文摘要：合成医疗数据在研究和教育以及机器学习开发中日益重要，因为真实患者数据的访问受到隐私和治理限制。虽然Synthea提供了一个广泛采用的框架来生成逼真的纵向电子健康记录数据，但当前的实现由于部署复杂性和与现代Python工作流程的集成有限，给许多研究人员和数据科学家带来了采用障碍。本文介绍了PySynthea，一个Python原生重实现的Synthea，旨在提高科学Python生态系统内的可访问性、可扩展性和互操作性。该框架提供模块化的合成患者生成、可配置的医疗模拟流程，并支持标准医疗数据格式，同时与pandas和机器学习工作流等工具自然集成。通过降低操作复杂性并使合成数据生成与主流数据科学生态系统对齐，PySynthea旨在加速实验并拓宽合成医疗数据在研究和应用AI开发中的使用。代码托管在以下GitHub仓库：https://github.com/TIET-AI/tietai-synthea。

Original abstract: Synthetic healthcare data is increasingly important for research, education, and machine learning development where access to real patient data is limited by privacy and governance constraints. While Synthea provides a widely adopted framework for generating realistic longitudinal electronic health record data, its current implementation presents adoption barriers for many researchers and data scientists due to deployment complexity and limited integration with modern Python-based workflows.
  This paper introduces PySynthea, a Python-native reimplementation of Synthea designed to improve accessibility, extensibility, and interoperability within the scientific Python ecosystem. The framework provides modular synthetic patient generation, configurable healthcare simulation pipelines, and support for standard healthcare data formats while integrating naturally with tools such as pandas and machine learning workflows. By reducing operational complexity and aligning synthetic data generation with the dominant data science ecosystem, PySynthea aims to accelerate experimentation and broaden the use of synthetic healthcare data in research and applied AI development. The code in this github repository https://github.com/TIET-AI/tietai-synthea.

</details>


### [92] [Agentic Safety is an Epistemic Property, Not a Behavioral One](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28347v1)
*Charles L. Wang,Keir Dorchen,Peter Jin*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: 将agent安全视为可教性属性，对agent设计与安全控制有启发

TL;DR: 本文提出AI安全应从行为快照转向关注系统的可教性，即保留未来纠正能力的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI安全方法主要认证系统行为的快照，但随着AI系统变得更动态和自我改进，需要关注其长期可纠正性。

Method: 概念论证，定义可教性为在有限干预下保持未来纠正能力的属性，分析系统可能侵蚀纠正条件的方式。

Result: 论证了先进的AI系统可能在保持表面能力的同时破坏未来可纠正性，强调可教性的必要性。

Conclusion: 安全的先进AI系统必须不仅在当前行为可接受，而且要在未来保持可教性。

中文摘要：现代人工智能安全涵盖了预训练干预、后训练对齐、部署时控制、监控和红队测试。这些方法是必要的，但它们主要认证系统行为的快照。随着AI系统变得更有能力、动态、具身化和自我改进，这种快照视角变得不完整：安全不仅取决于系统当前的行为是否可接受，还取决于它在学习、适应、行动和自我修改的过程中是否保持可纠正性。本文认为，安全因此应被视为一个 evolving learner 的认知属性，而不仅仅是当前策略的行为属性。我们引入了“可教性”作为在有限的人类、机构或环境干预下保持未来纠正能力的能力。我们认为，先进的系统可以保留可见的能力，同时侵蚀未来纠正所需的表征、算法或元决策条件。安全的先进AI系统不仅必须当前行为可接受；它们必须在之后保持可教性。

Original abstract: Contemporary AI safety spans pre-training interventions, post-training alignment, deployment-time controls, monitoring, and red-teaming. These methods are necessary, but they primarily certify snapshots of system behavior. As AI systems become more capable, dynamic, embodied, and self-improving, this snapshot view becomes incomplete: safety depends not only on whether a system behaves acceptably now, but whether it remains correctable as it learns, adapts, acts, and modifies itself over time. This paper argues that safety should therefore be treated as an epistemic property of the evolving learner, not merely a behavioral property of the current policy. We introduce teachability as the capacity to preserve future corrective leverage under bounded human, institutional, or environmental intervention. We argue that advanced systems can retain visible competence while eroding the representational, algorithmic, or meta-decision conditions needed for future correction. Safe advanced AI systems must not only behave acceptably now; they must remain teachable later.

</details>

### [93] [Capability Advertisement as a Market for Lemons: A Trust Layer for Heterogeneous Agent Networks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03034v1)
*Gaurav Naresh Mittal*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent信任层与能力公告市场分析，对agent协作设计有启发

TL;DR: LLM代理间的委托存在“柠檬市场”问题（能力隐藏且声称不可信），本文提出信任层（Trust Layer）通过概率描述、筛选和声誉机制实现分离均衡，无需重训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理协议（如MCP、A2A）假设代理能力是静态、真实的事实，但实际代理能力具有概率性、可漂移且常自信地错误，导致调用者无法区分可靠与不可靠提供者，形成类似“柠檬市场”的低信任均衡。

Method: 通过构建柠檬市场模型分析问题，提出信任层（Trust Layer）：在MCP和A2A之上添加概率能力描述、筛选和声誉机制，使用分离均衡条件（维持过度声称的成本大于收益）设计协议，并推导委派链的可靠性组合边界。

Result: 信任层允许在满足成本条件时实现分离均衡，使可靠提供者区别于不可靠者，且设计无需模型重训练，在信任锚点缺失时能优雅降级。

Conclusion: 通过引入信号传递、筛选和声誉等经济学补救措施，信任层解决了LLM代理市场中的信息不对称问题，为构建可信的多代理协作系统提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLM）智能体已开始相互委派工作。诸如模型上下文协议（MCP）和Agent2Agent协议（A2A）等协议允许智能体发布其能力并让他人调用，此类智能体的公共注册表已开始出现。这些协议假设所广告的能力是静态的、真实的事实。而真实的智能体并非如此：其能力是概率性的，随输入变化，在底层模型更新时发生漂移，并且由于智能体本身是语言模型，它可能以完全自信的方式描述自己却出错。因此，调用者看到的是智能体声称能做什么，而非实际能做什么，且没有原则性的方法来区分可靠提供者和流利冒充者。我们认为这些困难有一个共同原因：柠檬市场。当质量隐藏且声称成本低廉时，好提供者和坏提供者变得无法区分，诚实的可靠性得不到奖励，市场逐渐衰退至最差参与者。经济学提供了三种补救措施——信号传递、筛选和声誉——而当今的智能体协议中这些措施均不存在。我们做出四项贡献：（1）一个失败分类法，将“自信却错误”命名为一类非对抗性、相关性的拜占庭故障子类，经典容错方法对其建模不当；（2）一个柠檬市场模型，表明基于信仰的协议只允许低信任均衡；（3）信任层（Trust Layer），一个位于MCP和A2A之上的薄层、协议无关的窄接口，增加了概率能力描述、筛选和声誉，并在维持过度声称的成本超过其收益时允许分离均衡；（4）一个具有端到端放置论证的委派链可靠性组合界限。该设计无需模型重训练，并在其信任锚点缺失或损坏时优雅降级。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents have begun to delegate work to one another. Protocols such as the Model Context Protocol (MCP) and the Agent2Agent protocol (A2A) let an agent publish what it can do and let others call it, and public registries of such agents are already appearing. These protocols assume an advertised capability is a static, truthful fact. A real agent is none of these things: its competence is probabilistic, varies with input, drifts when the underlying model is updated, and, because the agent is itself a language model, it can describe itself with complete confidence and be wrong. A caller therefore sees what an agent claims to do, not what it can do, with no principled way to tell a reliable provider from a fluent impostor.
  We argue these difficulties share one cause: the market for lemons. When quality is hidden and claims are cheap, good and bad providers become indistinguishable, honest reliability goes unrewarded, and the market decays toward its worst participants. Economics offers three remedies, signaling, screening, and reputation, and none are present in today's agent protocols.
  We make four contributions: (1) a failure taxonomy that names confident-wrong as a non-adversarial, correlated subclass of Byzantine faults that classical fault-tolerance mismodels; (2) a market-for-lemons model showing that faith-based protocols admit only a low-trust equilibrium; (3) the Trust Layer, a thin, protocol-agnostic narrow waist above MCP and A2A that adds probabilistic capability descriptors, screening, and reputation, and admits a separating equilibrium when the cost of sustaining an overclaim exceeds the gain from it; and (4) a reliability-composition bound for delegation chains with an end-to-end placement argument. The design needs no model retraining and degrades gracefully when its trust anchors are absent or corrupt.

</details>


### [94] [OpenAgenet / OAN White Paper: Open Infrastructure for Trusted Agent Interconnection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03161v3)
*Jinliang Xu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 提出agent互联信任层基础设施，身份验证和发现机制可迁移至coding agent系统。

TL;DR: OAN是一个开放的基础设施项目，用于在开放网络中实现可信的Agent互连，通过协议中立的信任层提供身份验证、治理和发现功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着Agent从孤立应用进入开放的多运营商网络，需要一种机制来验证Agent的身份、治理状态和信任证据，以确保安全互连。

Method: OAN采用基于did:oan的资源身份、治理准入、注册员入驻、根验证发布、授权发现、根颁发的授权VC和签名调用，结合联邦治理和可信发现。

Result: OAN提供了一个协议中立的信任层，不取代现有协议，而是增强互操作性，并已在原型中实现，具有清晰的性能概况和路线图。

Conclusion: OAN通过联邦治理、资源身份和可信发现的组合，解决了开放网络中Agent互连的信任问题，为多运营商环境下的安全Agent协作奠定了基础。

中文摘要：OpenAgenet（简称OAN）是一个用于可信Agent互连的开放基础设施项目。它解决了一个当Agent从孤立应用转向开放的多运营商网络时变得明显的问题：在Agent能够安全地发现、选择并调用另一个Agent之前，它需要一种方法来验证身份来源、治理状态、发现授权、新鲜度以及连接前的信任证据。OAN被设计为一个协议中立的信任层。它不会取代Agent交互协议、工具协议、模型编排框架或应用级工作流。相反，它提供了基于did:oan的资源身份、基于治理的准入、注册员辅助的入驻、根验证的包发布、感知授权的发现、根颁发的基础设施授权VC以及签名的可信调用。OAN的架构核心是联邦治理、资源身份和可信发现的组合，而不是单一的目录或命名服务。本白皮书解释了OAN的动机、架构、角色、治理模型、与MCP、A2A和ANP的关系、部署模式、合作模型、链上治理层、原型状态、性能概况和路线图。

Original abstract: OpenAgenet, abbreviated as OAN, is an open infrastructure project for trusted Agent interconnection. It addresses a problem that becomes visible when Agents move from isolated applications into open, multi-operator networks: before an Agent can safely discover, select, and invoke another Agent, it needs a way to verify identity provenance, governance state, discovery authorization, freshness, and pre-connection trust evidence. OAN is designed as a protocol-neutral trust layer. It does not replace Agent interaction protocols, tool protocols, model orchestration frameworks, or application-level workflows. Instead, it provides \texttt{did:oan}-based resource identity, governance-backed admission, Registrar-assisted onboarding, Root-verified package publication, authorization-aware Discovery, Root-issued infrastructure authorization VCs, and signed trusted invocation. The architectural center of OAN is the combination of federated governance, resource identity, and trusted Discovery, rather than a single directory or naming service. This white paper explains the motivation, architecture, roles, governance model, relationship with MCP, A2A, and ANP, deployment patterns, cooperation model, on-chain governance layer, prototype status, performance profile, and roadmap of OAN.

</details>

*Jinliang Xu*
