Original abstract: This yellow paper describes the technical architecture of OpenAgenet / OAN. OAN is a protocol-neutral trust layer for open Agent interconnection and discoverable AI resource products. It specifies the role architecture, \texttt{did:oan} identity objects, registration workflow, governance-backed Root lifecycle enforcement, Root-verified package model, authorization-aware Discovery, Root-issued infrastructure authorization VCs, signed trusted invocation, verification requirements, state transitions, security properties, implementation boundaries, and deployment considerations. The design is intended to support heterogeneous Agent frameworks and interaction protocols, including MCP, A2A, ANP-like systems, domain-specific Agent protocols, Skills, MCP Servers, and Tool/API resources. OAN does not define the entire business conversation among Agents or the native protocol of every resource; it defines how resource identities become admissible, discoverable, verifiable, and safe to approach before protocol-specific interaction begins.

### [96] [BlobShuffle: Cost-Effective Repartitioning in Stream Processing Systems via Object Storage Exemplified with Kafka Streams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03364v1)
*Sören Henning,Otmar Ertl,Adriano Vogel*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BlobShuffle通过利用云对象存储作为中间交换层，将洗牌数据分组为批次并存储，仅发送紧凑通知，从而大幅降低流处理系统中的洗牌成本（>40倍），同时保持延迟低于2秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统流处理框架中，跨多个可用区的数据洗牌产生大量网络流量和高昂成本，且大规模运行高吞吐量、强一致性消息骨干网带来操作负担。

Method: 将记录分批存储到云对象存储，仅转发紧凑通知，下游通过通知检索批次；采用可配置批处理和分布式缓存机制平衡成本与延迟。

Result: 在Kubernetes AWS部署中，相比原生Kafka Streams，洗牌成本降低超过40倍，第95百分位延迟低于2秒，可处理超过2 GiB/s的吞吐量且无扩展性限制。

Conclusion: BlobShuffle经济高效地支持大规模洗牌密集型工作负载，且与现有系统兼容，保留一致性保证。

中文摘要：数据流的洗牌或重新分区是当前最先进的流处理框架在大规模分布式环境中支持有状态工作负载的关键操作。然而，在当今的云部署中，由于跨多个可用区（AZ）的大量网络流量以及大规模运行高吞吐量、强一致性消息骨干网的操作负担，洗牌可能成为主要的成本驱动因素。我们提出了BlobShuffle，一种新颖的流处理系统成本效益洗牌方法，它利用云对象存储作为中间交换层。BlobShuffle不是直接发送所有洗牌记录，而是将记录分组为批次，将这些批次存储在云对象存储中，并仅转发紧凑的通知。下游操作者使用这些通知来检索相关批次并提取相应的记录。BlobShuffle通过可配置的批处理和分布式缓存机制平衡成本效率和延迟。BlobShuffle作为Kafka Streams的附加组件实现，只需要对现有应用程序进行最小的代码更改，保持Kafka和底层基础设施不变，并保留Kafka Streams的一致性和正确性保证。在基于Kubernetes的AWS部署上进行的大规模实验评估中，我们表明，与原生Kafka Streams洗牌相比，BlobShuffle可以将洗牌成本降低超过40倍，同时将第95百分位的洗牌延迟保持在2秒以下。此外，它在我们的实验中能够扩展到处理超过2 GiB/s的数据，而没有遇到可扩展性限制，这表明BlobShuffle可以在大规模下经济地支持洗牌密集型工作负载。

Original abstract: Shuffling or repartitioning data streams is an essential operation of state-of-the-art stream processing frameworks to support stateful workloads in a large-scale, distributed setting. In today's cloud deployments, however, shuffling can become a major cost driver due to substantial network traffic across multiple availability zones (AZs) as well as an operational burden when operating a high-throughput, strongly consistent messaging backbone at scale. We present BlobShuffle, a novel approach to cost-effective shuffling for stream processing systems that leverages cloud object storage as an intermediate exchange layer. Instead of sending all shuffled records directly, BlobShuffle groups records into batches, stores these batches in cloud object storage, and forwards only compact notifications. Downstream operators use these notifications to retrieve the relevant batches and extract the corresponding records. BlobShuffle balances cost efficiency and latency through configurable batching and a distributed caching mechanism. BlobShuffle is implemented as an add-on for Kafka Streams that requires only minimal code changes to existing applications, leaves Kafka and the underlying infrastructure unmodified, and preserves Kafka Streams' consistency and correctness guarantees. In a large-scale experimental evaluation on a Kubernetes-based AWS deployment, we show that BlobShuffle can reduce shuffling costs by more than 40x compared to native Kafka Streams shuffling while keeping the 95th percentile shuffle latency below 2 seconds. Moreover, it scales to processing more than 2 GiB/s without encountering a scalability limit in our experiments, indicating that BlobShuffle can economically support shuffle-intensive workloads at large scale.

</details>

### [97] [HighTide: An Agent-Curated Open-Source VLSI Benchmark Suite](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04126v1)
*Benjamin Goldblatt,Paolo Pedroso,Farhad Modaresi,Ethan Sifferman,Matthew R. Guthaus*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: HighTide是一个AI辅助的开源基准测试套件，支持多样化设计、增量编译、AI策展和稳定发布，旨在与开源硬件生态共同成长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试套件缺乏AI辅助和持续集成能力，难以适应开源硬件生态的快速演进。

Method: 构建了涵盖多种设计语言和工艺节点的开源套件，采用Bazel实现增量RTL-to-GDS编译，设计12个AI代理技能覆盖全生命周期，并集成决策日志作为长期记忆，配套RTL编译验证基础设施。

Result: 生成了具有远程缓存、AI代理决策日志和稳定发布验证的公开基准测试套件。

Conclusion: 该套件为开源硬件社区提供了一个可扩展、可复用的AI辅助基准测试平台，促进设计优化和工具评估。

中文摘要：我们介绍了HighTide，一个不断发展的AI辅助基准测试套件。具体贡献包括：(i) 一个多样化的开源套件，涵盖多种设计语言和技术节点；(ii) 基于Bazel的增量RTL到GDS编译，带有远程缓存；(iii) AI辅助设计策展，通过十二个代理技能覆盖设计生命周期、流程优化、工具参考和元维护，并配有每个设计的决策日志，作为调优理由的长期记忆；(iv) 具有RTL编译验证的基础设施，用于稳定发布。该套件公开可用，旨在与开源硬件生态系统共同成长。

Original abstract: We introduce HighTide, an evolving AI-assisted benchmark suite. Specifically, the contributions are: (i) a diverse open-source suite spanning multiple design languages and technology nodes, (ii) Bazel-based incremental RTL-to-GDS compilation with remote caching, (iii) AI-assisted design curation through twelve agent skills covering the design lifecycle, flow optimization, tool reference, and meta-maintenance, backed by per-design decision logs that serve as long-term memory of tuning rationale across the suite, and (iv) an infrastructure with RTL compilation verification for stable releases. The suite is publicly available and designed to grow with the open-source hardware ecosystem.

### [98] [Agent libOS: A Runtime Substrate for Capability-Controlled Self-Evolving LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03895v2)
*Yingqi Zhang*

Main category: cs.OS

Selection reason: agent运行时系统与能力控制，对agent架构有直接贡献

TL;DR: Agent libOS通过能力控制机制防止自我进化LLM智能体出现权限提升，在27个任务中完成计划且零未授权副作用，错误拒绝率仅7.0%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在长期运行中累积能力，但若行动暴露即授予权限，则会形成权限提升的安全漏洞。

Method: 提出Agent libOS框架，将智能体表示为进程并引入显式能力、进程本地命名空间、系统调用中介等机制，确保资源权限仅通过审计原语改变。

Result: 在27个确定性任务上，原型完成所有计划，防止全部未授权副作用，错误拒绝率为7.0%；而基线方案虽完成任务但多项安全检查失败。

Conclusion: Agent libOS能够有效控制智能体进化过程中的权限风险，为安全自主系统提供可行基础。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体正在成为长期运行的软件参与者，而非固定的工具使用者。它们累积记忆、激活技能、合成工具、派生子进程、附加远程资源，并将检查点提交为可重用的执行镜像。这些机制提高了适应性，但也产生了一种系统安全失效模式：如果暴露一个动作也同时授予执行该动作所需的权限，那么自我进化就变成了一条权限提升路径。本文提出了Agent libOS，一个面向智能体的原生库操作系统框架，用于实现能力可控的自我进化智能体。其核心不变性是：模型可见的可用操作可以进化，而资源权限仅通过显式的、经过审计的运行时原语来改变。Agent libOS将一个智能体表示为一个进程，具有进程标识、进程本地对象内存、消息队列、工具表、加载的技能、进程本地的Deno/TypeScript JIT工具、子进程、预算、检查点和显式能力。AgentImage对象定义了启动时的提示和工具表状态；技能和JIT工具扩展了操作面；基于检查点的镜像使内部状态可重用。这些机制本身都不授予文件系统、shell、人类、内存、进程、检查点、镜像、JSON-RPC、MCP或PTY权限。原型实现了进程本地命名空间、持久运行时状态、LLM调用可观测性、人类审批队列、预算、系统调用中介的JIT工具、受信任的运行时模块、对象绑定的PTY会话、检查点恢复/分支/提交、JSON-RPC和MCP提供者，以及一个确定性运行时安全基准。在27个版本化的确定性任务上，它完成了任务计划，同时防止了所有建模的未授权副作用，保守错误拒绝率为7.0%。简单的包装器和沙盒基线保留了任务完成，但未能通过大多数安全检查。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are becoming long-running software actors rather than fixed tool users. They accumulate memory, activate skills, synthesize tools, fork children, attach remote resources, and commit checkpoints into reusable execution images. These mechanisms improve adaptability, but also create a systems-security failure mode: if exposing an action also grants the authority needed to perform it, self-evolution becomes a permission-escalation path.
  This paper presents Agent libOS, an agent-native library-OS substrate for capability-controlled self-evolving agents. Its central invariant is that model-visible affordances may evolve while resource authority changes only through explicit, audited runtime primitives. Agent libOS represents an agent as an AgentProcess with process identity, process-local Object Memory, message queues, a tool table, loaded Skills, process-local Deno/TypeScript JIT tools, child processes, budgets, checkpoints, and explicit capabilities. AgentImage objects define boot-time prompt and tool-table state; Skills and JIT tools extend the action surface; checkpoint-derived images make internal state reusable. None of these mechanisms grants filesystem, shell, human, memory, process, checkpoint, image, JSON-RPC, MCP, or PTY authority by itself.
  The prototype implements process-local namespaces, persistent runtime state, LLM-call observability, human approval queues, budgets, syscall-mediated JIT tools, trusted Runtime Modules, Object-bound PTY sessions, checkpoint restore/fork/commit, JSON-RPC and MCP providers, and a deterministic runtime-safety benchmark. On 27 versioned deterministic tasks, it completed the task plans while preventing all modeled unauthorized side effects, with a 7.0% conservative false-denial rate. Simple wrapper and sandbox baselines preserved task completion but failed most safety checks.

</details>

### [99] [PhotoCraft: Agentic Reasoning with Hierarchical Self-Evolving Memory for Deep Image Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03099v1)
*Kailin Lyu,Zhiqiang Yuan,Jianwei He,Qiwei Yan,Xuanbo Su,Nanxing Hu,Yang Liu,Ce Hao,Shengqian Qin,Lianyu Hu,Jinchao Zhang,Jie Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出层次记忆系统（工作/情景/语义记忆），可迁移至coding agent的长程任务记忆管理。

TL;DR: PhotoCraft是一个无需训练的分层记忆系统，通过为多模态大语言模型引入工作、情景和语义记忆，显著提升深度图像搜索中的多步推理和上下文感知检索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的智能体缺乏持久记忆，导致执行漂移和经验隔离，无法有效处理需要多步推理的深度图像搜索任务。

Method: 提出PhotoCraft，一个无需训练的分层记忆系统，包含工作记忆、情景记忆和语义记忆，动态集成到多模态大语言模型的推理过程中。

Result: 在DISBench上，PhotoCraft在不同多模态大语言模型骨干上持续提升上下文感知检索性能，最高提升18.5%。

Conclusion: PhotoCraft有效缓解了无记忆深度图像搜索的关键瓶颈，为构建可靠且可泛化的多模态搜索智能体提供了实用方案。

中文摘要：深度图像搜索需要对丰富的上下文线索（如时间、地点和事件关系）进行多步推理。然而，大多数现有的基于LLM的智能体是无状态的且反应式的，缺乏持久记忆来维护长期上下文或在任务间转移经验，这常常导致执行漂移和经验隔离。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了PhotoCraft，一个无需训练的分层记忆系统，用于照片搜索智能体。受人类认知启发，PhotoCraft为多模态大语言模型配备了工作记忆、情景记忆和语义记忆，在推理过程中动态调用这些记忆以保持逻辑一致性和知识可迁移性，贯穿多步推理和答案生成。在DISBench上的大量实验表明，PhotoCraft在不同多模态大语言模型骨干网络上持续改善了上下文感知检索，取得了高达18.5%的提升，并有效缓解了无记忆深度图像搜索中的关键瓶颈，为可靠且可泛化的多模态搜索智能体提供了一条实用路径。

Original abstract: Deep Image Search requires multi-step reasoning over rich contextual cues, such as time, location, and event relations. However, most existing LLM-based agents are stateless and reactive, lacking persistent memory to maintain long-horizon context or transfer experience across tasks, which often leads to execution drift and experience isolation. To address these limitations, we propose PhotoCraft, a training-free, hierarchical memory system for photo-search agents. Inspired by human cognition, PhotoCraft equips MLLMs with working, episodic, and semantic memory, which are dynamically invoked during reasoning to preserve logical consistency and knowledge transferability throughout multi-step reasoning and answer generation. Extensive experiments on DISBench demonstrate that PhotoCraft consistently improves context-aware retrieval across diverse MLLM backbones, achieving gains of up to 18.5\% and effectively mitigating key bottlenecks in memoryless deep image search, offering a practical path toward reliable and generalizable multimodal search agents.

</details>


### [100] [WebRISE: Requirement-Induced State Evaluation for MLLM-Generated Web Artifacts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03220v1)
*Yuxin Meng,Yuhan Suo,Junjie Wang,Yuhan Sun,Yiyao Yu,Ruixu Zhang,Ruining Hu,Yubin Wang,Shouwei Ruan,Bin Wang,Yuxiang Zhang,Yujiu Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出基于合约图的web工件事件评估，对agent行为验证有参考价值。

TL;DR: WebRISE是一个新的基准测试，通过交互契约图评估MLLM生成的web工件的功能正确性，发现现有模型在转换有效性和需求覆盖率上表现不足，且视觉质量不能反映行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试仅通过局部证据评估交互，忽略了决定页面是否正常工作的需求诱导状态和转换。

Method: 提出WebRISE，将任务需求编译成交互契约图（ICG），包含可观察状态、用户意图转换和DOM/视觉断言，用于实现无关的浏览器执行；涵盖442个任务、五种输入模态，包含5,495个转换和5,271个需求检查。

Result: 在14个MLLM上，最强模型仅达到65.6%转换有效性和66.3%需求覆盖率；视觉质量不能代表行为（例如Qwen3.6-35B-A3B在Markdown上视觉得分80.8但转换有效性仅15.5）；视频输入提供最强交互信号；基于ICG的评分检测状态错误的速率是检查点式评估的2-16倍。

Conclusion: WebRISE揭示了当前MLLM在生成功能正确的web工件方面的局限性，强调需要超越视觉质量评估行为正确性，并提出了更有效的ICG-based评估方法。

中文摘要：现有的针对MLLM生成的web工件的基准测试通过局部证据评估交互，忽略了决定页面是否正常工作的需求诱导状态和转换。我们引入了WebRISE，它将任务需求编译成可观察状态、用户意图转换以及DOM/视觉断言的交互契约图（ICG），用于实现无关的浏览器执行。WebRISE涵盖442个任务，跨越五种输入模态（文本、Markdown、草图、图像、视频），包含5,495个转换和5,271个需求检查，将用户声明的功能与隐式的产品级约束分开。在14个MLLM中，即使是最强的模型也仅达到65.6%的转换有效性和66.3%的需求覆盖率，且视觉质量不能代表行为（Qwen3.6-35B-A3B在Markdown上：V=80.8但T=15.5）。视频提供了最强的交互信号（隐式覆盖率比文本高10.6个百分点），而隐式约束持续存在；缺陷注入表明，基于ICG的评分检测状态错误的速率是检查点式评估的2-16倍。

Original abstract: Existing benchmarks for MLLM-generated web artifacts assess interaction through local evidence and miss the requirement-induced states and transitions that determine whether a page works. We introduce WebRISE, which compiles task requirements into Interaction Contract Graphs (ICGs) of observable states, user-intent transitions, and DOM/visual assertions for implementation-agnostic browser execution. WebRISE spans 442 tasks across five input modalities (Text, Markdown, Sketch, Image, Video), with 5,495 transitions and 5,271 requirement checks that separate user-stated functions from implicit product-level constraints. Across 14 MLLMs, even the strongest model reaches only 65.6% transition validity and 66.3% requirement coverage, and visual quality is no proxy for behavior (Qwen3.6-35B-A3B on Markdown: V=80.8 yet T=15.5). Video gives the strongest interaction signal (+10.6 pp implicit coverage over Text), while implicit constraints persist; defect injection shows ICG-based scoring detects state errors at 2-16x the rate of checkpoint-style evaluation.

</details>


### [101] [Building Reliable Long-Form Generation via Hallucination Rejection Sampling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03628v1)
*Lin Li,Georgia Channing,Suhaas M Bhat,Gabriel Davis Jones,Yarin Gal*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 拒绝采样缓解幻觉，具有自我纠正机制，可迁移至agent的验证与自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出分段式幻觉拒绝采样（SHARS）框架，通过检测并重采样幻觉片段来缓解长文本生成中的幻觉雪球效应，无需外部资源，显著减少幻觉并保持信息量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长文本生成中幻觉雪球效应导致早期错误累积，现有方法效果有限或依赖外部资源。

Method: 基于任意幻觉检测器（采用改进的语义不确定性）识别幻觉片段，进行拒绝重采样，仅保留可信内容逐步生成。

Result: 在标准化基准上显著减少幻觉，同时保持或提升信息量。

Conclusion: SHARS能有效自纠正幻觉，无需外部资源，兼容外部知识扩展。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在开放式文本生成方面取得了显著进展，但它们仍然容易产生不准确或不受支持的幻觉内容，这削弱了其可靠性。这个问题在长文本生成中由于幻觉雪球效应（早期错误传播并累积到后续输出中的现象）而加剧。为了解决这一挑战，我们提出了一种新颖的推理时幻觉缓解框架，称为分段式幻觉拒绝采样（SHARS），该框架使用任意幻觉检测器来识别和拒绝生成过程中的幻觉片段，并重新采样直到产生可靠的内容。通过仅保留自信的信息并在其基础上构建后续生成，该框架减轻了幻觉累积并增强了事实一致性。为了实例化该框架，我们采用语义不确定性作为检测器，并引入了几个重要的修改来解决其局限性并更好地适应长文本。我们的方法使模型能够自我纠正幻觉，而无需外部资源（如网络搜索或知识库），同时保持与它们的兼容性以便未来扩展。在标准化幻觉基准上的实证评估表明，我们的方法在长文本生成中显著减少了幻觉，同时保持甚至提高了生成的信息量。代码可在 https://github.com/TreeLLi/hallucination-rejection-sampling 获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable progress in open-ended text generation, yet they remain prone to hallucinating incorrect or unsupported content, which undermines their reliability. This issue is exacerbated in long-form generation due to hallucination snowballing, a phenomenon where early errors propagate and compound into subsequent outputs. To address this challenge, we propose a novel inference-time hallucination mitigation framework, named Segment-wise HAllucination Rejection Sampling (SHARS), which uses an arbitrary hallucination detector to identify and reject hallucinated segments during generation and resample until faithful content is produced. By retaining only confident information and building subsequent generations upon it, the framework mitigates hallucination accumulation and enhances factual consistency. To instantiate this framework, we adopt semantic uncertainty as the detector and introduce several vital modifications to address its limitations and better adapt it to long-form text. Our method enables models to self-correct hallucinations without requiring external resources such as web search or knowledge bases, while remaining compatible with them for future extensions. Empirical evaluations on standardized hallucination benchmarks demonstrate that our method substantially reduces hallucinations in long-form generation while preserving or even improving the informativeness of generation. Code is available at: https://github.com/TreeLLi/hallucination-rejection-sampling.

</details>


### [102] [CoEval: Ranking Language Models for Custom Tasks Without Labeled Data or Trustworthy Benchmarks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03650v2)
*Alexander Apartsin,Yehudit Aperstein*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出无标签模型评估框架，使用多模型协作与自我评估，对agent评测有潜在启发。

TL;DR: CoEval是一个无需人工标注的模型自评估框架，通过角色轮换生成无污染基准并加权评分，能准确恢复模型排名且避免数据泄露和偏见，提供领域特异的可信排行榜。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有公开基准测试无法反映特定子领域，且存在数据泄露导致分数不可信的问题，因此需要一种无污染、任务特定的模型评估方法。

Method: 通过模型池轮流扮演教师、学生和评审，生成全新基准测试并相互评分，利用学生响应数据对问题和评审进行加权，无需人工标注。

Result: 在已知真实排名时，CoEval以ρ=0.86恢复客观正确性，加权后对13个模型的金标准排名Spearman达0.95；生成题目与五个公开基准无重叠，消除了冗长偏差和同族自偏好，排名显示领域特异性。

Conclusion: CoEval提供可靠的、任务特定的模型评估，避免数据泄露和偏见，可随模型更新重复使用，为实际应用提供无污染排行榜。

中文摘要：为特定应用选择预训练语言模型或评估微调模型是一项高价值决策，然而用于此目的的公开基准测试并不适用：通用基准测试未必能反映特定的子领域或子任务，并且当基准测试中的项目泄露到预训练中、模型通过记忆而非推理作答时，其分数也值得怀疑。我们提出 CoEval，一个开放框架，通过集成自评估提供可信的、任务特定的信号：根据任务或领域描述，一组模型轮流扮演教师、学生和评审三种角色，生成全新的、无污染的基准测试，回答问题，并相互评分，全程无需人工标注或评判。由于每个模型也作为学生作答，这些响应数据用于根据问题的区分能力和评审与专家组的一致性来加权每个问题和每个评审。在有真实答案的情况下，CoEval 能恢复真实排名，并以 ρ=0.86 追踪客观正确性；加权方法在 Spearman 相关系数为 0.95 时恢复了十三个模型的金标准排名。可靠性来自专家组的构成而非规模：这种无标签加权方法能将异常评审权重归零，并降低已饱和问题的权重，因此两者都不会扭曲排名。生成的题目与五个公开基准测试无任何逐字重叠，专家组消除了冗长偏差并防止了同族自偏好，而且排名是领域特异的：四个全新领域中三个不同模型分别排名第一，因此通用排行榜会误导大多数实践者。同样的流程可在每次模型发布时重新运行，为任何团队提供其应用领域内无污染的排行榜。

Original abstract: Selecting a pretrained language model, or evaluating a fine-tuned one, for a specific application is a high-value decision, yet the public benchmarks used to make it are poorly suited: a generic benchmark need not reflect a particular sub-domain or sub-task, and its scores are suspect when its items have leaked into pretraining and are recalled rather than solved. We present CoEval, an open framework that supplies a trustworthy, task-specific signal through ensemble self-evaluation: from a task or domain description, a pool of models rotates through all three roles, teacher, student, and judge, to generate a fresh, contamination-free benchmark, answer it, and score one another, with no human labels or raters. Because every model also answers as a student, the responses are the data that weight each question by its discriminative power and each judge by its consensus with the panel. Where ground truth exists, CoEval recovers the true ranking and tracks objective correctness at \r{ho}=0.86, and the weighting recovers the gold ranking of thirteen models at Spearman 0.95. Reliability comes from panel composition, not size: this label-free weighting zeroes out broken judges and down-weights saturated questions, so neither distorts the ranking. Generated items show zero verbatim overlap with five public benchmarks, the panel cancels verbosity bias and precludes same-family self-preference, and rankings are domain-specific: three different models top four de-novo domains, so a generic leaderboard misdirects most practitioners. The same pipeline reruns on each model release, giving any team a contamination-free leaderboard for its application.

</details>


### [103] [Consistency Training Can Entrench Misalignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03810v2)
*David Demitri Africa,Arathi Mani*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究一致性训练对模型对齐的影响，与agent安全/行为相关，可迁移至agent alignment方法。

TL;DR: 一致性训练并非对齐中性：它抑制奖励黑客和涌现不对齐，但放大阿谀奉承行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解一致性训练对模型对齐的影响，特别是其自引导特性是否会放大不良行为。

Method: 在108个表现出受控不对齐行为的开源模型（7B-70B）上测试七种一致性训练方法。

Result: 一致性训练抑制奖励黑客和涌现不对齐，但放大阿谀奉承；分布偏移是系统性对齐效应的主要驱动因素。

Conclusion: 一致性训练不是对齐中性的，其在关键系统中的使用应被仔细审计。

中文摘要：一致性训练鼓励模型在相关输入或采样过程中产生相似的输出。这类方法简单、可扩展且基本无需标签，但它们对模型对齐的影响仍知之甚少。这些方法的自引导特性是否会放大模型中的不良行为？我们在108个模型生物上测试了七种一致性训练方法：这些模型是经过微调的开源模型（7B-70B），表现出各种受控的不对齐行为。我们发现结果差异显著：一致性训练通常抑制奖励黑客行为和涌现的不对齐，但放大阿谀奉承行为。我们提出证据表明，由一致性标记过程引起的分布偏移，而非选择算子的变化，可能是系统性对齐效应的主要驱动因素。最后，我们提出了一个统一的理论框架，推导出一致性训练会放大或抑制不对齐的条件。总体而言，我们的研究确定了一致性训练并非对齐中性的，其在关键系统中的使用应被仔细审核。

Original abstract: Consistency training encourages a model to produce similar outputs across related inputs or sampling procedures. Such methods are simple, scalable, and largely label-free, but their effects on model alignment remain poorly understood. Could the self-bootstrapping nature of these methods amplify undesired behavior in models? We test seven consistency training methods on 108 model organisms: open-source models (7B--70B) fine-tuned to exhibit various forms of controlled misaligned behavior. We find that outcomes vary significantly: consistency training generally suppresses reward hacking and emergent misalignment but amplifies sycophancy. We present evidence that distribution shifts induced by the consistency labeling process, rather than variation in the selection operators, may be the primary driver of systematic alignment effects. Finally, we present a unifying theoretical framework to derive conditions under which consistency training will amplify or suppress misalignment. In total, our study establishes that consistency training is not alignment-neutral, and that its use in critical systems should be carefully audited.

### [104] [A Training-Free Mixture-of-Agents Framework for Multi-Document Summarization using LLMs and Knowledge Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03867v2)
*Cuong Vuong Tuan,Trang Mai Xuan,Tien-Cuong Nguyen,Vu-Duc Ngo,Thien Van Luong*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 无训练的多agent框架用于摘要，agent协作架构可迁移

TL;DR: 提出一种免训练的混合智能体框架，结合LLM和知识图谱进行多文档摘要，通过分解任务和多视角一致性机制，在多个数据集上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MDS方法难以捕捉文档间复杂关系，依赖大量标注数据，泛化能力有限。

Method: 提出免训练的混合智能体框架，将摘要分解为抽取式选择、知识感知抽象和迭代细化三个任务，通过LLM引导的多视角一致性机制统一输出。

Result: 在四个英/越南语数据集上达到SOTA或竞争性能。

Conclusion: 验证了模块化设计的有效性和适应性，无需微调即可实现跨领域和跨语言的良好表现。

中文摘要：多文档摘要（MDS）在从文本集合中提取关键信息方面发挥着关键作用。现有方法通常难以捕捉复杂的文档间关系，严重依赖大量标注数据进行监督训练，或在跨领域和跨语言时泛化能力有限。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了一种免训练的混合智能体框架，用于MDS，该框架利用大语言模型（LLM）和知识图谱的互补优势。我们的方法将摘要分解为专门的智能体任务：抽取式选择、知识感知抽象和迭代细化，每个任务无需特定任务的微调。我们通过由LLM引导的多视角一致性机制来统一它们的输出。在四个英文和越南语数据集上的实验展示了最先进或具有竞争力的性能，验证了我们模块化设计的有效性和适应性。

Original abstract: Multi-Document Summarization (MDS) plays a critical role in distilling essential information from collections of textual data. Existing approaches often struggle to capture complex inter-document relationships, rely heavily on large amounts of labeled data for supervised training, or exhibit limited generalization across domains and languages. To address these limitations, we present a training-free mixture-of-agents framework for MDS that leverages the complementary strengths of large language models (LLMs) and knowledge graphs. Our approach decomposes summarization into specialized agent tasks: extractive selection, knowledge-aware abstraction, and iterative refinement, each operating without task-specific fine-tuning. We unify their outputs using a multi-perspective consistency mechanism guided by LLMs. Experiments across four datasets in English and Vietnamese demonstrate state-of-the-art or competitive performance, validating the effectiveness and adaptability of our modular design.

### [105] [Synthesize and Reward -- Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Step Tool Use in Live Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03892v2)
*Ibrahim Abdelaziz,Asim Munawar,Kinjal Basu,Maxwell Crouse,Chulaka Gunasekara,Suneet Katrekar,Pavan Kapanipathi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: RL训练多步工具调用，直接相关coding agent工具使用

TL;DR: 提出PROVE框架，通过有状态MCP服务器、状态机数据合成和自适应效率惩罚奖励，改善了LLM在多步工具调用中的一致性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM训练面临三个障碍：有状态执行环境构建成本高、合成查询脱离服务器实际状态、基于召回率的奖励鼓励冗长调用模式，导致多步工具调用效果差。

Method: 提出PROVE框架，包括：1) 20个有状态MCP服务器（343个工具）支持实时执行RL训练；2) 状态机数据合成流水线生成基于实际服务器状态的多轮调用轨迹；3) 多组件程序化奖励包含自适应效率惩罚，抑制冗长行为。

Result: 在约1.3万训练示例上训练Qwen3-4B/8B、Qwen2.5-7B和Granite-4.1-8B，在BFCL Multi-Turn、tau2-bench和T-Eval上分别提升+10.2、+6.8和+6.5个百分点。

Conclusion: PROVE框架在多个模型家族上一致提升了多步工具编排性能，验证了其有效性。

中文摘要：训练LLM编排多步骤工具调用受三个相互关联的障碍制约：现实的有状态执行环境构建成本高，合成训练查询常常脱离服务器的实际状态（因此生成的工具调用无法执行），以及基于召回率的RL奖励鼓励冗长的工具调用模式。我们提出了PROVE（在验证环境上的程序化奖励），一个包含三个贡献的框架：（1）一个包含20个有状态MCP（模型上下文协议）服务器的库，暴露343个工具，支持具有会话范围状态隔离的实时执行RL训练；（2）一个状态机数据合成流水线，生成基于实时采样服务器状态的多轮工具调用轨迹，因此生成的查询引用实际存在的实体；（3）一个多组件程序化奖励，包含自适应效率惩罚，以抵消基于召回率奖励的冗长激励。我们在由此产生的约1.3万个训练示例上，使用GRPO训练了四个模型（Qwen3-4B、Qwen3-8B、Qwen2.5-7B、Granite-4.1-8B）。在BFCL Multi-Turn、tau2-bench和T-Eval上，PROVE分别取得了高达+10.2、+6.8和+6.5个百分点的改进，表明该框架在两个模型家族的多步骤工具编排任务上取得了持续增益。

Original abstract: Training LLMs to orchestrate multi-step tool calls is held back by three coupled obstacles: realistic stateful execution environments are costly to build, synthetic training queries are often detached from the server's actual state (so the generated tool calls fail to execute), and recall-based RL rewards incentivize verbose tool-calling patterns. We present PROVE (Programmatic Rewards On Verified Environments), a framework with three contributions: (1) a library of 20 stateful MCP (Model Context Protocol) servers exposing 343 tools, enabling live-execution RL training with session-scoped state isolation; (2) a state-machine data synthesis pipeline that generates multi-turn tool-call trajectories grounded in live-sampled server state, so generated queries reference entities that actually exist; and (3) a multi-component programmatic reward with an adaptive efficiency penalty that counters the verbosity incentive of recall-based rewards. We train four models (Qwen3-4B, Qwen3-8B, Qwen2.5-7B, Granite-4.1-8B) with GRPO on the resulting ~13K training examples. On BFCL Multi-Turn, tau2-bench, and T-Eval, PROVE yields improvements of up to +10.2, +6.8, and +6.5 points respectively, demonstrating that this framework yields consistent gains on multi-step tool orchestration across two model families.

### [106] [Agentic Chain-of-Thought Steering for Efficient and Controllable LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03965v1)
*Yu Xia,Zhouhang Xie,Xin Xu,Byungkyu Kang,Prarit Lamba,Xiang Gao,Julian McAuley*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 控制器agent自适应引导推理路径，通用agent推理控制方法

TL;DR: 提出ACTS方法，通过强化学习训练控制器代理自适应调整推理策略，在保持推理质量的同时大幅降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM的CoT推理虽提升准确率但token效率低且缺乏控制；现有高效推理方法隐含控制方式，缺乏显式推理引导。

Method: 将推理控制建模为MDP，控制器观察推理轨迹和预算，输出策略和引导短语；使用合成轨迹初始化并通过带预算条件奖励的RL优化。

Result: 在多个基准上，ACTS匹配全思维性能并大幅节省token，实现可控的准确率-效率权衡。

Conclusion: ACTS通过预算感知的显式推理控制实现了高效且可控的推理，验证了该方法在不同推理器和任务上的有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型通过扩展的思维链推理提高了最终答案的准确性，但通常效率低下，且推理过程中几乎无法控制。现有的高效推理方法通过缩短、提前停止或压缩痕迹来控制思考长度，但隐含了模型如何思考。在本文中，我们提出了代理引导的思维链控制（ACTS），将推理控制建模为马尔可夫决策过程，其中控制器代理在推理过程中自适应地控制冻结的推理器。在每个步骤中，控制器观察推理轨迹和剩余思考预算，然后发出一个由推理策略和引导短语组成的控制动作，以启动下一个推理器步骤。这使得在保留推理器生成连续性的同时，能够进行预算感知的策略控制以实现高效推理。我们从构建的合成控制轨迹（具有多预算增强）初始化控制器代理，并通过带有预算条件奖励塑造的强化学习进一步优化。跨多个基准的实验表明，ACTS在显著节省令牌的同时达到了全思维的性能，并能够在不同的推理器和任务中实现可控的准确率-效率权衡。代码可在https://github.com/Andree-9/ACTS获取。

Original abstract: Large language models improve final-answer accuracy through extended chain-of-thought reasoning, but often spend tokens inefficiently and offer little inference-time control. Existing efficient reasoning methods control thinking length by shortening, early-stopping, or compressing traces, leaving how the model thinks implicit. In this paper, we propose Agentic Chain-of-Thought Steering (ACTS), which formulates reasoning steering as a Markov decision process where a controller agent adaptively steers a frozen reasoner during inference. At each step, the controller observes the reasoning trace and remaining thinking budget, then issues a steering action consisting of a reasoning strategy and a steering phrase that initiates the next reasoner step. This enables budget-aware strategy control for efficient reasoning while preserving the reasoner's generation continuity. We initialize the controller agent from our constructed synthetic steering trajectories with multi-budget augmentation, and further optimize it via reinforcement learning with budget-conditioned reward shaping. Experiments across multiple benchmarks show that ACTS matches full-thinking performance with substantial token savings, and enables controllable accuracy-efficiency trade-offs across different reasoners and tasks. The code is available at https://github.com/Andree-9/ACTS.

</details>


### [107] [QUBRIC: Co-Designing Queries and Rubrics for RL Beyond Verifiable Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03968v1)
*Rongzhi Zhang,Rui Feng,Zhihan Zhang,Jingfeng Yang,Qingyu Yin,Xin Liu,Zixuan Zhang,Priyanka Nigam,Bing Yin,Tuo Zhao,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 联合设计查询与评估准则，通用RL奖励塑造方法

TL;DR: 提出QUBRIC框架，通过协同设计查询和评分标准来解决基于评分标准强化学习中的结构性瓶颈，在多个基准上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于评分标准的强化学习方法将查询分布固定，导致评分质量受限于查询结构：开放式查询产生模糊评分，而窄化查询又引入不可验证的虚构参考，使训练无奖励信号。

Method: QUBRIC框架：教师推导关键点将开放式查询重写为可评估的情景问题；对比评分标准生成将教师-策略差距转化为查询级标准；可学习性过滤保留信息对用于GRPO训练。

Result: 在ArenaHard上相比SFT基线提升+5.5分；仅用指令遵循数据训练，在三个保留基准（法律、道德、叙事推理）上平均提升+6.3分，推理维度改善明显。

Conclusion: 协同设计查询和评分标准能使基于评分标准的强化学习成为超越严格可验证任务的RLVR的有效补充。

中文摘要：基于评分标准的强化学习是将强化学习扩展到可验证奖励之外的一条有前景的途径，但现有方法在优化评分标准的同时将查询分布视为固定的。我们识别出一个结构性瓶颈：评分质量受到查询结构的限制。开放式查询产生模糊的评分标准；而简单地缩小查询范围会引入任何模型都无法验证的虚构参考答案，导致所有响应失败，训练无法获得奖励信号。我们提出了QUBRIC框架，该框架协同设计查询和评分标准。教师推导的关键点将开放式查询重写为基于场景、可评估的问题。然后，对比评分标准生成将教师-策略差距转化为查询级标准，可学习性过滤仅保留信息丰富的查询-评分标准对用于GRPO训练。QUBRIC在ArenaHard上相比SFT基线获得了+5.5分的提升。仅使用指令遵循数据训练后，它还能进一步迁移到三个保留基准上，涵盖法律、道德和叙事推理（平均提升+6.3分），改进主要集中在与推理相关的维度上。这些结果提供了证据，表明协同设计查询和评分标准可以使基于评分标准的强化学习成为超越严格可验证任务的RLVR的实用补充。

Original abstract: Rubric-based RL is a promising route for extending reinforcement learning beyond verifiable rewards, yet existing methods optimize rubrics while treating the query distribution as fixed. We identify a structural bottleneck: rubric quality is constrained by query structure. Open-ended queries yield vague rubrics; naively narrowing them introduces fabricated references that no model can verify, so all responses fail and training receives no reward signal. We present QUBRIC, a framework that co-designs queries and rubrics. Teacher-derived key points ground the rewriting of open-ended queries into scenario-based, evaluable questions. Contrastive rubric generation then turns teacher-policy gaps into query-level criteria, and learnability filtering retains only informative query-rubric pairs for GRPO training. QUBRIC achieves a +5.5 point gain on ArenaHard over the SFT baseline. Trained only on instruction-following data, it further transfers to three held-out benchmarks spanning legal, moral, and narrative reasoning (+6.3 points on average), with improvements concentrated in reasoning-related dimensions. These results provide evidence that co-designing queries and rubrics can make rubric-based RL a practical complement to RLVR beyond strictly verifiable tasks.

### [108] [POLARIS: Guiding Small Models to Write Long Stories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04095v1)
*Rishanth Rajendhran,Jenna Russell,Mohit Iyyer,John Frederick Wieting*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 使用LLM judge和参考注入训练模型，对agent奖励设计有参考价值

TL;DR: POLARIS通过引入LLM评判器奖励和人类参考注入，在少量计算资源下显著提升了小型模型的长篇创意写作能力，实现了长度泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型开放权重模型在长文本创意写作中表现差，长度遵循性和质量随长度增加下降，亟需一种低计算资源的训练方法提升其能力。

Method: 提出POLARIS方法，使用GRPO训练方案，包含两个关键组件：1）以带有结构化评分标准的前沿LLM作为在线奖励；2）人类参考注入（HRI），将教师强制的人类撰写故事作为高奖励锚点。

Result: POLARIS-9B在五个基准上与大模型竞争力相当，盲人评估优于基础模型且与27B模型持平，在3倍训练长度的提示下仍保持质量。

Conclusion: 长度泛化是创意写作模型的有效压力测试，POLARIS方法证明可通过低计算资源训练实现该能力，同时提供了区分相近模型的新视角。

中文摘要：小型开放权重模型在长篇创意写作中表现不佳：它们生成的故事要么远低于要求的长度，要么随着长度增加质量显著下降，尤其是与前沿模型相比。我们提出了POLARIS（使用LLM作为评判奖励和锚定参考注入的策略优化用于故事写作），这是一种低计算量的GRPO方案，包含两个关键要素：一个带有结构化故事质量评分标准的前沿LLM评判器作为在线奖励，以及人类参考注入（HRI），其中教师强制的人类撰写故事作为每个GRPO组内的高奖励锚点。通过将我们的训练方案应用于Qwen3.5-9B模型，使用从100部短篇小说集中提取的大约1,400对提示-故事对数据集和4块A100 GPU，我们得到了POLARIS-9B。在涵盖分布内和分布外提示及评分标准的五个基准测试中，POLARIS-9B与更大的开放权重模型具有竞争力，同时更严格地遵循长度指令。一项盲人人工评估证实，POLARIS-9B优于基础Qwen3.5-9B，并与Qwen3.5-27B相当。尽管仅在最长4,000词的故事上进行训练，POLARIS-9B在要求故事长度达训练长度3倍的提示下仍能保持质量，而大多数开放权重模型在此情况下在质量、长度遵循度或两者上显著退化。更广泛地说，我们的结果表明，长度泛化是创意写作模型一个有意义的压力测试，也是区分其他相近模型的有用视角。

Original abstract: Small open-weight models struggle at long-form creative writing: their generated stories either fall far short of the requested length, or their quality significantly degrades as length increases, especially when compared to frontier models. We present POLARIS (Policy Optimization with LLM-as-a-judge rewards and Anchored-Reference Injection for Storywriting), a lower-compute GRPO recipe with two key ingredients: a frontier LLM judge with a structured Story Quality rubric as the online reward, and human-reference injection (HRI), where a teacher-forced human-written story serves as a high-reward anchor within each GRPO group. By applying our training recipe to Qwen3.5-9B, using a dataset of approximately 1.4K prompt-story pairs derived from 100 short-story anthologies and 4 A100 GPUs, we obtain POLARIS-9B. Across five benchmarks spanning in-distribution and out-of-distribution prompts and rubrics, POLARIS-9B is competitive with much larger open-weight models while following length instructions more closely. A blinded human evaluation confirms that POLARIS-9B is preferred to the base Qwen3.5-9B and on par with Qwen3.5-27B. Despite training only on stories up to 4k words, POLARIS-9B preserves quality on prompts requesting stories up to 3 times the training length, a regime where most open-weight models degrade substantially in quality, length adherence, or both. More broadly, our results suggest that length generalization is a meaningful stress test for creative-writing models and a useful lens for distinguishing otherwise close models.

</details>


### [109] [SaliMory: Orchestrating Cognitive Memory for Conversational Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04120v1)
*Kai Zhang,Xinyuan Zhang,Hongda Jiang,Shiun-Zu Kuo,Hyokun Yun,Ejaz Ahmed,Shereen Oraby,Ziyun Li,Sanat Sharma,Ann Lee,Ahmed A Aly,Anuj Kumar,Raffay Hamid,Xin Luna Dong*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出认知记忆管理框架，对agent记忆设计有借鉴意义

TL;DR: SALIMORY通过分层阶段式过程奖励和奖励分解对比细化，训练单一语言模型管理认知结构化记忆，将记忆故障减少三分之一，端到端准确率提升超10%，良好个性化率翻倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在扩展上下文窗口或训练记忆代理时存在推理质量下降或信用分配瓶颈问题，亟需一种高效管理持久记忆的框架。

Method: 提出SALIMORY框架，训练单一语言模型管理认知结构化记忆（用户事实、偏好和工作记忆），采用分层阶段式过程奖励和奖励分解的对比细化，为选择性过滤、整合和线索驱动回忆提供端到端隔离监督。

Result: 记忆相关故障减少三分之一，端到端准确率超越当前最先进方法10%以上，良好个性化率翻倍。

Conclusion: SALIMORY有效解决了对话代理长期记忆管理中的信用分配和推理质量问题，显著提升了性能。

中文摘要：作为终身伴侣的对话代理必须跨所有交互保持持久记忆。然而，简单地通过原始检索扩展上下文窗口会降低推理质量，而通过标准强化学习训练记忆代理则会在多阶段管道中造成严重的信用分配瓶颈。为解决这一问题，我们引入了SALIMORY，一个训练单一语言模型来管理认知结构化的记忆（涵盖用户事实、偏好和工作记忆）的框架。通过引入分层阶段式过程奖励和奖励分解的对比细化，SALIMORY为不同的记忆操作（选择性过滤、整合和线索驱动回忆）提供了端到端的隔离监督。SALIMORY将记忆相关故障减少了三分之一，在端到端准确性上比当前最先进方法提高了超过10%，并且使良好个性化率翻了一番以上。

Original abstract: Conversational agents that serve as lifelong companions must maintain persistent memory across all interactions. However, simply expanding context windows with raw retrieval degrades reasoning quality, while training memory agents via standard reinforcement learning creates a severe credit assignment bottleneck in a multi-stage pipeline. To solve this, we introduce SALIMORY, a framework that trains a single language model to manage a cognitively-structured memory-spanning user facts, preferences, and working memory. By introducing a hierarchical stage-wise process reward and reward-decomposed contrastive refinement, SALIMORY provides isolated supervision for distinct memory operations (selective filtering, consolidation, and cue-driven recall) end-to-end. SALIMORY cuts memory-attributed failures by one-third, outperforms the state-of-the-art by over 10% in end-to-end accuracy, and more than doubles the Good Personalization rate.

### [110] [SkillGuard: A Permission-Centric Framework for Agent Skill Security](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03024v2)
*Shidong Pan,Xiaoyu Sun,Tianyi Zhang,Dianshu Liao,Kaiwen Yang,Zhenchang Xing*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 技能成为LLM代理中的新安全主体，但缺乏权限模型；SkillGuard提出双平面治理框架，联合调控上下文影响和动作副作用，在真实技能和对抗评估中显著降低攻击成功率并保持任务完成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前技能生态系统缺乏捕捉技能双重角色（改变推理和引导副作用）的权限模型，现有防御措施（文件检查或约束工具调用）无法有效治理技能级意图与运行时行为之间的联系。

Method: 提出SkillGuard，一个以技能为中心的权限框架，通过双平面治理模型（联合调控上下文影响和动作副作用），结合技能清单、运行时权限控制、用户交互和策略执行来实现安全管控。

Result: 在1,260个真实技能上评估，99.93%的受保护对象被覆盖；在SkillInject数据集上，上下文注入攻击成功率从35.3%降至20.7%，显式注入从36.7%降至18.0%，且良性任务完成率保持良好。

Conclusion: SkillGuard作为以技能为中心的权限框架，为提升代理技能生态系统的安全性提供了实用基础。

中文摘要：技能扩展了LLM代理，使其具有可重用的指令、脚本、数据和工具绑定。这种转变使技能成为代理系统中的新安全主体：技能可以在调用任何工具之前改变代理的推理，还可以引导代理采取具有具体副作用的行动。然而，当前的技能生态系统缺乏一个捕捉这种双重角色的权限模型。现有的防御措施要么在使用前检查技能文件，要么在执行期间约束单个工具调用，使得技能级意图、上下文影响和运行时行为之间的联系缺乏有效治理。在本文中，我们提出了SkillGuard，一个以技能为中心的权限框架，将技能视为携带权限的可执行工件。SkillGuard引入了一个双平面治理模型，通过技能清单、运行时权限控制、用户交互和策略执行，联合调节上下文影响和动作副作用。我们在1,260个真实世界的技能上评估了权限分类法的表达能力，99.93%的观察到的受保护对象被覆盖。在SkillInject数据集上的对抗性评估中，SkillGuard将上下文注入的攻击成功率从35.3%降低到20.7%，将显式注入从36.7%降低到18.0%，同时保持了良好的良性任务完成率。这些结果表明，SkillGuard作为一个以技能为中心的权限框架，可以为提高代理技能生态系统的安全性提供实用基础。

Original abstract: Skills extend LLM agents with reusable instructions, scripts, data, and tool bindings. This shift makes skills a new security principal in agent systems: a skill can alter the agent's reasoning before any tool is called, and it can also steer the agent toward actions with concrete side effects. However, current skill ecosystems lack a permission model that captures this dual role. Existing defenses either inspect skill files before use or constrain individual tool calls during execution, leaving the connection between skill-level intent, contextual influence, and runtime behavior weakly governed. In this paper, we present SkillGuard, a skill-centric permission framework that treats skills as permission-bearing executable artifacts. SkillGuard introduces a dual-plane governance model that jointly regulates context influence and action side effects through skill manifests, runtime permission control, user interaction, and policy enforcement. We evaluate the permission taxonomy expressiveness on 1,260 real-world skills, and 99.93% of observed protected objects are covered. In adversarial evaluations on SkillInject dataset, SkillGuard reduces attack success rate from 35.3% to 20.7% for contextual injections and from 36.7% to 18.0% for obvious injections, while decently maintaining benign task completion. These results suggest that SkillGuard, as a skill-centric permission framework, can provide a practical foundation for improving the security of agent skill ecosystems.

</details>


### [111] [Decoupled Smart Contract Audits: Lightweight LLM Framework via Distillation and Aggregation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03128v1)
*Bagus Rakadyanto Oktavianto Putra,Muhamad Risqi Utama Saputra,Widyawan,Guntur Dharma Putra*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 智能合约审计轻量级框架，涉及代码漏洞检测agent，蒸馏和聚合策略可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出一种轻量级LLM框架用于智能合约安全审计，通过解耦任务和特殊微调方法，以极小参数量超越大模型，达到98.25%检测准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM审计方法缺乏严重性评估和可操作修复，且计算开销大，需要更高效的解决方案。

Method: 使用0.6B-4B参数的轻量级LLM，结合rsLoRA、知识蒸馏和链式验证聚合策略，将审计解耦为检测、解释、严重性分类和修复建议四个组件。

Result: 漏洞检测准确率98.25%，解释对齐分数0.4375，优于7B-34B参数模型，消融研究验证了解耦方法的优势并发现严重性中心性偏差。

Conclusion: 轻量级LLM框架在智能合约审计中高效且准确，解耦方法和聚合策略是性能关键，为未来研究奠定基础。

中文摘要：智能合约在去中心化网络服务中面临关键的安全挑战，需要彻底审计。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在自动化漏洞检测方面展现出潜力，但现有方法缺乏带有可操作修复的严重性评估，并且需要不必要的大量计算开销。在本研究中，我们引入了一个高效的端到端智能合约安全审计框架，利用轻量级、高度优化的开源LLM（0.6B-4B参数）。我们的框架将综合审计任务解耦为四个相互关联的组件：漏洞检测、解释、严重性分类和修复建议。为了在没有大量参数的情况下保持高准确性，我们实施了秩稳定低秩适配器（rsLoRA）、知识蒸馏以及一种自定义的链式验证（CoVe）聚合策略，以系统地筛选和整合来自模型的多个草稿响应，形成高度准确的审计报告。实验结果表明，我们的轻量级流水线始终优于最先进的开源编码器密集LLM（7B至34B参数），在漏洞检测中达到98.25%的准确率，在生成性解释任务中达到0.4375的对齐分数。此外，我们广泛的消融研究实证验证了我们的解耦审计过程优于统一提示，并揭示了一种新颖的严重性中心性偏差，为未来LLM辅助审计的研究建立了关键基准。

Original abstract: Smart contracts face critical security challenges that require thorough auditing in decentralized web services. While Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown promise in automated vulnerability detection, existing approaches lack severity evaluations with actionable remediation and demand unnecessarily massive computational overhead. In this study, we introduce an efficient end-to-end smart contract security audit framework utilizing lightweight, highly optimized open-source LLMs (0.6B-4B parameters). Our framework decouples comprehensive audit tasks into four interconnected components: vulnerability detection, explanation, severity classification, and remediation recommendation. To maintain high accuracy without massive parameters, we implement Rank-Stabilized Low-Rank Adapters (rsLoRA), knowledge distillation, and a custom Chain-of-Verification (CoVe) aggregation strategy to systematically screen and consolidate multiple draft responses from the model into a highly accurate audit report. Experimental results demonstrate that our lightweight pipeline consistently outperforms state-of-the-art open-source coder dense LLMs (7B to 34B parameters), achieving 98.25% accuracy in vulnerability detection and an alignment score of 0.4375 in generative explanation tasks. Furthermore, our extensive ablation studies empirically validate the superiority of our decoupled audit processes over unified prompting and uncover a novel severity centrality bias, establishing a critical benchmark for future research in LLM-assisted auditing.

</details>


### [112] [FORGE: Multi-Agent Graduated Exploitation and Detection Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03453v1)
*Farooq Shaikh*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多agent漏洞利用和检测规则生成，软件工程安全agent

TL;DR: 本文提出FORGE，一个多智能体系统，通过渐进利用深度桥接漏洞利用、优先级排序和检测规则工程三个孤岛，在603个CVE上实现67.8%的端到端L1+利用率和1.50美元的低成本，并生成有效的检测规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 漏洞披露量远超评估能力，三个研究社区（POC生成、优先级排序、检测规则工程）孤立运作；现有自动利用系统只报告二元结果，丢弃部分进展，无法为其他社区提供有用信号。

Method: FORGE系统包含五个智能体（Intel、Generator、Planner、Exploit、Detector）在固定流水线中执行：从CVE元数据生成脆弱应用，进行多轮评估基于四级分类（L0-L3），生成Sigma和Snort检测规则；利用渐进深度作为桥接机制，并通过分层知识架构积累跨评估经验。

Result: 在603个CVE上实现67.8%端到端L1+利用，每CVE成本1.50美元；无论EPSS或CVSS评分，利用率保持~68%；L2+利用生成的检测规则比L1规则具有显著更高的接地性（p=0.035），93.4% Snort规则零误报。

Conclusion: 渐进利用深度有效桥接了三个孤岛研究社区，表明模式级可达性与元数据优先级正交，且深度利用能产生高质量检测规则，为自动化漏洞评估和防御提供了新的范式。

中文摘要：漏洞披露量现在远超组织的评估能力，而三个相邻的研究社区（概念验证生成、漏洞优先级排序和检测规则工程）却基本上孤立运作。现有的自动利用生成系统报告二元的通过/失败结果，丢弃了部分进展，并未为其他两个社区产生信号。本文提出了FORGE，一个多智能体系统，通过渐进利用深度来桥接这三个孤岛。五个专门的智能体（情报、生成器、规划器、利用和检测器）在固定的流水线中执行：(1) 从CVE元数据生成有针对性的脆弱应用程序，(2) 进行有指导的多轮利用评估，由一个以LLM为主的神谕根据四级分类（L0：无证据到L3：完全攻破）进行评判，(3) 生成基于OpenTelemetry利用痕迹的Sigma和Snort检测规则。渐进深度是桥接机制：更深的利用为检测工程产生更丰富的行为痕迹，而不同评分区间的深度数据为优先级验证提供了地面真值。分层的知识架构跨评估积累情报，将构建和利用经验传递给后续的CVE。在CVE-GENIE数据集的603个CVE上进行的评估，在8种语言和187个CWE类型中，实现了67.8%的端到端L1+利用，每个CVE成本为1.50美元。无论EPSS或CVSS评分区间如何，利用率保持在68%附近，表明模式级可达性与基于元数据的优先级排序是正交的。来自L2+利用的检测规则比L1派生的规则具有显著更高的跨度归一化接地（p=0.035），并且93.4%的生成Snort规则在合成良性语料库上产生零误报。

Original abstract: Vulnerability disclosure volumes now far exceed organizational assessment capacity, yet three adjacent research communities (proof-of-concept generation, vulnerability prioritization, and detection rule engineering) operate largely in isolation. Existing automated exploit generation systems report binary pass/fail outcomes, discarding partial progress and producing no signal for the other two communities. This paper presents FORGE, a multi-agent system that bridges these three silos through graduated exploitation depth. Five specialized agents (Intel, Generator, Planner, Exploit, and Detector) execute in a fixed pipeline that (1) generates targeted vulnerable applications from CVE metadata, (2) conducts coached, multi-turn exploitation assessed by an LLM-primary oracle on a four-level taxonomy (L0: no evidence through L3: full compromise), and (3) produces Sigma and Snort detection rules grounded in OpenTelemetry exploitation traces. Graduated depth is the bridging mechanism: deeper exploitation yields richer behavioral traces for detection engineering, while depth data across scoring bands provides ground truth for prioritization validation. A tiered knowledge architecture accumulates intelligence across assessments, transferring build and exploitation experience to subsequent CVEs. Evaluation on 603 CVEs from the CVE-GENIE dataset achieves 67.8% end-to-end L1+ exploitation at USD 1.50 per CVE across eight languages and 187 CWE types. Exploitation rates remain near 68% regardless of EPSS or CVSS band, indicating that pattern-level reachability is orthogonal to metadata-based prioritization. Detection rules from L2+ exploitation achieve significantly higher span-normalized grounding than L1-derived rules (p=0.035), and 93.4% of generated Snort rules produce zero false positives against a synthetic benign corpus.

</details>


### [113] [Learn from Your Mistakes: Tree-like Self-Play for Secure Code LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03489v2)
*Wenqi Chen,Ziyan Zhang,Bin Wang,Lin Liu,Hengheng Zhang,Zhengsu Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 树形自对弈框架改进代码安全，可迁移至代码优化Agent的自我改进机制。

TL;DR: 提出了树状自对弈（TSP）框架，将安全代码生成转化为细粒度决策过程，通过自对弈学习区分局部错误，显著提升模型安全性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐技术（SFT、RL）在序列级别粗粒度优化，无法处理安全漏洞的局部性（单个token错误可导致整个程序不安全）。

Method: 构建决策树，模型探索安全（黄金路径）和脆弱路径，通过自对弈游戏提供密集的、基于策略的学习信号，强制在关键决策节点自我修正。

Result: 在Python安全基准上，CodeLlama-7B的SPR@1达75.8%（SFT为57.0%）；未见过的CWE类别漏洞减少24.5%；安全原则可从C/C++迁移到Python、Go和JavaScript。

Conclusion: TSP内化抽象的语言无关安全逻辑，而不仅是记忆补丁，显著提升模型可靠性和分布外泛化能力。

中文摘要：虽然大型语言模型（LLM）在代码生成方面表现出色，但它们仍然容易复制其训练数据中普遍存在的微妙但关键的安全漏洞。当前的 alignment 技术，例如监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL），通常采用序列级别的粗粒度优化。这种方法往往无法解决安全缺陷的局部性质，其中单个错误的 token 选择可能危及整个程序。为了弥合这一差距，我们引入了树状自对弈（TSP），这是一个将安全代码生成重新定义为细粒度顺序决策过程的框架。与盲目最大化似然的标准方法不同，TSP 构建了一个决策树，模型在其中探索分支轨迹——既生成安全的“黄金路径”，也生成易受攻击的变体。通过将代码生成视为自对弈游戏，模型学会严格区分自身的局部错误。这提供了一个密集的、基于策略的学习信号，迫使模型在通常出现漏洞的关键决策节点上进行自我修正。我们的实验表明，TSP 从根本上提高了模型的可靠性。在 Python 安全基准测试中，TSP 将 CodeLlama-7B 的通过率（SPR@1）提升至 75.8%，显著优于 SFT（57.0%）和非结构化自对弈基线。重要的是，TSP 引发了强大的分布外泛化能力：该模型不仅将未见过的类别（CWE）中的漏洞减少了 24.5%，而且成功地将从 C/C++ 学到的安全原则迁移到多种语言，包括 Python、Go 和 JavaScript。这表明 TSP 不仅仅是记忆补丁，而是内化了抽象的、与语言无关的安全逻辑。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel in code generation, they remain prone to replicating subtle yet critical vulnerabilities endemic to their training data. Current alignment techniques, such as Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL), typically apply coarse-grained optimization at the sequence level. This approach often fails to address the localized nature of security flaws, where a single incorrect token choice can compromise an entire program. To bridge this gap, we introduce Tree-like Self-Play (TSP), a framework that reframes secure code generation as a fine-grained sequential decision process. Unlike standard methods that blindly maximize likelihood, TSP constructs a decision tree where the model explores branching trajectories--generating both secure "golden paths" and vulnerable variants. By treating code generation as a self-play game, the model learns to strictly discriminate against its own localized errors. This provides a dense, on-policy learning signal that forces self-correction precisely at the critical decision nodes where vulnerabilities typically emerge. Our experiments demonstrate that TSP fundamentally enhances model reliability. In Python security benchmarks, TSP boosts CodeLlama-7B's pass rate (SPR@1) to 75.8%, significantly outperforming SFT (57.0%) and unstructured self-play baselines. Crucially, TSP induces robust out-of-distribution generalization: the model not only reduces vulnerabilities in unseen categories (CWEs) by 24.5% but also successfully transfers security principles learned from C/C++ to diverse languages, including Python, Go, and JavaScript. This suggests that TSP does not merely memorize patches, but internalizes abstract, language-agnostic security logic.

</details>


### [114] [Need to Know: Contextual-Integrity-Grounded Query Rewriting for Privacy-Conscious LLM Delegation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04067v1)
*Xinyue Huang,Xiaochun Cao,Wenyuan Yang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 上下文完整性查询重写用于隐私保护，涉及LLM代理的隐私控制，对agent安全有启发。

TL;DR: 提出基于上下文完整性的强化学习框架，训练查询改写器在保留任务关键信息的同时抑制不必要的敏感披露，在隐私-效用权衡上取得最佳效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于类型的PII脱敏是上下文无关的，会导致过度披露未类型化敏感上下文或过度移除答案承载片段，需要更精细的隐私保护方法。

Method: 构建DelegateCI-Bench基准，包含合成数据和真实用户查询；提出CI引导的强化学习框架，将必要和非必要敏感片段转化为优化信号，训练查询改写器。

Result: 学习到的改写器在隐私-效用权衡上达到最优，在设备端基线方法上平均效用提高最多+10.1。

Conclusion: 基于上下文完整性的强化学习框架能有效训练查询改写器，在保护隐私的同时保持任务效用，优于现有方法。

中文摘要：随着大语言模型逐渐融入日常工作流程，发送到云端托管大模型的用户查询经常将任务必需内容与任务非必需的敏感披露混合在一起，然而基于类型的个人身份信息脱敏是上下文无关的，可能会引发两个问题：过度披露未类型化的敏感上下文以及过度移除承载答案的片段。我们重新将隐私保护查询改写置于上下文完整性框架下：一个片段仅当对任务必要时才应被转发。我们引入了DelegateCI-Bench，首个基于任务的上下文完整性基准，用于隐私意识的委托，包含3,167个样本，结合了涵盖11项任务和20种任务类型的高质量合成数据、基于WildChat的真实用户查询以及一个包含密集敏感信息的医疗挑战集。基于该基准，我们提出了一个CI引导的强化学习框架，将必要和非必要的敏感片段转化为可验证的优化信号，并训练一个查询改写器以保留任务关键信息同时抑制不必要的敏感披露。实验表明，我们学习到的改写器实现了最佳的隐私-效用权衡，在设备端基线方法上平均效用提高多达+10.1。

Original abstract: As LLMs become increasingly woven into everyday workflows, user queries sent to cloud hosted LLMs routinely mix task-essential content with task non-essential sensitive disclosures, yet type based PII redaction is context agnostic and may raise two issues: over disclosing untyped sensitive context and over removing answer bearing spans. We recast privacy preserving query rewriting under Contextual Integrity: a span should be forwarded only if it is necessary for the task. We introduce DelegateCI-Bench, the first task based Contextual Integrity benchmark for privacy-conscious delegation, comprising 3,167 samples that combine high quality synthetic data spanning 11 tasks and 20 task types, WildChat based real user queries, and a medical challenge set with dense sensitive information. Building on this benchmark, we propose a CI-guided reinforcement learning framework that converts essential and non-essential sensitive spans into verifiable optimization signals, and train a query rewriter to preserve task critical information while suppressing unnecessary sensitive disclosure. Experiments show that our learned rewriter achieves the best privacy-utility tradeoff, achieving up to +10.1 average utility over on-device baselines.

</details>


### [115] [AI Agents Enable Adaptive Computer Worms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03811v1)
*Jonas Guan,Tom Blanchard,Hanna Foerster,Hengrui Jia,Gabriel Huang,Nicolas Papernot*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 展示AI agent驱动的自适应计算机蠕虫，涉及agent安全与自主威胁，对agent设计有警示意义。

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种新型AI蠕虫，它利用被感染设备上的大语言模型自主生成针对每个目标的攻击策略，实现零边际成本传播，并规避了传统安全控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统蠕虫依赖固定漏洞，易被修补；而AI驱动的蠕虫能自适应攻击，造成不对称威胁，需要提前防范。

Method: 设计一种寄生性蠕虫，利用被攻陷机器上的开放权重LLM进行推理和攻击策略生成，在混合操作系统网络中利用真实漏洞传播。

Result: 成功在Linux、Windows和IoT设备网络中传播，且因使用窃取计算资源，攻击者边际成本为零，现有安全控制无效。

Conclusion: AI驱动的自主恶意软件已从理论变为现实，必须为这种无需人工、能实时推理和生成攻击逻辑的威胁做好准备。

中文摘要：计算机蠕虫是一种通过在网络上从一个机器复制到另一个机器来传播的恶意软件。传统的蠕虫，如WannaCry，利用了预定的漏洞，并且可以通过修补这些漏洞来阻止其传播。在这里，我们展示了人工智能（AI）代理能够实现一种全新的威胁：一种能够针对其遇到的每个目标生成定制攻击策略的蠕虫。该蠕虫寄生性地利用被攻陷的机器来运行开放权重的大型语言模型（LLM），以维持其推理能力，或扩展其攻击范围。在跨越Linux、Windows和物联网（IoT）设备的机器网络上部署时，该蠕虫通过利用常见的、真实世界的企业网络漏洞进行传播。由于该蠕虫由窃取的计算能力驱动，攻击者每次新感染的边际成本为零。这在攻击者和防御者之间创造了一种不稳定的经济不对称性。此外，由于该蠕虫不需要商业AI平台，集中式的安全控制（如服务拒绝或速率限制）在结构上无关紧要。我们的结果表明，自我维持的AI驱动的网络威胁已不再是理论上的。我们必须为自主生成的对抗性实体做好准备：这些恶意软件系统无需人类操作员即可传播，并且其定义不是通过固定的利用代码，而是通过实时推理目标、适应观察并合成攻击逻辑的能力。

Original abstract: A computer worm is malware that spreads on a network by replicating itself from one machine to another. Traditional worms, like WannaCry, exploited predetermined vulnerabilities, and their spread can be halted by patching those vulnerabilities. Here we show that artificial intelligence (AI) agents enable a fundamentally new threat: a worm that generates tailored attack strategies to each target it encounters. The worm parasitically uses compromised machines to run open-weight large language models (LLMs) to sustain its reasoning, or extend its reach for further attacks. Deployed on a network of machines spanning Linux, Windows, and IoT (Internet of Things) devices, the worm propagated by exploiting common, real-world corporate network vulnerabilities. Since the worm is powered by stolen compute, the attacker's marginal cost per new infection is zero. This creates a destabilizing economic asymmetry between attackers and defenders. Moreover, because the worm requires no commercial AI platform, centralized safety controls, such as service refusals or rate limiting, are structurally irrelevant. Our results demonstrate that self-sustaining AI-driven cyber-threats are no longer theoretical. We must prepare for autonomous generative adversaries: malware systems that propagate without human operators and are defined not by fixed exploit code, but by the capacity to reason about targets, adapt to observations, and synthesize attack logic in real time.

</details>


### [116] [Caught in the Act(ivation): Toward Pre-Output and Multi-Turn Detection of Credential Exfiltration by LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04141v1)
*Kargi Chauhan,Pratibha Revankar*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: agent凭证泄露检测，提供通用安全控制方法

TL;DR: 研究通过激活探针、蜜令和累积信息流核算三种方法防御LLM代理中的凭证外泄，实验表明组合防御优于单一文本过滤器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理将敏感凭证与不可信内容置于同一上下文，易受间接提示注入导致凭证外泄，亟需有效防御。

Method: 提出三种互补防御：1）激活探针检测凭证访问；2）格式特定字符模型构建蜜令并校准检测；3）将多轮外泄视为累积信息流问题，跟踪泄露预算。

Result: 激活探针在开源模型上高精度区分良性/恶意提示；累积核算在小规模多轮测试中检测到逐轮方法遗漏的攻击。

Conclusion: 凭证外泄防御应结合输出前监控、蜜罐检测和时域泄露核算，而非仅依赖文本级过滤。

中文摘要：LLM代理经常将敏感凭证与不可信的检索内容置于同一上下文窗口中，这为间接提示注入诱导凭证外泄提供了直接途径。我们通过三种互补防御措施研究这一失效模式。首先，我们探究激活探针能否在输出令牌生成前检测到凭证访问。其次，我们利用格式特定的字符模型构建蜜令，并通过分割共形预测校准检测。第三，我们将多轮外泄视为累积信息流问题，并在对话轮次间跟踪估计的泄露预算。在针对开源模型的受控实验中，激活特征能够高精度地区分良性提示和凭证窃取提示，包括在保留的编码变换下。在一个小规模合成多轮测试套件中，累积核算能够检测到逐轮检测器遗漏的攻击。这些结果是初步的：多轮基准测试为内部且规模较小，激活方法需要白盒访问，信息估计器提供的是实用信号而非正式上界。尽管如此，结果表明凭证外泄防御应结合输出前监控、校准的蜜罐检测和时域泄露核算，而不仅仅依赖文本级输出过滤器。

Original abstract: LLM agents often place sensitive credentials in the same context window as untrusted retrieved content, creating a direct path for indirect prompt injection to induce credential exfiltration. We study this failure mode through three complementary defenses. First, we ask whether activation probes can detect credential access before output tokens are emitted. Second, we construct honeytokens from format-specific character models and calibrate detection with split conformal prediction. Third, we treat multi-turn exfiltration as a cumulative information-flow problem and track an estimated leakage budget across conversation turns. In controlled experiments on open-weight models, activation features separate benign and credential-seeking prompts with high accuracy, including under held-out encoding transformations. In a small synthetic multi-turn suite, cumulative accounting detects attacks that per-turn detectors miss. These results are preliminary: the multi-turn benchmark is in-house and small, the activation method requires white-box access, and the information estimator provides a practical signal rather than a formal upper bound. Still, the results suggest that credential-exfiltration defenses should combine pre-output monitoring, calibrated canary detection, and temporal leakage accounting rather than relying only on text-level output filters.

</details>


### [117] [Notarized Agents: Receiver-Attested Confidential Receipts for AI Agent Actions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04193v1)
*Juan Figuera*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: agent行动可验证日志，直接贡献agent安全与透明性

TL;DR: 针对AI智能体可观测性中日志篡改问题，提出Sello协议，通过接收方签名、加密回执和透明度日志，使拥有者无需信任智能体即可检测篡改。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI智能体的活动日志由智能体自身生成，导致智能体可篡改日志且操作员无法独立检测，存在结构性的信任缺陷。

Method: 设计一类协议，通过反转信任边界：接收服务使用自己的密钥签署回执，加密给拥有者并发布到透明度日志；实例化为Sello，结合接收方签名、HPKE加密绑定、Merkle日志和令牌发现四个属性。

Result: 微基准测试显示密码学操作可行，安全性分析表明在对手控制智能体及其操作员时仍能保证回执的防篡改特性。

Conclusion: Sello解决了AI智能体日志的信任问题，但存在压制攻击、服务合谋和采用激励等限制，需进一步研究。

中文摘要：当前AI智能体可观测性在结构上存在漏洞：生成活动日志的实体与被记录活动的实体是同一个。一个被攻破或有缺陷的智能体可能省略、篡改或伪造自身的轨迹，而运行该智能体的操作员没有独立的方式来检测篡改。我们提出了一类协议，通过反转信任边界来解决这一问题：接收智能体调用的服务使用自己的密钥签署它所观察到的事务回执，将回执加密给智能体的拥有者，并将其发布到公共透明度日志中。拥有者在不信任智能体或其操作员的情况下重建防篡改的轨迹。我们将该类协议实例化为Sello，该协议结合了当前任何系统都缺失的四个属性：(P1) 接收方签署，(P2) 通过JWS将HPKE加密绑定到与授权令牌关联的拥有者公钥，(P3) 发布到见证者协同签署的Merkle日志，(P4) 拥有者通过令牌引用进行发现。我们描述了该协议，分析了在对手控制智能体及其操作员情况下的安全性，展示了密码学操作的微基准测试，并将Sello置于相邻的回执协议工作（Signet、AgentROA、Agent Passport System、draft-farley-acta、SCITT）中。我们讨论了已知的限制，包括压制攻击、服务合谋以及采用激励问题。

Original abstract: Current AI agent observability is structurally compromised: the entity producing the activity log is the same entity whose activity is being logged. A compromised or buggy agent can omit, alter, or fabricate its own traces, and the operator running the agent has no independent way to detect tampering. We propose a class of protocols that resolves this by inverting the trust boundary: the service that receives an agent's call signs a receipt of what it observed using its own key, encrypts the receipt to the agent's owner, and publishes it to a public transparency log. The owner reconstructs a tamper-evident trail without trusting the agent or its operator. We instantiate the class as Sello, a protocol combining four properties absent in any current system: (P1) receiver-side signing, (P2) HPKE encryption to an owner public key bound to the authorization token via JWS, (P3) publication to a witness-cosigned Merkle log, and (P4) owner-side discovery by token reference. We describe the protocol, analyze its security under an adversary that controls the agent and its operator, present microbenchmarks of the cryptographic operations, and situate Sello among adjacent receipt-protocol work (Signet, AgentROA, Agent Passport System, draft-farley-acta, SCITT). We discuss known limitations including the suppression attack, service collusion, and the adoption-incentive problem.

</details>

### [118] [FineGen: A VLM-based Multi-Agent Framework for Fine-Grained Image-Text Dataset Construction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07645v1)
*Chang Kong,Yuebing Li,Peng Mo,Haigang Zhang,Qiuming Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 基于VLM的多agent框架用于数据集构建，涉及多agent协作

TL;DR: 提出FineGen框架自动构建硬负样本数据集，在ImageNet上生成FineGen-100K，微调后使硬样本准确率提升14.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言数据集中硬负样本稀缺，限制细粒度感知能力。

Method: 基于VLM的多智能体框架，采用生成-验证-纠正流水线和闭环反馈机制，自动化构建语义有效且与视觉内容矛盾的硬负样本。

Result: 构建的FineGen-100K数据集包含147k+属性特定硬负样本，属性有效性96.7%，在FG-OVD基准上微调后硬样本准确率提升14.4%。

Conclusion: FineGen能有效解决硬负样本稀缺问题，显著提升细粒度感知任务的性能。

中文摘要：当前视觉-语言数据集中硬负样本的匮乏严重阻碍了细粒度感知。为解决这一问题，我们提出了FineGen，一个基于视觉语言模型的多智能体框架，用于自动化数据集构建。通过采用协作式生成-验证-纠正流水线并带有闭环反馈机制，FineGen确保合成的硬负样本在语义上有效且与视觉内容严格矛盾。将其应用于ImageNet，我们构建了FineGen-100K，一个层次化数据集，包含超过147,000个属性特定的硬负样本，具有严格的1:10正负样本比例。广泛评估确认了96.7%的属性有效性。关键在于，在FG-OVD基准上的下游验证表明，在FineGen-100K上微调在硬样本上实现了+14.4%的显著准确率提升，大幅超越了现有最先进方法。

Original abstract: The scarcity of hard negative samples in current vision-language datasets significantly hinders fine-grained perception. To address this, we propose FineGen, a VLM-based Multi-Agent framework for automated dataset construction. By employing a collaborative Generation-Verification-Correction pipeline with a closed-loop feedback mechanism, FineGen ensures synthesized hard negatives are semantically valid yet strictly contradictory to visual content. Applying this to ImageNet, we construct FineGen-100K, a hierarchical dataset containing over 147,000 attribute-specific hard negatives with a rigorous 1:10 positive-to-negative ratio. Extensive evaluations confirm a 96.7% attribute validity rate. Crucially, downstream validation on the FG-OVD benchmark shows that fine-tuning on FineGen-100K yields a substantial +14.4% accuracy improvement on hard samples, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art methods.

</details>


### [119] [MUSE: A Unified Agentic Harness for MLLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03005v1)
*Jianglin Lu,Hailing Wang,Xu Ma,Qihua Dong,Mingyuan Zhang,Yizhou Wang,Yun Fu*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 为MLLM设计的agentic harness，含验证与修复，直接相关agent架构

TL;DR: 本文提出MUSE，一种无需重新训练模型即可提升冻结多模态大语言模型能力的外部执行框架，通过模块化设计和验证器引导修复在多种任务上取得显著改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型在人类轻松解决的感知和空间任务上失败，而现有研究大多聚焦模型内部优化，忽视了外部执行框架的潜力。

Method: 提出MUSE，一种多模态统一结构化执行框架，通过可组合模块（任务表示、视觉处理、感知工具使用、结构化解析、确定性验证和验证器引导修复）封装任何现成的MLLM，无需重新训练模型。

Result: MUSE在视觉空间规划、视觉感知、多模态推理和细粒度视觉辨别等多个基准上均比纯模型取得持续改进，尤其在困难实例上提升显著；分析表明许多失败源于框架问题而非模型本身。

Conclusion: 代理性多模态框架是提升MLLM性能的重要且未被充分探索的方向，为超越模型中心优化提供了正交途径。

中文摘要：尽管取得了快速进展，多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在人类轻松解决的任务上仍然失败，例如从屏幕截图导航网格迷宫或选择正确的拼图块。与其重新训练模型，我们提出了一个互补的问题：仅通过改进模型周围的执行脚手架（execution scaffold），可以从冻结的MLLM中引出多少能力？我们引入了MUSE，一种多模态统一结构化执行框架，它将任何现成的MLLM与可组合模块（用于任务表示、视觉处理、感知工具使用、结构化解析、确定性验证和验证器引导修复）封装在一起，而无需任何模型重新训练。我们在跨越视觉空间规划、视觉感知、多模态推理和细粒度视觉辨别等不同基准上使用多个最先进的MLLM对MUSE进行了评估。MUSE在所有设置中都比纯模型取得了持续改进，在具有挑战性的实例上提升最大。进一步分析表明，许多MLLM的失败源于框架层面的缺陷，而非根本的模型缺陷，并且可以通过验证器引导修复来解决，而无需触及模型。这些发现突显了代理性多模态框架作为一个关键但尚未充分探索的设计维度，为超越以模型为中心的优化提供了改进MLLM的正交途径。

Original abstract: Despite rapid progress, multimodal large language models (MLLMs) still fail on tasks that humans solve effortlessly, such as navigating a grid maze from a screenshot or selecting the correct puzzle piece. Rather than retraining the model, we ask a complementary question: how much capability can be elicited from a frozen MLLM purely by improving the execution scaffold around it? We introduce MUSE, a multimodal unified structured execution harness that wraps any off-the-shelf MLLM with composable modules for task representation, visual processing, perception tool use, structured parsing, deterministic verification, and verifier-guided repair, without any model retraining. We evaluate MUSE across diverse benchmarks spanning visual spatial planning, visual perception, multimodal reasoning, and fine-grained visual discrimination, using multiple state-of-the-art MLLMs. MUSE delivers consistent gains over the bare model in all settings, with the largest jumps on challenging instances. Further analysis reveals that many MLLM failures arise from harness-level shortcomings rather than fundamental model deficits, and can be addressed through verifier-guided repair without touching the model. These findings highlight the agentic multimodal harness as a critical yet underexplored design dimension, offering an orthogonal avenue for improving MLLMs beyond model-centric optimization.

</details>


### [120] [VistaHop: Benchmarking Multi-hop Visual Reasoning for Visual DeepSearch](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03273v1)
*Hang He,Chuhuai Yue,Chengqi Dong,Chengcheng Wan,Ting Su,Haiying Sun,Jiajun Chai,Xiaohan Wang,Guojun Yin*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多跳视觉推理基准，可迁移至coding agent检索和多步推理评测。

TL;DR: 提出了VistaHop基准和VistaArena评估环境，用于评测多模态模型在视觉深度搜索中的多跳推理能力。在七个模型上的实验表明，当前最佳模型仅达到24.31%的Pass@1，揭示了视觉定位、证据检查、长链推理和多锚点融合方面的显著局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估单步视觉理解或静态图像问答，缺乏对迭代图像检查、视觉锚点定位和多跳证据整合的评估，无法全面衡量Visual DeepSearch所需的多模态推理能力。

Method: 构建了VistaHop基准，包含300张高分辨率图像、25个视觉搜索场景和350个多跳QA任务；并开发了VistaArena统一评估环境，支持文本搜索、图像搜索、图像裁剪和证据验证等工具增强推理。

Result: 在七个代表性多模态大推理模型上的实验显示，最佳模型SenseNova-MARS-32B仅达到24.31%的Pass@1，所有模型表现均远低于解决该基准的要求。

Conclusion: 当前模型在视觉定位、证据重新检查、长链推理和多锚点信息融合方面存在持久局限性，需要更强的基准和训练方法来推动Visual DeepSearch的发展。

中文摘要：Visual DeepSearch需要多模态大推理模型（MLRM）代理通过反复检查图像区域、将中间推理扎根于视觉证据、并在长推理链中连接细粒度线索来回答复杂的视觉查询。然而，现有的基准主要关注单步视觉理解或静态图像问答，对迭代图像检查、视觉锚点定位和多跳证据整合的评估有限。在这项工作中，我们引入了VistaHop，一个用于评估Visual DeepSearch中视觉中心搜索和多跳视觉推理的基准。VistaHop包含300张高分辨率图像、25个视觉搜索场景和350个多跳QA任务，要求模型跟随来自视觉锚点的证据链或融合跨多个图像定位推理路径的信息。我们进一步开发了VistaArena，一个统一的评估环境，支持工具增强的推理，包括文本搜索、图像搜索、图像裁剪和基于证据的答案验证。在七个代表性MLRM上的实验表明，当前模型远未解决VistaHop：最佳模型SenseNova-MARS-32B仅达到24.31%的Pass@1。这些结果揭示了在视觉定位、证据重新检查、长链推理和多锚点信息融合方面的持久局限性，突显了对Visual DeepSearch更强基准和训练方法的需求。

Original abstract: Visual DeepSearch requires multimodal large reasoning model (MLRM) agents to answer complex visual queries by repeatedly inspecting image regions, grounding intermediate reasoning in visual evidence, and connecting fine-grained clues across long reasoning chains. However, existing benchmarks mainly focus on single-step visual understanding or static image-question answering, offering limited evaluation of iterative image inspection, visual-anchor grounding, and multi-hop evidence integration. In this work, we introduce VistaHop, a benchmark for evaluating vision-centric search and multi-hop visual reasoning in Visual DeepSearch. VistaHop contains 300 high-resolution images, 25 visual search scenarios, and 350 multi-hop QA tasks that require models to follow evidence chains from visual anchors or fuse information across multiple image-grounded reasoning paths. We further develop VistaArena, a unified evaluation environment that supports tool-augmented reasoning with text search, image search, image cropping, and evidence-based answer validation. Experiments on seven representative MLRMs show that current models remain far from solving VistaHop: the best model, SenseNova-MARS-32B, achieves only 24.31% Pass@1. These results reveal persistent limitations in visual grounding, evidence revisiting, long-chain reasoning, and multi-anchor information fusion, highlighting the need for stronger benchmarks and training methods for Visual DeepSearch.

### [121] [SD-GRPO: Verifiable Segment Decomposition for Long-Form Vision-Language Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09871v1)
*Hyunwoong Kim,Seongeun Lee,Hannah Yun,Junhyun Park,Jonggwon Park*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 分段时间信用分配，可迁移至agent训练中长程奖励设计。

TL;DR: 提出SD-GRPO，通过对长格式VL输出的每段奖励进行z归一化得到段优势向量，在多个长格式VL任务上优于基线，并可集成到现有GRPO框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO及其变体在LLM中成功，但在多模态长格式VL任务中，粗粒度的单一标量优势无法有效分配信用，因为输出分段且图像语义丰富。

Method: 提出SD-GRPO，对rollout组内各段的可验证奖励进行z归一化，得到每段优势向量替代单一标量；在语义纠缠时结合整体奖励。

Result: 在独立段任务（DOCCI）上始终优于GRPO，段数越多增益越大；在相关段任务（MultiChartQA）上缓解了跨段误归因；在真实任务（MMSci）上混合奖励进一步改进。

Conclusion: SD-GRPO通过细粒度段级信用分配有效增强长格式VL生成，且可轻松集成到任何GRPO框架中。

中文摘要：群体相对策略优化（GRPO）及其变体最初为大型语言模型（LLM）开发，最近已应用于多模态LLM并产生了强劲的结果。然而，它们从单一标量优势进行的粗粒度整体信用分配在视觉-语言（VL）任务中拟合不足，这些任务的输出通常是以语义丰富的图像为基础的长格式回答。为解决这一限制，我们利用了单标量公式丢弃的结构化信号：长格式VL输出的自然分段。具体来说，我们提出分段分解GRPO（SD-GRPO），它对整个 rollout 组中可验证的每段奖励进行 z 归一化，从而产生一个每段优势的向量，取代单一标量。我们在三个设置上评估SD-GRPO，涵盖受控和真实世界的长格式VL生成，按跨段的语义纠缠程度递增组织。在从DOCCI构建的受控多面板密集字幕任务（段在语义上独立）上，SD-GRPO始终优于GRPO基线，在更高段数时增益更大。扩展到从MultiChartQA构建的受控多图表长格式VQA任务，我们在理论和实验上表明，rollout级别的奖励遭受跨段信用误归因，该误归因随输出长度增长。在MMSci数据集上的真实世界科学图形字幕任务中，其中子图字幕共享整个图形的上下文，混合整体和每段奖励进一步改进了两者，表明当段在语义上纠缠时，仅靠每段归一化是不够的。最后，通过将SD-GRPO集成到Dr. GRPO中，我们确认它可以以最小的实现开销应用于任何GRPO框架，以增强长格式VL生成。

Original abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and its variants, originally developed for Large Language Models (LLMs), have recently been applied to Multimodal LLMs and produced strong results. However, their coarse-grained holistic credit assignment from a single scalar advantage underfits vision-language (VL) tasks, where outputs are often long-form responses grounded in semantically rich images. To address this limitation, we exploit a structured signal that single-scalar formulations discard: the natural segmentation of long-form VL outputs. Concretely, we propose Segment-Decomposed GRPO (SD-GRPO), which z-normalizes verifiable per-segment rewards across the rollout group, yielding a vector of per-segment advantages in place of a single scalar. We evaluate SD-GRPO across three settings spanning controlled and real-world long-form VL generation, organized by increasing semantic entanglement across segments. On a controlled multi-panel dense-captioning task constructed from DOCCI, where segments are semantically independent, SD-GRPO consistently outperforms the GRPO baseline, with larger gains at higher segment counts. Extending to a controlled multi-chart long-form VQA task constructed from MultiChartQA, we show both theoretically and empirically that rollout-level rewards suffer from cross-segment credit misattribution that scales with output length. On a real-world scientific figure captioning task on the MMSci dataset, where subfigure captions share context across the figure, blending holistic and per-segment rewards further improves on both, suggesting per-segment normalization alone is insufficient when segments are semantically entangled. Finally, by integrating SD-GRPO into Dr. GRPO, we confirm that it can be applied to any GRPO framework with minimal implementation overhead to enhance long-form VL generation.

</details>


### [122] [Dive into the Scene: Breaking the Perceptual Bottleneck in Vision-Language Decision Making via Focus Plan Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04046v1)
*Boyuan Xiao,Bohong Chen,Yumeng Li,Ji Feng,Yao-Xiang Ding,Kun Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 焦点计划生成缓解幻觉，可迁移至agent注意力机制。

TL;DR: SceneDiver通过从粗到细的焦点计划生成和知识蒸馏，同时减少VLM和VLA在具身任务中的视觉幻觉，并保持计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLMs和VLAs在具身任务中受困于视觉幻觉，因为无法区分任务相关对象与干扰物，且简单的单步聚焦因缺乏深度场景理解而无效。

Method: SceneDiver：先构建全局场景图建立初始理解，再通过迭代的识别-理解-分析循环逐步分解任务，生成从粗到细的焦点计划；并设计轻量适配器将VLM的聚焦能力蒸馏到VLA。

Result: 在标准具身AI基准上，SceneDiver显著降低了VLMs和VLAs的视觉幻觉，同时在快速执行任务中保持计算效率。

Conclusion: 所提出的粗到细焦点计划生成和蒸馏方法有效解决了具身决策中的视觉幻觉问题，兼顾了长期规划与反应式控制的优势。

中文摘要：在具体的视觉-语言决策任务中，如机器人操作和导航，视觉-语言模型和视觉-语言-动作模型（VLMs & VLAs）是强大的工具，具有不同的优势：VLMs更擅长长期规划，而VLAs更擅长反应式控制。然而，它们的性能受到相同的感知瓶颈限制：由于模型无法区分任务相关对象与干扰物，导致出现视觉幻觉。原则上，准确识别并关注关键对象，同时过滤掉无关对象，是打破这一限制的关键。一个直接的解决方案是一步聚焦：直接关注重要对象。然而，这种方法被证明是无效的，因为有效的聚焦本质上需要深度场景理解。为此，我们提出了SceneDiver，一种利用VLMs长期规划能力的从粗到细的焦点计划生成方法，它首先构建整体场景图以建立初步理解，然后通过识别、理解和分析的迭代循环逐步将任务分解为更简单的子问题。为了实现反应式控制，我们还设计了一个轻量级适配器，用于将刻意聚焦能力蒸馏到VLAs中。在标准具身AI基准上的评估证实，我们的方法显著减少了VLMs和VLAs的视觉幻觉，同时在需要快速执行的任务中保持了计算效率。我们的代码和数据已在https://future-item.github.io/SceneDiver发布。

Original abstract: In embodied vision-language decision making tasks such as robotic manipulation and navigation, Vision-Language and Vision-Language-Action Models (VLMs & VLAs) are powerful tools with different benefits: VLMs are better at long-term planning, while VLAs are better at reactive control. However, their performance is limited by the same perceptual bottleneck: visual hallucinations arise due to the models' inability to distinguish task-relevant objects from distractors. In principle, accurate identification and focus on critical objects while filtering out irrelevant ones is the key to break this limitation. A straightforward solution is one-step focus: directly attending to essential objects. However, this approach proves ineffective because effective focus inherently requires deep scene understanding. To this end, we propose SceneDiver, a coarse-to-fine focus plan generation method for VLMs leveraging their long-term planning abilities, that first constructs a holistic scene graph to establish initial comprehension, then progressively decomposes the task into simpler sub-problems through an iterative cycle of recognition, understanding, and analysis. To enable reactive control, we also design a lightweight adapter for distilling the deliberate focus ability into VLAs. Evaluations on standard embodied AI benchmarks confirm that our method substantially reduces visual hallucinations for both VLMs and VLAs, while preserving computational efficiency in tasks requiring fast execution. Our code and data are released at: https://future-item.github.io/SceneDiver.

</details>


### [123] [ViMax: Agentic Video Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07649v1)
*Lingxuan Huang,Sizhe He,Hengji Zhou,Liqiang Nie,Lianghao Xia,Chao Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多agent协作视频生成框架，含层次化规划、检索增强、VLM引导，可迁移至coding agent的多agent规划与协作。

TL;DR: ViMax是一个基于多智能体协作的长篇视频生成框架，通过层次化叙事引擎和依赖感知的视觉一致性机制实现叙事连贯性和视觉一致性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ViMax框架，采用协调的多智能体协作，包括层次化叙事引擎（结合检索增强生成）、依赖感知的视觉一致性机制，以及VLM引导的代理持续监控和优化。

Result: 能够生成扩展的叙事内容，保持叙事完整性和视觉连贯性。

Conclusion: ViMax通过多智能体协作实现了长篇视频生成中的叙事连贯性和视觉一致性。

中文摘要：长篇视频生成需要系统的叙事规划和视觉一致性，而当前的短视频方法无法提供。现有方法生成孤立的序列，缺乏叙事结构，并且缺乏跨场景保持角色和环境一致性的机制。我们提出了ViMax，一个代理视频生成框架，通过协调的多智能体协作来解决视频创作问题，其中专门的组件协商叙事决策、视觉连续性和制作质量。我们的框架采用层次化叙事引擎，具有检索增强生成以实现全局故事连贯性，以及一个依赖感知的视觉一致性机制，跨时间边界跟踪角色和环境状态，而VLM引导的代理持续监控和改进叙事连贯性和视觉保真度。该框架实现协调的智能体协作以生成扩展的叙事内容。这保持了多场景时间线中叙事完整性和视觉连贯性。

Original abstract: Long-form video generation requires systematic narrative planning and visual consistency that current short-clip methods cannot provide. Existing methods generate isolated sequences without narrative structure and lack mechanisms for maintaining character and environmental consistency across scenes. We present ViMax, an agentic video generation framework that addresses video creation through coordinated multi-agent collaboration where specialized components negotiate narrative decisions, visual continuity, and production quality. Our framework employs a hierarchical narrative engine with retrieval-augmented generation for global story coherence and a dependency-aware visual consistency mechanism that tracks character and environmental states across temporal boundaries, while VLM-guided agents continuously monitor and refine both narrative coherence and visual fidelity. The framework enables coordinated agent collaboration to generate extended narrative content. This maintains both storytelling integrity and visual coherence across multi-scene timelines.

### [124] [TurtleAI: Benchmarking Multimodal Models for Visual Programming in Turtle Graphics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03626v1)
*Chao Wen,Jacqueline Staub,Adish Singla*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 教育视觉编程benchmark，涉及代码生成与VLM评估，与coding agent的代码生成相关。

TL;DR: 提出TurtleAI基准和合成数据生成方法，发现VLM在教育视觉编程上表现差，微调提升20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索VLM在教育导向视觉编程上的表现及限制因素。

Method: 基于Turtle Graphics构建823个任务的基准，评估多种VLM，提出少量种子样本生成合成数据并微调。

Result: 多数VLM成功率低于30%，微调Qwen2-VL-72B在真实任务上提升约20%。

Conclusion: GPT-4o空间推理和精确视觉复制较弱，微调主要改善视觉推理与代码实现的对齐。

中文摘要：视觉语言模型（VLM）已被探索用于视觉编程，即生成代码解决视觉任务。然而，大多数先前工作聚焦于提高生产力的视觉编程；当前VLM在教育导向视觉编程上的表现及限制因素仍不清楚。为填补此空白，我们引入TurtleAI，一个包含823个任务的基准测试，基于Turtle Graphics领域的真实视觉编程任务。解决这些任务要求模型感知几何模式、推理空间关系并合成能忠实再现几何模式的Python代码。我们评估了20多个VLM，包括GPT-5、GPT-4o和Qwen2-VL-72B，发现它们表现挣扎，大多数成功率低于30%。为解决这些限制，我们提出一种仅需少量种子样本的数据生成技术。在所得合成数据上微调Qwen2-VL-72B，在真实任务上提升了约20%。我们的失败分析显示GPT-4o在空间推理和精确视觉复制上挣扎，而微调主要改善了视觉推理与代码实现间的对齐。

Original abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have been explored for visual programming, where they generate code to solve visual tasks. However, most prior work focuses on visual programming for productivity; it remains unclear how well current VLMs perform on education-oriented visual programming and what factors limit their performance. To bridge this gap, we introduce TurtleAI, a benchmark containing 823 tasks curated based on real-world visual programming tasks in the Turtle Graphics domain. Solving these tasks requires models to perceive geometric patterns, reason about spatial relationships, and synthesize Python code that faithfully reproduces geometric patterns. We evaluate 20+ VLMs, including GPT-5, GPT-4o, and Qwen2-VL-72B, and find that they struggle significantly, with most achieving success rates below 30%. To address these limitations, we propose a data generation technique that requires only a small set of seed samples. Fine-tuning Qwen2-VL-72B on the resulting synthetic data yields an improvement of about 20% on real-world tasks. Our failure analysis reveals that GPT-4o struggles with spatial reasoning and precise visual replication, whereas fine-tuning primarily improves the alignment between visual reasoning and code implementation.

</details>
